sūta uvāca
ajamīḍhasya nīlinyāṃ nīlaḥ samabhavannṛpaḥ 
nīlasya tapasogreṇa suśāntirudapadyata  MatsP 
purujānuḥ suśāntestu pṛthustu purujānutaḥ 
bhadrāśvaḥ pṛthudāyādo bhadrāśvatanayāñchṛṇu  MatsP 
mudgalaśca jayaścaiva rājā bṛhadiṣustathā 
javīnaraśca vikrāntaḥ kapilaścaiva pañcamaḥ  MatsP 
pañcānāṃ caiva pañcālān etāñjanapadānviduḥ 
pañcālarakṣiṇo hy ete deśānāmiti naḥ śrutam  MatsP 
mudgalasyāpi maudgalyāḥ kṣatropetā dvijātayaḥ 
ete hy aṅgirasaḥ pakṣaṃ saṃśritāḥ kāṇvamudgalāḥ  MatsP 
mudgalasya suto jajñe brahmiṣṭhaḥ sumahāyaśāḥ 
indrasenaḥ sutastasya vindhyāśvastasya cātmajaḥ  MatsP 
vindhyāśvānmithunaṃ jajñe menakāyāmiti śrutiḥ 
divodāsaśca rājarṣir ahalyā ca yaśasvinī  MatsP 
śaradvatastu dāyādam ahalyā samprasūyata 
śatānandamṛṣiśreṣṭhaṃ tasyāpi sumahātapāḥ  MatsP 
sutaḥ satyadhṛtirnāma dhanurvedasya pāragaḥ 
āsītsatyadhṛteḥ śukram amoghaṃ dhārmikasya tu  MatsP 
skannaṃ retaḥ satyadhṛter dṛṣṭvā cāpsarasaṃ jale 
mithunaṃ tatra saṃbhṛtaṃ tasminsarasi saṃbhṛtam  MatsP 
tataḥ sarasi tasmiṃstu kramamāṇaṃ mahīpatiḥ 
dṛṣṭvā jagrāha kṛpayā śaṃtanurmṛgayāṃ gataḥ  MatsP 
ete śaradvataḥ putrā ākhyātā gautamā varāḥ 
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi divodāsasya vai prajāḥ  MatsP 
divodāsasya dāyādo dharmiṣṭho mitrayurnṛpaḥ 
maitrāyaṇāvaraḥ so 'tha maitreyastu tataḥ smṛtaḥ  MatsP 
ete vaṃśyā yateḥ pakṣāḥ kṣatropetāstu bhārgavāḥ 
rājā caidyavaro nāma maitreyasya sutaḥ smṛtaḥ  MatsP 
atha caidyavarādvidvān sudāsastasya cātmajaḥ 
ajamīḍhaḥ punarjātaḥ kṣīṇe vaṃśe tu somakaḥ  MatsP 
somakasya suto jantur hate tasmiñchataṃ babhau 
putrāṇāmajamīḍhasya somakasya mahātmanaḥ  MatsP 
mahiṣī tv ajamīḍhasya dhūminī putravardhinī 
putrābhāve tapastepe śataṃ varṣāṇi duścaram  MatsP 
hutvāgniṃ vidhivatsamyak pavitrīkṛtabhojanā 
agnihotrakrameṇaiva sā suṣvāpa mahāvratā  MatsP 
tasyāṃ vai dhūmavarṇāyām ajamīḍhaḥ samīyivān 
ṛkṣaṃ sā janayāmāsa dhūmavarṇaṃ śatāgrajam  MatsP 
ṛkṣātsaṃvaraṇo jajñe kuruḥ saṃvaraṇāt tataḥ 
yaḥ prayāgamatikramya kurukṣetramakalpayat  MatsP 
kṛṣyatastu mahārājo varṣāṇi subahūnyatha 
kṛṣyamāṇastataḥ śakro bhayāttasmai varaṃ dadau  MatsP 
puṇyaṃ ca ramaṇīyaṃ ca kurukṣetraṃ tu tatsmṛtam 
tasyānvavāyaḥ sumahān yasya nāmnā tu kauravāḥ  MatsP 
kurostu dayitāḥ putrāḥ sudhanvā jahnureva ca 
parīkṣicca mahātejāḥ prajanaścārimardanaḥ  MatsP 
sudhanvanastu dāyādaḥ putro matimatāṃ varaḥ 
cyavanastasya putrastu rājā dharmārthatattvavit  MatsP 
cyavanasya kṛmiḥ putra ṛkṣājjajñe mahātapāḥ 
kṛmeḥ putro mahāvīryaḥ khyātastvindrasamo vibhuḥ  MatsP 
caidyoparicaro vīro vasurnāmāntarikṣagaḥ 
caidyoparicarājjajñe girikā sapta vai sutān  MatsP 
mahāratho magadharāḍ viśruto yo bṛhadrathaḥ 
pratyaśravāḥ kuśaścaiva caturtho harivāhanaḥ  MatsP 
pañcamaśca yajuścaiva matsyaḥ kālī ca saptamī 
bṛhadrathasya dāyādaḥ kuśāgro nāma viśrutaḥ  MatsP 
kuśāgrasyātmajaścaiva vṛṣabho nāma vīryavān 
vṛṣabhasya tu dāyādaḥ puṇyavānnāma pārthivaḥ  MatsP 
puṇyaḥ puṇyavataścaiva rājā satyadhṛtistataḥ 
dāyādastasya dhanuṣas tasmātsarvaśca jajñivān  MatsP 
sarvasya sambhavaḥ putras tasmādrājā bṛhadrathaḥ 
dve tasya śakale jāte jarayā saṃdhitaś ca saḥ  MatsP 
jarayā saṃdhito yasmāj jarāsaṃdhastataḥ smṛtaḥ 
jetā sarvasya kṣatrasya jarāsaṃdho mahābalaḥ  MatsP 
jarāsaṃdhasya putrastu sahadevaḥ pratāpavān 
sahadevātmajaḥ śrīmān somavit sa mahātapāḥ  MatsP 
śrutaśravāstu somāder māgadhāḥ parikīrtitāḥ 
jahnustvajanayatputraṃ surathaṃ nāma bhūmipam  MatsP 
surathasya tu dāyādo vīro rājā vidūrathaḥ 
vidūrathasutaścāpi sārvabhauma iti smṛtaḥ  MatsP 
sārvabhaumājjayatseno rucirastasya cātmajaḥ 
rucirāttu tato bhaumas tvaritāyustato 'bhavat  MatsP 
akrodhanas tv āyusutas tasmāddevātithiḥ smṛtaḥ 
devātithestu dāyādo dakṣa eva babhūva ha  MatsP 
bhīmasenastato dakṣād dilīpas tasya cātmajaḥ 
dilīpasya pratīpastu tasya putrās trayaḥ smṛtāḥ  MatsP 
devāpiḥ śaṃtanuścaiva vāhlīkaścaiva te trayaḥ 
vāhlīkasya tu dāyādāḥ sapta vāhlīśvarā nṛpāḥ 
devāpistu hy apadhyātaḥ prajābhirabhavanmuniḥ  MatsP 
munaya ūcuḥ
prajābhistu kimarthaṃ vai hy apadhyāto janeśvaraḥ 
ko doṣo rājaputrasya prajābhiḥ samudāhṛtaḥ  MatsP 
sūta uvāca
kilāsīdrājaputrastu kuṣṭhī taṃ nābhyapūjayan 
kāryaṃ caiva tu devānāṃ kṣatraṃ prati dvijottamāḥ 
bhaviṣyaṃ kīrtayiṣyāmi śaṃtanostu nibodhata  MatsP 
śaṃtanustvabhavadrājā vidvānsa vai mahābhiṣak 
idaṃ codāharantyatra ślokaṃ prati mahābhiṣak  MatsP 
yaṃ yaṃ karābhyāṃ spṛśati jīrṇaṃ rogiṇameva ca 
punaryuvā ca bhavati tasmāttaṃ śaṃtanuṃ viduḥ  MatsP 
tattasya śaṃtanutvaṃ hi prajābhiriha kīrtyate 
tato 'vṛṇuta bhāryārthaṃ śaṃtanurjāhnavīṃ nṛpa  MatsP 
tasyāṃ devavrataṃ nāma kumāraṃ janayadvibhuḥ 
kālī vicitravīryaṃ tu dāśeyī janayatsutam  MatsP 
śaṃtanordayitaṃ putraṃ śāntātmānamakalmaṣam 
kṛṣṇadvaipāyano nāma kṣetre vaicitraviryake  MatsP 
dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ ca pāṇḍuṃ ca viduraṃ cāpyajījanat 
dhṛtarāṣṭrastu gāndhāryāṃ putrānajanayacchatam  MatsP 
teṣāṃ duryodhanaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sarvakṣatrasya vai prabhuḥ 
mādrī kuntī tathā caiva pāṇḍorbhārye babhūvatuḥ  MatsP 
devadattāḥ sutāḥ pañca pāṇḍorarthe 'bhijajñire 
dharmādyudhiṣṭhiro jajñe mārutācca vṛkodaraḥ  MatsP 
indrāddhanaṃjayaścaiva indratulyaparākramaḥ 
nakulaṃ sahadevaṃ ca mādryaśvibhyāmajījanat  MatsP 
pañcaite pāṇḍavebhyastu draupadyāṃ jajñire sutāḥ 
draupadyajanayacchreṣṭhaṃ prativindhyaṃ yudhiṣṭhirāt  MatsP 
śrutasenaṃ bhīmasenāc chrutakīrtiṃ dhanaṃjayāt 
caturthaṃ śrutakarmāṇaṃ sahadevād ajāyata  MatsP 
nakulācca śatānīkaṃ draupadeyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ 
tebhyo 'pare pāṇḍaveyāḥ ṣaḍevānye mahārathāḥ  MatsP 
haiḍambo bhīmasenāttu putro jajñe ghaṭotkacaḥ 
kāśī baladharādbhīmāj jajñe vai sarvagaṃ sutam  MatsP 
suhotraṃ tanayaṃ mādrī sahadevādasūyata 
kareṇumatyāṃ caidyāyāṃ niramitrastu nākuliḥ  MatsP 
subhadrāyāṃ rathī pārthād abhimanyurajāyata 
yaudheyaṃ devakī caiva putraṃ jajñe yudhiṣṭhirāt  MatsP 
abhimanyoḥ parīkṣittu putraḥ parapurajayaḥ 
janamejayaḥ parīkṣitaḥ putraḥ paramadhārmikaḥ  MatsP 
brahmāṇaṃ kalpayāmāsa sa vai vājasaneyakam 
sa vaiśampāyanenaiva śaptaḥ kila maharṣiṇā  MatsP 
na sthāsyatīha durbuddhe tavaitadvacanaṃ bhuvi 
yāvatsthāsyasi tvaṃ loke tāvadeva prapatsyati  MatsP 
kṣatrasya vijayaṃ jñātvā tataḥprabhṛti sarvaśaḥ 
abhigamya sthitāścaiva nṛpaṃ ca janamejayam  MatsP 
tataḥprabhṛti śāpena kṣatriyasya tu yājinaḥ 
utsannā yājino yajñe tataḥprabhṛti sarvaśaḥ  MatsP 
kṣatrasya yājinaḥ kecic chāpāttasya mahātmanaḥ 
paurṇamāsena haviṣā iṣṭvā tasminprajāpatim 
sa vaiśampāyanenaiva praviśanvāritastataḥ  MatsP 
parīkṣitaḥ suto 'sau vai pauravo janamejayaḥ 
dvir aśvamedhamāhṛtya mahāvājasaneyakaḥ  MatsP 
pravartayitvā taṃ sarvam ṛṣiṃ vājasaneyakam 
vivāde brāhmaṇaiḥ sārdham abhiśapto vanaṃ yayau  MatsP 
janamejayācchatānīkas tasmājjajñe sa vīryavān 
janamejayaḥ śatānīkaṃ putraṃ rājye 'bhiṣiktavān  MatsP 
athāśvamedhena tataḥ śatānīkasya vīryavān 
jajñe 'dhisomakṛṣṇākhyaḥ sāmprataṃ yo mahāyaśāḥ  MatsP 
tasmiñchāsati rāṣṭraṃ tu yuṣmābhiridamāhṛtam 
durāpaṃ dīrghasattraṃ vai trīṇi varṣāṇi puṣkare 
varṣadvayaṃ kurukṣetre dṛṣadvatyāṃ dvijottamāḥ  MatsP 
munaya ūcuḥ
bhaviṣyaṃ śrotumicchāmaḥ prajānāṃ lomaharṣaṇe 
purā kila yadetadvai vyatītaṃ kīrtitaṃ tvayā  MatsP 
yeṣu vai sthāsyate kṣatram utpatsyante nṛpāśca ye 
teṣām āyuṣpramāṇaṃ ca nāmataścaiva tānnṛpān  MatsP 
kṛtayugapramāṇaṃ ca tretādvāparayostathā 
kaliyugapramāṇaṃ ca yugadoṣaṃ yugakṣayam  MatsP 
sukhaduḥkhapramāṇaṃ ca prajādoṣaṃ yugasya tu 
etatsarvaṃ prasaṃkhyāya pṛcchatāṃ brūhi naḥ prabho  MatsP 
sūta uvāca
yathā me kīrtitaṃ pūrvaṃ vyāsenākliṣṭakarmaṇā 
bhāvyaṃ kaliyugaṃ caiva tathā manvantarāṇi ca  MatsP 
anāgatāni sarvāṇi bruvato me nibodhata 
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi bhaviṣyā ye nṛpāstathā  MatsP 
aiḍekṣvākvanvaye caiva paurave cānvaye tathā 
yeṣu saṃsthāsyate tacca aiḍekṣvākukulaṃ śubham 
tānsarvānkīrtayiṣyāmi bhaviṣye kathitānnṛpān  MatsP 
tebhyo 'pare 'pi ye tv anye hy utpatsyante nṛpāḥ punaḥ 
kṣatrāḥ pāraśavāḥ śūdrās tathānye ye bahiścarāḥ  MatsP 
andhāḥ śakāḥ pulindāśca cūlikā yavanāstathā 
kaivartābhīraśabarā ye cānye mlecchasambhavāḥ 
paryāyataḥ pravakṣyāmi nāmataścaiva tānnṛpān  MatsP 
adhisomakṛṣṇaś caiteṣāṃ prathamaṃ vartate nṛpaḥ 
tasyānvavāye vakṣyāmi bhaviṣye kathitānnṛpān  MatsP 
adhisomakṛṣṇaputrastu vivakṣurbhavitā nṛpaḥ 
gaṅgayā tu hṛte tasmin nagare nāgasāhvaye  MatsP 
tyaktvā vivakṣurnagaraṃ kauśāmbyāṃ tu nivatsyati 
bhaviṣyāṣṭau sutāstasya mahābalaparākramāḥ  MatsP 
bhūrirjyeṣṭhaḥ sutastasya tasya citrarathaḥ smṛtaḥ 
śucidravaścitrarathād vṛṣṇimāṃśca śucidravāt  MatsP 
vṛṣṇimataḥ suṣeṇaśca bhaviṣyati śucirnṛpaḥ 
tasmātsuṣeṇādbhavitā sunītho nāma pārthivaḥ  MatsP 
nṛpātsunīthādbhavitā nṛcakṣuḥ sumahāyaśāḥ 
nṛcakṣuṣastu dāyādo bhavitā vai sukhīvalaḥ  MatsP 
sukhīvalasutaścāpi bhāvī rājā pariṣṇavaḥ 
pariṣṇavasutaścāpi bhavitā sutapā nṛpaḥ  MatsP 
medhāvī tasya dāyādo bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ 
medhāvinaḥ sutaścāpi bhaviṣyati puraṃjayaḥ  MatsP 
urvo bhāvyaḥ sutastasya tigmātmā tasya cātmajaḥ 
tigmādbṛhadratho bhāvyo vasudāmā bṛhadrathāt  MatsP 
vasudāmnaḥ śatānīko bhaviṣyodayanastataḥ 
bhaviṣyate codayanād vīge rājā vahīnaraḥ  MatsP 
vahīnarātmajaścaiva daṇḍapāṇirbhaviṣyati 
daṇḍapāṇerniramitro niramitrāttu kṣemakaḥ  MatsP 
atrānuvaṃśaśloko 'yaṃ gīto vipraiḥ purātanaiḥ 
brahmakṣatrasya yo yonir vaṃśo devarṣisatkṛtaḥ 
kṣemakaṃ prāpya rājānaṃ saṃsthāsyati kalau yuge  MatsP 
ityeṣa pauravo vaṃśo yathāvadiha kīrtitaḥ 
dhīmataḥ pāṇḍuputrasya cārjunasya mahātmanaḥ  MatsP

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
ye pūjyāḥ syur dvijātīnām agnayaḥ sūta sarvadā 
tānidānīṃ samācakṣva tadvaṃśaṃ cānupūrvaśaḥ  MatsP 
sūta uvāca
yo 'sāv agnirabhīmānī smṛtaḥ svāyambhuve 'ntare 
brahmaṇo mānasaḥ putras tasmātsvāhā vyajījanat  MatsP 
pāvakaṃ pavamānaṃ ca śuciragniśca yaḥ smṛtaḥ 
nirmathyaḥ pavamāno 'gnir vaidyutaḥ pāvakātmajaḥ  MatsP 
śuciragniḥ smṛtaḥ sauraḥ sthāvarāścaiva te smṛtāḥ 
pavamānātmajo hy agnir havyavāhaḥ sa ucyate  MatsP 
pāvakaḥ saharakṣastu havyavāhamukhaḥ śuciḥ 
devānāṃ havyavāho 'gniḥ prathamo brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ  MatsP 
saharakṣaḥ surāṇāṃ tu trayāṇāṃ te trayo 'gnayaḥ 
eteṣāṃ putrapautrāśca catvāriṃśattathaiva ca  MatsP 
pravakṣye nāmatastānvai pravibhāgena tānpṛthak 
pāvano laukiko hy agniḥ prathamo brahmaṇaśca yaḥ  MatsP 
brahmaudanāgnis tatputro bharato nāma viśrutaḥ 
vaiśvānaro havyavāho vahanhavyaṃ mamāra saḥ  MatsP 
sa mṛto 'tharvaṇaḥ putro mathitaḥ puṣkarodadhiḥ 
yo 'tharvā laukiko hy agnir dakṣiṇāgniḥ sa ucyate  MatsP 
bhṛgoḥ prajāyatātharvā hy aṅgirātharvaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ 
tasya hy alaukiko hy agnir dakṣiṇāgniḥ sa vai smṛtaḥ  MatsP 
atha yaḥ pavamānastu nirmathyo 'gniḥ sa ucyate 
sa ca vai gārhapatyo 'gniḥ prathamo brahmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ  MatsP 
tataḥ sabhyāvasathyau ca saṃśatyās tau sutāvubhau 
tataḥ ṣoḍaśa nadyastu cakame havyavāhanaḥ 
yaḥ khalvāhavanīyo 'gnir abhimānī dvijaiḥ smṛtaḥ  MatsP 
kāverīṃ kṛṣṇaveṇīṃ ca narmadāṃ yamunāṃ tathā 
godāvarīṃ vitastāṃ ca candrabhāgāmirāvatīm  MatsP 
vipāśāṃ kauśikīṃ caiva śatadruṃ sarayūṃ tathā 
sītāṃ manasvinīṃ caiva hrādinīṃ pāvanāṃ tathā  MatsP 
tāsu ṣoḍaśadhātmānaṃ pravibhajya pṛthakpṛthak 
tadā tu viharaṃstāsu dhiṣṇyecchaḥ sa babhūva ha  MatsP 
svābhidhānasthitā dhiṣṇyās tāsūtpannāśca dhiṣṇavaḥ 
dhiṣṇyeṣu jajñire yasmāt tataste dhiṣṇavaḥ smṛtāḥ  MatsP 
ityete vai nadīputrā dhiṣṇyeṣu pratipedire 
teṣāṃ viharaṇīyā ye upastheyāśca tāñśṛṇu 
vibhuḥ pravāhaṇo 'gnīdhras tatrasthā dhiṣṇavo 'pare  MatsP 
viharati yathāsthānaṃ puṇyāhe samupakrame 
anirdeśyānivāryāṇām agnīnāṃ śṛṇuta kramam  MatsP 
vāsavo 'gniḥ kṛśānuryo dvitīyottaravedikaḥ 
samrāḍagnisuto hyaṣṭāv upatiṣṭhanti tāndvijāḥ  MatsP 
parjanyaḥ pavamānastu dvitīyaḥ so 'nudṛśyate 
pāvakoṣṇaḥ samūhyastu vottare so 'gnirucyate  MatsP 
havyasūdo hy asaṃmṛjyaḥ śāmitraḥ sa vibhāvyate 
śatadhāmā sudhājyotī raudraiśvaryaḥ sa ucyate  MatsP 
brahmajyotir vasudhāmā brahmasthānīya ucyate 
ajaikapādupastheyaḥ sa vai śālāmukho yataḥ  MatsP 
anirdeśyo hyahirbudhnyo bahirante tu dakṣiṇau 
putrā hyete tu sarvasya upastheyā dvijaiḥ smṛtāḥ  MatsP 
tato viharaṇīyāṃstu vakṣyāmyaṣṭau tu tānsutān 
hautriyasya suto hyagnir barhiṣo havyavāhanaḥ  MatsP 
praśaṃsyo 'gniḥ pracetāstu dvitīyaḥ saṃsahāyakaḥ 
suto hyagner viśvavedā brāhmaṇācchaṃsirucyate  MatsP 
apāṃ yoniḥ smṛtaḥ svāmbhaḥ seturnāma vibhāvyate 
dhiṣṇya āharaṇā hyete somenejyanta vai dvijaiḥ  MatsP 
tato yaḥ pāvako nāmnā yaḥ sadbhiryoga ucyate 
agniḥ so 'vabhṛtho jñeyo varuṇena sahejyate  MatsP 
hṛdayasya suto hyagner jaṭhare 'sau nṛṇāṃ pacan 
manyumāñjaṭharaścāgnir viddhāgniḥ satataṃ smṛtaḥ  MatsP 
parasparotthito hyagnir bhūtānīha vibhurdahan 
agnermanyumataḥ putro ghoraḥ saṃvartakaḥ smṛtaḥ  MatsP 
pibannapaḥ sa vasati samudre vaḍavāmukhe 
samudravāsinaḥ putraḥ saharakṣo vibhāvyate  MatsP 
saharakṣastu vai kāmān gṛhe sa vasate nṛṇām 
kravyādagniḥ sutastasya puruṣānyo 'tti vai mṛtān  MatsP 
ityete pāvakasyāgner dvijaiḥ putrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ 
tataḥ sutāstu sauvīryād gandharvairasurair hṛtāḥ  MatsP 
mathito yastvaraṇyāṃ tu so 'gnirāpa samindhanam 
āyur nāmnā tu bhagavān paśau yastu praṇīyate  MatsP 
āyuṣo mahimānputro dahanastu tataḥ sutaḥ 
pākayajñeṣv abhīmānī hutaṃ havyaṃ bhunakti yaḥ  MatsP 
sarvasmāddevalokācca havyaṃ kavyaṃ bhunakti yaḥ 
putro 'sya sahito hyagnir adbhutaḥ sa mahāyaśāḥ  MatsP 
prāyaścitteṣvabhīmānī hṛtaṃ havyaṃ bhunakti yaḥ 
adbhutasya suto vīro devāṃśastu mahānsmṛtaḥ  MatsP 
vividhāgnistatastasya tasya putro mahākaviḥ 
vividhāgnisutādarkād agnayo 'ṣṭau sutāḥ smṛtāḥ  MatsP 
kāmyāsviṣṭiṣvabhīmānī rakṣohāyatikṛcca yaḥ 
surabhirvasumānnādo haryaśvaścaiva rukmavān  MatsP 
pravargyaḥ kṣemavāṃścaiva ityaṣṭau ca prakīrtitāḥ 
śucyagnestu prajā hyeṣā agnayaśca caturdaśa  MatsP 
ityete hyagnayaḥ proktāḥ praṇītā ye hi cādhvare 
samatīte tu sarge ye yāmaiḥ saha surottamaiḥ  MatsP 
svāyambhuve 'ntare pūrvam agnayaste 'bhimāninaḥ 
ete viharaṇīyeṣu cetanācetaneṣviha  MatsP 
sthānābhimānino 'gnīdhrāḥ prāgāsanhavyavāhanāḥ 
kāmyanaimittikādyāste ye te karmasvavasthitāḥ  MatsP 
pūrve manvantare 'tīte śukrairyāmaiśca taiḥ saha 
ete devagaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ prathamasyāntare manoḥ  MatsP 
ityetā yonayo hyaktāḥ sthānākhyā jātavedasām 
svārociṣādiṣu jñeyāḥ savarṇānteṣu saptasu  MatsP 
tairevaṃ tu prasaṃkhyātaṃ sāmpratānāgateṣviha 
manvantareṣu sarveṣu lakṣaṇaṃ jātavedasām  MatsP 
manvantareṣu sarveṣu nānārūpaprayojanaiḥ 
vartante vartamānaiśca yāmairdevaiḥ sahāgnayaḥ  MatsP 
anāgataiḥ suraiḥ sārdhaṃ vatsyanto 'nāgatāstvatha 
ityeṣa pracayo 'gnīnāṃ mayā prokto yathākramam 
vistareṇānupūrvyā ca kimanyacchrotumicchatha  MatsP

idānīṃ prāha yadviṣṇuḥ pṛṣṭaḥ paramamuttamam 
tadidānīṃ samācakṣva dharmādharmasya vistaram  MatsP 
sūta uvāca
evamekārṇave tasmin matsyarūpī janārdanaḥ 
vistāramādisargasya pratisargasya cākhilam  MatsP 
kathayāmāsa viśvātmā manave sūryasūnave 
karmayogaṃ ca sāṃkhyaṃ ca yathāvadvistarānvitam  MatsP 
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
śrotumicchāmahe sūta karmayogasya lakṣaṇam 
yasmādaviditaṃ loke na kiṃcittava suvrata  MatsP 
sūta uvāca
karmayogaṃ ca vakṣyāmi yathā viṣṇuvibhāṣitam 
jñānayogasahasrāddhi karmayogaḥ praśasyate  MatsP 
karmayogodbhavaṃ jñānaṃ tasmāttatparamaṃ padam 
karmajñānodbhavaṃ brahma na ca jñānamakarmaṇaḥ  MatsP 
tasmātkarmaṇi yuktātmā tattvamāpnoti śāśvatam 
vedo 'khilo dharmamūlam ācāraścaiva tadvidām  MatsP 
aṣṭāvātmaguṇās tasmin pradhānatvena saṃsthitāḥ 
dayā sarveṣu bhūteṣu kṣāntī rakṣāturasya tu  MatsP 
anasūyā tathā loke śaucamantarbahirdvijāḥ 
anāyāseṣu kāryeṣu māṅgalyācārasevanam  MatsP 
na ca dravyeṣu kārpaṇyam ārteṣūpārjiteṣu ca 
tathāspṛhā paradravye parastrīṣu ca sarvadā  MatsP 
aṣṭāvātmaguṇāḥ proktāḥ purāṇasya tu kovidaiḥ 
ayameva kriyāyogo jñānayogasya sādhakaḥ  MatsP 
karmayogaṃ vinā jñānaṃ kasyacin neha dṛśyate 
śrutismṛtyuditaṃ dharmam upatiṣṭhetprayatnataḥ  MatsP 
devatānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca sarvadā 
kuryādaharaharyajñair bhūtarṣigaṇatarpaṇam  MatsP 
svādhyāyairarcayeccarṣīn homairvidvānyathāvidhi 
pitṝñchrāddhair annadānair bhūtāni balikarmabhiḥ  MatsP 
pañcaite vihitā yajñāḥ pañcasūnāpanuttaye 
kaṇḍanī peṣaṇī cullī jalakumbhī pramārjanī  MatsP 
pañca sūnā gṛhasthasya tena svargaṃ na gacchati 
tatpāpanāśanāyāmī pañca yajñāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  MatsP 
dvāviṃśatistathāṣṭau ca ye saṃskārāḥ prakīrtitāḥ 
tadyukto 'pi na mokṣāya yastvātmaguṇavarjitaḥ  MatsP 
tasmādātmaguṇopetaḥ śrutikarma samācaret 
gobrāhmaṇānāṃ vittena sarvadā bhadramācaret  MatsP 
gobhūhiraṇyavāsobhir gandhamālyodakena ca 
pūjayedbrahmaviṣṇvarkarudravasvātmakaṃ śivam  MatsP 
vratopavāsair vidhivacchraddhayā ca vimatsaraḥ 
yo 'sāv atīndriyaḥ śāntaḥ sūkṣmo 'vyaktaḥ sanātanaḥ 
vāsudevo jaganmūrtis tasya sambhūtayo hy amī  MatsP 
brahmā viṣṇuśca bhagavān mārtaṇḍo vṛṣavāhanaḥ 
aṣṭau ca vasavastadvad ekādaśa gaṇādhipāḥ 
lokapālādhipāścaiva pitaro mātarastathā  MatsP 
imā vibhūtayaḥ proktāś carācarasamanvitāḥ 
brahmādyāś caturo mūlam avyaktādhipatiḥ smṛtaḥ  MatsP 
oṃ oṃ brahmaṇā cātha sūryeṇa viṣṇunātha śivena vā 
abhedātpūjitena syāt pūjitaṃ sacarācaram  MatsP 
brahmādīnāṃ paraṃ dhāma trayāṇāmapi saṃsthitiḥ 
vedamūrtāv ataḥ pūṣā pūjanīyaḥ prayatnataḥ  MatsP 
tasmādagnidvijamukhān kṛtvā sampūjayedimān 
dānairvratopavāsaiśca japahomādinā naraḥ  MatsP 
iti kriyāyogaparāyaṇasya vedāntaśāstrasmṛtivatsalasya 
vikarmabhītasya sadā na kiṃcit prāptavyamastīha pare ca loke  MatsP 
MatsyaPurāṇa 
munaya ūcuḥ
purāṇasaṃkhyāmācakṣva sūta vistaraśaḥ kramāt 
dānadharmamaśeṣaṃ tu yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ  MatsP 
sūta uvāca
idameva purāṇeṣu purāṇapuruṣastadā 
yaduktavānsa viśvātmā manave tannibodhata  MatsP 
matsya uvāca
purāṇaṃ sarvaśāstrāṇāṃ prathamaṃ brahmaṇā smṛtam 
anantaraṃ ca vaktrebhyo vedāstasya vinirgatāḥ  MatsP 
purāṇamekamevāsīt tadā kalpāntare 'nagha 
trivargasādhanaṃ puṇyaṃ śatakoṭipravistaram  MatsP 
nirdagdheṣu ca lokeṣu vājirūpeṇa vai mayā 
aṅgāni caturo vedān purāṇaṃ nyāyavistaram  MatsP 
mīmāṃsāṃ dharmaśāstraṃ ca parigṛhya mayā kṛtam 
matsyarūpeṇa ca punaḥ kalpādāvudakārṇave  MatsP 
aśeṣam etatkathitam udakāntargatena ca 
śrutvā jagāda ca munīn prati devāṃścaturmukhaḥ  MatsP 
pravṛttiḥ sarvaśāstrāṇāṃ purāṇasyābhavattataḥ 
kālenāgrahaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā purāṇasya tato nṛpa  MatsP 
vyāsarūpamahaṃ kṛtvā saṃharāmi yuge yuge 
caturlakṣapramāṇena dvāpare dvāpare sadā  MatsP 
tathāṣṭādaśadhā kṛtvā bhūrloke 'sminprakāśyate 
adyāpi devaloke 'smiñ chatakoṭipravistaram  MatsP 
tadartho 'tra caturlakṣaṃ saṃkṣepeṇa nivaśitaḥ 
purāṇāni daśāṣṭau ca sāmprataṃ tadihocyate  MatsP 
nāmatastāni vakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvaṃ munisattamāḥ 
brahmaṇābhihitaṃ pūrvaṃ yāvanmātraṃ marīcaye  MatsP 
brāhmaṃ tridaśasāhasraṃ purāṇaṃ parikīrtyate 
likhitvā tacca yo dadyāj jaladhenusamanvitam 
vaiśākhapūrṇimāyāṃ ca brahmaloke mahīyate  MatsP 
etadeva yadā padmam abhūddhairaṇmayaṃ jagat 
tadvṛttāntāśrayaṃ tadvat pādmamityucyate budhaiḥ 
pādmaṃ tatpañcapañcāśatsahasrāṇīha kathyate  MatsP 
tatpurāṇaṃ ca yo dadyāt suvarṇakamalānvitam 
jyeṣṭhe māsi tilairyuktam aśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet  MatsP 
vārāhakalpavṛttāntam adhikṛtya parāśaraḥ 
yatprāha dharmānakhilāṃs tadyuktaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ viduḥ  MatsP 
tadāṣāḍhe ca yo dadyād ghṛtadhenusamanvitam 
paurṇamāsyāṃ vipūtātmā sa padaṃ yāti vāruṇam 
trayoviṃśatisāhasraṃ tatpramāṇaṃ vidurbudhāḥ  MatsP 
śvetakalpaprasaṅgena dharmānvāyurihābravīt 
yatra tadvāyavīyaṃ syād rudramāhātmyasaṃyutam 
caturviṃśasahasrāṇi purāṇaṃ tadihocyate  MatsP 
śrāvaṇyāṃ śrāvaṇe māsi guḍadhenusamanvitam 
yo dadyādvṛṣasaṃyuktaṃ brāhmaṇāya kuṭumbine 
śivaloke sa pūtātmā kalpamekaṃ vasennaraḥ  MatsP 
yatrādhikṛtya gāyatrīṃ varṇyate dharmavistaraḥ 
vṛtrāsuravadhopetaṃ tadbhāgavatamucyate  MatsP 
sārasvatasya kalpasya madhye ye syurnarottamāḥ 
tadvṛttāntodbhavaṃ loke tadbhāgavatamucyate  MatsP 
likhitvā tacca yo dadyād dhemasiṃhasamanvitam 
paurṇamāsyāṃ prauṣṭhapadyāṃ sa yāti paramāṃ gatim 
aṣṭādaśa sahasrāṇi purāṇaṃ tatpracakṣate  MatsP 
yatrāha nārado dharmān bṛhatkalpāśrayāṇi ca 
pañcaviṃśatsahasrāṇi nāradīyaṃ taducyate  MatsP 
āśvine pañcadaśyāṃ tu dadyāddhenusamanvitam 
paramāṃ siddhimāpnoti punarāvṛttidurlabhām  MatsP 
yatrādhikṛtya śakunīn dharmādharmavicāraṇā 
vyākhyātā vai munipraśne munibhirdharmacāribhiḥ  MatsP 
mārkaṇḍeyena kathitaṃ tatsarvaṃ vistareṇa tu 
purāṇaṃ navasāhasraṃ mārkaṇḍeyam ihocyate  MatsP 
pratilikhya ca yo dadyāt sauvarṇakarisaṃyutam 
kārttikyāṃ puṇḍarīkasya yajñasya phalabhāgbhavet  MatsP 
yat tad īśānakaṃ kalpaṃ vṛttāntamadhikṛtya ca 
vasiṣṭhāyāgninā proktam āgneyaṃ tatpracakṣate  MatsP 
likhitvā tacca yo dadyād dhemapadmasamanvitam 
mārgaśīrṣyāṃ vidhānena tiladhenusamanvitam  MatsP 
tacca ṣoḍaśasāhasraṃ sarvakratuphalapradam 
yaḥ pradadhannaraḥ so 'tha svargaloke mahīyate  MatsP 
yatrādhikṛtya māhātmyam ādityasya caturmukhaḥ 
aghorakalpavṛttāntaprasaṅgena jagatsthitim 
manave kathayāmāsa bhūtagrāmasya lakṣaṇam  MatsP 
caturdaśa sahasrāṇi tathā pañca śatāni ca 
bhaviṣyacaritaprāyaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ tadihocyate  MatsP 
tatpauṣe māsi yo dadyāt paurṇamāsyāṃ vimatsaraḥ 
guḍakumbhasamāyuktam agniṣṭomaphalaṃ bhavet  MatsP 
rathaṃtarasya kalpasya vṛttāntamadhikṛtya ca 
sāvarṇinā nāradāya kṛṣṇamāhātmyamuttamam  MatsP 
yatra brahmavarāhasya codantaṃ varṇitaṃ muhuḥ 
tadaṣṭādaśasāhasraṃ brahmavaivartamucyate  MatsP 
purāṇaṃ brahmavaivartaṃ yo dadyānmāghamāsi ca 
paurṇamāsyāṃ śubhadine brahmaloke mahīyate  MatsP 
yatrāgniliṅgamadhyasthaḥ prāha devo maheśvaraḥ 
dharmārthakāmamokṣārtham āgneyamadhikṛtya ca  MatsP 
kalpānte laiṅgamityuktaṃ purāṇaṃ brahmaṇā svayam 
tadekādaśasāhasraṃ phālgunyāṃ yaḥ prayacchati 
tiladhenusamāyuktaṃ sa yāti śivasāmyatām  MatsP 
mahāvarāhasya punar māhātmyamadhikṛtya ca 
viṣṇunābhihitaṃ kṣoṇyai tadvārāham ihocyate  MatsP 
mānavasya prasaṅgena kalpasya munisattamāḥ 
caturviṃśatsahasrāṇi tatpurāṇamihocyate  MatsP 
kāñcanaṃ garuḍaṃ kṛtvā tiladhenusamanvitam 
paurṇamāsyāṃ madhau dadyād brāhmaṇāya kuṭumbine 
varāhasya prasādena padamāpnoti vaiṣṇavam  MatsP 
yatra māheśvarāndharmān adhikṛtya ca ṣaṇmukhaḥ 
kalpe tatpuruṣaṃ vṛttaṃ caritairupabṛṃhitam  MatsP 
skāndaṃ nāma purāṇaṃ ca hy ekāśītirnigadyate 
sahasrāṇi śataṃ caikam iti martyeṣu gadyate  MatsP 
parilikhya ca yo dadyād dhemaśūlasamanvitam 
śaivaṃ padamavāpnoti mīne copāgate ravau  MatsP 
trivikramasya māhātmyam adhikṛtya caturmukhaḥ 
trivargamabhyadhāttacca vāmanaṃ parikīrtitam  MatsP 
purāṇaṃ daśasāhasraṃ kūrmakalpānugaṃ śivam 
yaḥ śaradviṣuve dadyād vaiṣṇavaṃ yātyasau padam  MatsP 
yatra dharmārthakāmānāṃ mokṣasya ca rasātale 
māhātmyaṃ kathayāmāsa kūrmarūpī janārdanaḥ  MatsP 
indradyumnaprasaṅgena ṛṣibhyaḥ śakrasaṃnidhau 
aṣṭādaśa sahasrāṇi lakṣmīkalpānuṣaṅgikam  MatsP 
yo dadyādayane kūrmaṃ hemakūrmasamanvitam 
gosahasrapradānasya phalaṃ samprāpnuyānnaraḥ  MatsP 
śrutīnāṃ yatra kalpādau pravṛttyarthaṃ janārdanaḥ 
matsyarūpeṇa manave narasiṃhopavarṇanam  MatsP 
adhikṛtyābravītsaptakalpavṛttaṃ munīśvarāḥ 
tanmātsyamiti jānīdhvaṃ sahasrāṇi caturdaśa  MatsP 
viṣuve hemamatsyena dhenvā caiva samanvitam 
yo dadyātpṛthivī tena dattā bhavati cākhilā  MatsP 
yadā ca gāruḍe kalpe viśvāṇḍādgaruḍodbhavam 
adhikṛtyābravītkṛṣṇo gāruḍaṃ tadihocyate  MatsP 
tad aṣṭādaśakaṃ caikaṃ sahasrāṇīha paṭhyate 
sauvarṇahaṃsasaṃyuktaṃ yo dadāti pumāniha 
sa siddhiṃ labhate mukhyāṃ śivaloke ca saṃsthitim  MatsP 
brahmā brahmāṇḍamāhātmyam adhikṛtyābravītpunaḥ 
tacca dvādaśasāhasraṃ brahmāṇḍaṃ dviśatādhikam  MatsP 
bhaviṣyāṇāṃ ca kalpānāṃ śrūyate yatra vistaraḥ 
tadbrahmāṇḍapurāṇaṃ ca brahmaṇā samudāhṛtam  MatsP 
yo dadyāttadvyatīpāte pītorṇāyugasaṃyutam 
rājasūyasahasrasya phalamāpnoti mānavaḥ 
hemadhenvā yutaṃ tacca brahmalokaphalapradam  MatsP 
caturlakṣamidaṃ proktaṃ vyāsenādbhutakarmaṇā 
matpiturmama pitrā ca mayā tubhyaṃ niveditam  MatsP 
iha lokahitārthāya saṃkṣiptaṃ paramarṣiṇā 
idamadyāpi deveṣu śatakoṭipravistaram  MatsP 
upabhedānpravakṣyāmi loke ye sampratiṣṭhitāḥ 
pādme purāṇe yatroktaṃ narasiṃhopavarṇanam 
taccāṣṭādaśasāhasraṃ nārasiṃhamihocyate  MatsP 
nandāyā yatra māhātmyaṃ kārttikeyena varṇyate 
nandīpurāṇaṃ tallokair ākhyātamiti kīrtyate  MatsP 
yatra sāmbaṃ puraskṛtya bhaviṣyati kathānakam 
procyate tatpunarloke sāmbametanmunivratāḥ  MatsP 
purātanasya kalpasya purāṇāni vidurbudhāḥ 
dhanyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ purāṇānāmanukramam 
evamādityasaṃjñā ca tatraiva parigadyate  MatsP 
aṣṭādaśabhyastu pṛthak purāṇaṃ yatpradiśyate 
vijānīdhvaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhās tadetebhyo vinirgatam  MatsP 
pañcāṅgāni purāṇeṣu ākhyānakamiti smṛtam 
sargaśca pratisargaśca vaṃśo manvantarāṇi ca 
vaṃśyānucaritaṃ caiva purāṇaṃ pañcalakṣaṇam  MatsP 
brahmaviṣṇvarkarudrāṇāṃ māhātmyaṃ bhuvanasya ca 
sasaṃhārapradānāṃ ca purāṇe pañcavarṇake  MatsP 
dharmaścārthaśca kāmaśca mokṣaścaivātra kīrtyate 
sarveṣvapi purāṇeṣu tadviruddhaṃ ca yatphalam  MatsP 
sāttvikeṣu purāṇeṣu māhātmyamadhikaṃ hareḥ 
rājaseṣu ca māhātmyam adhikaṃ brahmaṇo viduḥ  MatsP 
tadvadagneśca māhātmyaṃ tāmaseṣu śivasya ca 
saṃkīrṇeṣu sarasvatyāḥ pitṝṇāṃ ca nigadyate  MatsP 
aṣṭādaśa purāṇāni kṛtvā satyavatīsutaḥ 
bhāratākhyānamakhilaṃ cakre tadupabṛṃhitam 
lakṣeṇaikena yatproktaṃ vedārthaparibṛṃhitam  MatsP 
vālmīkinā tu yatproktaṃ rāmopākhyānamuttamam 
brahmaṇābhihitaṃ yacca śatakoṭipravistaram  MatsP 
āhṛtya nāradāyaivaṃ tena vālmīkaye punaḥ 
vālmīkinā ca lokeṣu dharmakāmārthasādhanam 
evaṃ sapādāḥ pañcaite lakṣā martye prakīrtitāḥ  MatsP 
purātanasya kalpasya purāṇāni vidurbudhāḥ 
dhanyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ purāṇānāmanukramam 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi sa yāti paramāṃ gatim  MatsP 
idaṃ pavitraṃ yaśaso nidhānam idaṃ pitṝṇāmativallabhaṃ ca 
idaṃ ca deveṣv amṛtāyitaṃ ca nityaṃ tvidaṃ pāpaharaṃ ca puṃsām  MatsP

sūta uvāca
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi dānadharmānaśeṣataḥ 
vratopavāsasaṃyuktān yathāmatsyoditāniha  MatsP 
mahādevasya saṃvāde nāradasya ca dhīmataḥ 
yathāvṛttaṃ pravakṣyāmi dharmakāmārthasādhakam  MatsP 
kailāsaśikharāsīnam apṛcchannāradaḥ purā 
vinayanamanaṅgārim anaṅgāṅgaharaṃ haram  MatsP 
nārada uvāca
bhagavandevadeveśa brahmaviṣṇvindranāyaka 
śrīmadārogyarūpāyur bhāgyasaubhāgyasampadā 
saṃyuktastava viṣṇorvā pumānbhaktaḥ kathaṃ bhavet  MatsP 
nārī vā vidhavā sarvaguṇasaubhāgyasaṃyutā 
kramānmuktipradaṃ deva kiṃcidvratamihocyatām  MatsP 
īśvara uvāca
samyakpṛṣṭaṃ tvayā brahman sarvalokahitāvaham 
śrutamapyatra yacchāntyai tadvrataṃ śṛṇu nārada  MatsP 
nakṣatrapuruṣaṃ nāma vrataṃ nārāyaṇātmakam 
pādādi kuryādvidhivad viṣṇunāmānukīrtanam  MatsP 
pratimāṃ vāsudevasya mūlarkṣādiṣu cārcayet 
caitramāsaṃ samāsādya kṛtvā brāhmaṇavācanam  MatsP 
mūle namo viśvadharāya pādau gulphāvanantāya ca rohiṇīṣu 
jaṅghe 'bhipūjye varadāya caiva dve jānunī vāśvikumāraṛkṣe  MatsP 
pūrvottarāṣāḍhayuge tathorū namaḥ śivāyetyabhipūjanīyau 
pūrvottarāphalguniyugmake ca meḍhraṃ namaḥ pañcaśarāya pūjyam  MatsP 
kaṭiṃ namaḥ śārṅgadharāya viṣṇoḥ sampūjayennārada kṛttikāsu 
tathārcayedbhādrapadādvaye ca pārśve namaḥ keśiniṣūdanāya  MatsP 
kukṣidvayaṃ nārada revatīṣu dāmodarāyetyabhipūjanīyam 
ṛkṣe 'nurādhāsu ca mādhavāya namastathoraḥsthalameva pūjyam  MatsP 
pṛṣṭhaṃ dhaniṣṭhāsu ca pūjanīyam aghaughavidhvaṃsakarāya tacca 
śrīśaṅkhacakrāsigadādharāya namo viśākhāsu bhujāśca pūjyāḥ  MatsP 
haste tu hastā madhusūdanāya namo 'bhipūjyā iti kaiṭabhāreḥ 
punarvasāvaṅgulipūrvabhāgāḥ sāmnāmadhīśāya namo 'bhipūjyāḥ  MatsP 
bhujaṃganakṣatradine nakhāni sampūjayenmatsyaśarīrabhājaḥ 
kūrmasya pādau śaraṇaṃ vrajāmi jyeṣṭhāsu kaṇṭhe harirarcanīyaḥ  MatsP 
śrotre varāhāya namo 'bhipūjyā janārdanasya śravaṇena samyak 
puṣye mukhaṃ dānavasūdanāya namo nṛsiṃhāya ca pūjanīyam  MatsP 
namo namaḥ kāraṇavāmanāya svātīṣu dantāgramathārcanīyam 
āsyaṃ harerbhārgavanandanāya saṃpūjanīyaṃ dvija vāruṇe tu  MatsP 
namo 'stu rāmāya maghāsu nāsā saṃpūjanīyā raghunandanasya 
mṛgottamāṅge nayane 'bhipūjye namo 'stu te rāma vighūrṇitākṣa  MatsP 
buddhāya śāntāya namo lalāṭaṃ citrāsu saṃpūjyatamaṃ murāreḥ 
śiro 'bhipūjyaṃ bharaṇīṣu viṣṇor namo 'stu viśveśvara kalkirūpiṇe  MatsP 
ārdrāsu keśāḥ puruṣottamasya saṃpūjanīyā haraye namaste 
upoṣitenarkṣadineṣu bhaktyā saṃpūjanīyā dvijapuṃgavāḥ syuḥ  MatsP 
pūrṇe vrate sarvaguṇānvitāya vāgrūpaśīlāya ca sāmagāya 
haimīṃ viśālāyatabāhudaṇḍāṃ muktāphalendūpalavajrayuktām  MatsP 
jalasya pūrṇe kalaśe niviṣṭām arcāṃ harervastragavā sahaiva 
śayyāṃ tathopaskarabhājanādiyuktāṃ pradadyāddvijapuṃgavāya  MatsP 
yadyasti yatkiṃcidihāsti deyaṃ dadyāddvijāyātmahitāya sarvam 
manorathānnaḥ saphalīkuruṣva hiraṇyagarbhācyutarudrarūpin  MatsP

caturthīkarma kartavyaṃ deyā tatrāpi śaktitaḥ 
dakṣiṇā rājaśārdūla varuṇakṣmāpaṇaṃ tataḥ  MatsP

hemapātrīṃ ca śayyāṃ ca sthāpakāya nivedayet  MatsP 
tataḥ sahasraṃ viprāṇām athavāṣṭaśataṃ tathā

evameṣa purāṇeṣu taḍāgavidhirucyate  MatsP

mantratastu viśeṣaḥ syāt prāsādādyānabhūmiṣu 
ayaṃ tvaśaktāvardhena vidhirdṛṣṭaḥ svayambhuvā

tatrāntare 'bhyājagāma vasiṣṭho brahmasambhavaḥ  MatsP

videhastvaṃ bhavasveti tatastenāpyasau muniḥ  MatsP 
anyonyaśāpācca tayor vigate iva cetasī 
jagmatuḥ śāpanāśāya brahmāṇaṃ jagataḥ patim  MatsP 
atha brahmaṇa ādeśāl locaneṣvavasannimiḥ 
nimeṣāḥ syuśca lokānāṃ tadviśrāmāya nārada  MatsP 
vasiṣṭho 'pyabhavattasmiñ jalakumbhe ca pūrvavat 
tataḥ śvetaścaturbāhuḥ sākṣasūtrakamaṇḍaluḥ 
agastya iti śāntātmā babhūva ṛṣisattamaḥ  MatsP 
malayasyaikadeśe tu vaikhānasavidhānataḥ 
sabhāryaḥ saṃvṛto viprais tapaścakre suduścaram  MatsP 
tataḥ kālena mahatā tārakād atipīḍitam 
jagadvīkṣya sa kopena pītavānvaruṇālayam  MatsP 
tato 'sya varadāḥ sarve babhūvuḥ śaṃkarādayaḥ 
brahmā viṣṇuśca bhagavān varadānāya jagmatuḥ 
varaṃ vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te yadabhīṣṭaṃ ca vai mune  MatsP 
agastya uvāca
yāvadbrahmasahasrāṇāṃ pañcaviṃśatikoṭayaḥ 
vaimāniko bhaviṣyāmi dakṣiṇācalavartmani  MatsP 
madvimānodaye kuryād yaḥ kaścitpūjanaṃ mama 
sa saptalokādhipatiḥ paryāyeṇa bhaviṣyati  MatsP 
īśvara uvāca
evamastviti te 'pyuktvā jagmurdevā yathāgatam 
tasmādarghaḥ pradātavyo hy agastyasya sadā budhaiḥ  MatsP 
nārada uvāca
kathamarghapradānaṃ tu kartavyaṃ tasya vai vibho 
vidhānaṃ yadagastyasya pūjane tadvadasva me  MatsP 
īśvara uvāca
pratyūṣasamaye vidvān kuryādasyodaye niśi 
snānaṃ śuklatilaistadvac chuklamālyāmbaro gṛhī  MatsP 
sthāpayedavraṇaṃ kumbhaṃ mālyavastravibhūṣitam 
pañcaratnasamāyuktaṃ ghṛtapātrasamanvitam 
nānābhakṣyaphalairyuktaṃ tāmrapātrasamanvitam  MatsP 
aṅguṣṭhamātraṃ puruṣaṃ tathaiva sauvarṇam atyāyatabāhudaṇḍam 
caturmukhaṃ kumbhamukhe nidhāya dhānyāni saptāmbarasaṃyutāni  MatsP 
sakāṃsyapātrākṣataśuktiyuktaṃ mantreṇa dadyāddvijapuṃgavāya 
utkṣipya lambodaradīrghabāhum ananyacetā yamadiṅmukhaḥ san  MatsP 
śvetāṃ ca dadyādyadi śaktirasti raupyaiḥ khurair hemamukhīṃ savatsām 
dhenuṃ naraḥ kṣīravatīṃ praṇamya savatsaghaṇṭābharaṇāṃ dvijāya  MatsP 
ā saptarātrodayam etadasya dātavyametatsakalaṃ nareṇa 
yāvatsamāḥ sapta daśāthavā syur athordhvamapyatra vadanti kecit  MatsP 
kāśapuṣpapratīkāśa vahnimārutasambhava 
mitrāvaruṇayoḥ putra kumbhayone namo 'stu te  MatsP 
vindhyavṛddhikṣayakara meghatoyaviṣāpaha 
ratnavallabha deveśa laṅkāvāsinnamo 'stu te  MatsP 
vātāpī bhakṣito yena samudraḥ śoṣitaḥ purā 
lopāmudrāpatiḥ śrīmān yo 'sau tasmai namo namaḥ  MatsP 
rājaputri mahābhāge ṛṣipatni varānane 
lopāmudre namastubhyam argho me pratigṛhyatām 
pratyabdaṃ tu phalatyāgam evaṃ kurvanna sīdati  MatsP 
homaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ paścād varjayenmānavaḥ phalam 
anena vidhinā yastu pumānarghyaṃ nivedayet  MatsP 
imaṃ lokaṃ sa cāpnoti rūpārogyasamanvitaḥ 
dvitīyena bhuvarlokaṃ svargalokaṃ tataḥ param  MatsP 
saptaiva lokānāpnoti saptārghān yaḥ prayacchati 
yāvadāyuśca yaḥ kuryāt paraṃ brahmādhigacchati  MatsP 
iha paṭhati śṛṇoti vā ya etad yugalamuniprabhavārghyasampradānam 
matimapi ca dadāti so 'pi viṣṇor bhavanagataḥ paripūjyate 'maraughaiḥ  MatsP 
MatsyaPurāṇa 
manuruvāca
saubhāgyārogyaphaladam amutrākṣayyakārakam 
bhuktimuktipradaṃ deva tanme brūhi janārdana  MatsP 
matsya uvāca
yadumāyāḥ purā deva uvāca purasūdanaḥ 
kailāsaśikharāsīno devyā pṛṣṭastadā kila  MatsP 
kathāsu sampravṛttāsu dharmyāsu lalitāsu ca 
tadidānīṃ pravakṣyāmi bhuktimuktiphalapradam  MatsP 
īśvara uvāca
śṛṇuṣvāvahitā devi tathaivānantapuṇyakṛt 
narāṇāmatha nārīṇām ārādhanamanuttamam  MatsP 
nabhasye vātha vaiśākhe puṇyamārgaśirasya ca 
śuklapakṣe tṛtīyāyāṃ susnāto gaurasarṣapaiḥ  MatsP 
gorocanaṃ sagomūtram uṣṇaṃ gośakṛtaṃ tathā 
dadhicandanasammiśraṃ lalāṭe tilakaṃ nyaset 
saubhāgyārogyadaṃ yasmāt sadā ca lalitāpriyam  MatsP 
pratipakṣaṃ tṛtīyāsu pumānāpītavāsasī 
dhārayedatha raktāni nārī cedatha saṃyatā  MatsP 
vidhavā dhāturaktāni kumārī śuklavāsasī 
devīṃ tu pañcagavyena tataḥ kṣīreṇa kevalam 
snāpayenmadhunā tadvat puṣpagandhodakena ca  MatsP 
pūjayecchuklapuṣpaiśca phalairnānāvidhairapi 
dhānyakājājilavaṇair guḍakṣīraghṛtānvitaiḥ  MatsP 
śuklākṣatatilairarcyāṃ tato devīṃ sadārcayet 
pādādyabhyarcanaṃ kuryāt pratipakṣaṃ varānane  MatsP 
varadāyai namaḥ pādau tathā gulphau namaḥ śriyai 
aśokāyai namo jaṅghe pārvatyai jānunī tathā  MatsP 
ūrū maṅgalakāriṇyai vāmadevyai tathā kaṭim 
padmodarāyai jaṭharam uraḥ kāmaśriyai namaḥ  MatsP 
karau saubhāgyadāyinyai bāhū haramukhaśriyai 
mukhaṃ darpaṇavāsinyai smaradāyai smitaṃ namaḥ  MatsP 
gauryai namastathā nāsām utpalāyai ca locane 
tuṣṭyai lalāṭamalakān kātyāyanyai śirastathā  MatsP 
namo gauryai namo dhiṣṇyai namaḥ kāntyai namaḥ śriyai 
rambhāyai lalitāyai ca vāsudevyai namo namaḥ  MatsP 
evaṃ sampūjya vidhivad agrataḥ padmamālikhet 
pattrairdvādaśabhiryuktaṃ kuṅkumena sakarṇikam  MatsP 
pūrveṇa vinyasedgaurīm aparṇāṃ ca tataḥ param 
bhavānīṃ dakṣiṇe tadvad rudrāṇīṃ ca tataḥ param  MatsP 
vinyasetpaścime saumyāṃ sadā madanavāsinīm 
vāyavye pāṭalāmugrām antareṇa tato 'pyumām  MatsP 
madhye yathāsvaṃ māṃsāṅgāṃ maṅgalāṃ kumudāṃ satīm 
rudraṃ ca madhye saṃsthāpya lalitāṃ karṇikopari 
kusumairakṣatairvārbhir namaskāreṇa vinyaset  MatsP 
gītamaṅgalanirghoṣān kārayitvā suvāsinīḥ 
pūjayedraktavāsobhī raktamālyānulepanaiḥ 
sindūraṃ snānacūrṇaṃ ca tāsāṃ śirasi pātayet  MatsP 
sindūrakuṅkumasnānam atīveṣṭatamaṃ yataḥ 
tathopadeṣṭāramapi pūjayedyatnato gurum 
na pūjyate gururyatra sarvāstatrāphalāḥ kriyāḥ  MatsP 
nabhasye pūjayedgaurīm utpalairasitaiḥ sadā 
bandhujīvairāśvayuje kārttike śatapattrakaiḥ  MatsP 
jātīpuṣpairmārgaśīrṣe pauṣe pītaiḥ kuraṇṭakaiḥ 
kundakuṅkumapuṣpaistu devīṃ māghe tu pūjayet 
sinduvāreṇa jātyā vā phālgune 'pyarcayedumām  MatsP 
caitre tu mallikāśokair vaiśākhe gandhapāṭalaiḥ 
jyeṣṭhe kamalamandārair āṣāḍhe ca navāmbujaiḥ 
kadambairatha mālatyā śrāvaṇe pūjayetsadā  MatsP 
gomūtraṃ gomayaṃ kṣīraṃ dadhi sarpiḥ kuśodakam 
bilvapattrārkapuṣpaṃ ca yavāngośṛṅgavāri ca  MatsP 
pañcagavyaṃ ca bilvaṃ ca prāśayetkramaśastadā 
etadbhādrapadādyaṃ tu prāśanaṃ samudāhṛtam  MatsP 
pratipakṣaṃ ca mithunaṃ tṛtīyāyāṃ varānane 
pūjayitvārcayedbhaktyā vastramālyānulepanaiḥ  MatsP 
puṃsaḥ pītāmbare dadyāt striyai kausumbhavāsasī 
niṣpāvājājilavaṇam ikṣudaṇḍaguḍānvitam 
tasyai dadyātphalaṃ puṣpaṃ suvarṇotpalasaṃyutam  MatsP 
yathā na devi deveśas tvāṃ parityajya gacchati 
tathā mām uddharāśeṣaduḥkhasaṃsārasāgarāt  MatsP 
kumudā vimalānantā bhavānī ca sudhā śivā 
lalitā kamalā gaurī satī rambhātha pārvatī  MatsP 
nabhasyādiṣu māseṣu prīyatāmityudīrayet 
vratānte śayanaṃ dadyāt suvarṇakamalānvitam  MatsP 
mithunāni caturviṃśad daśa dvo ca samarcayet 
aṣṭau ṣaḍvāpyatha punaś cānumāsaṃ samarcayet  MatsP 
pūrvaṃ dattvā tu gurave śeṣānapyarcayedbudhaḥ 
uktānantatṛtīyaiṣā sadānantaphalapradā  MatsP 
sarvapāpaharāṃ devi saubhāgyārogyavardhinīm 
na caināṃ vittaśāṭhyena kadācidapi laṅghayet 
naro vā yadi vā nārī vittaśāṭhyāt patatyadhaḥ  MatsP 
garbhiṇī sūtikā naktaṃ kumārī vātha rogiṇī 
yadyaśuddhā tadānyena vārayetprayatā svayam  MatsP 
imāmanantaphaladāṃ yastṛtīyāṃ samācaret 
kalpakoṭiśataṃ sāgraṃ śivaloke mahīyate  MatsP 
vittahīno 'pi kurute varṣatrayamupoṣaṇaiḥ 
puṣpamantravidhānena so 'pi tatphalamāpnuyāt  MatsP

sāpi tatphalamāpnoti gauryanugrahalālitā  MatsP 
iti paṭhati śṛṇoti vā ya itthaṃ giritanayāvratam indravāsasaṃsthaḥ 
matimapi ca dadāti so 'pi devair amaravadhūjanakiṃnaraiśca pūjyaḥ  MatsP

īśvara uvāca
athānyāmapi vakṣyāmi tṛtīyāṃ pāpanāśinīm 
rasakalyāṇinīmetāṃ purākalpavido viduḥ  MatsP 
māghamāse tu samprāpte tṛtīyāṃ śuklapakṣataḥ 
prātargavyena payasā tilaiḥ snānaṃ samācaret  MatsP 
snāpayenmadhunā devīṃ tathaivekṣurasena ca 
gandhodakena tu punar lepayetkuṅkumena tu 
dakṣiṇāṅgāni sampūjya tato vāmāni pūjayet  MatsP 
lalitāyai namo devyāḥ pādau gulphau tato 'rcayet 
jaṅghāṃ jānuṃ tathā śāntyai tathaivoruṃ śriyai namaḥ  MatsP 
madālasāyai tu kaṭim amalāyai tathodaram 
stanau madanavāsinyai kumudāyai ca kandarām  MatsP 
bhujaṃ bhujāgraṃ mādhavyai kamalāyai mukhasmite 
bhūlalāṭaṃ ca rudrāṇyai śaṃkarāyai tathālakān  MatsP 
mukuṭaṃ viśvavāsinyai śiraḥ kāntyai tathārcayet 
madanāyai lalāṭaṃ tu mohanāyai punarbhruvau  MatsP 
netre candrārdhadhāriṇyai tuṣṭyai ca vadanaṃ punaḥ 
utkaṇṭhinyai namaḥ kaṇṭham amṛtāyai namaḥ stanau  MatsP 
rambhāyai vāmakukṣiṃ ca viśokāyai namaḥ kaṭim 
hṛdayaṃ manmathādhiṣṇyai pāṭalāyai tathodaram  MatsP 
kaṭiṃ suratavāsinyai tathoruṃ campakapriye 
jānujaṅghe namo gauryai gāyatryai ghuṭike namaḥ  MatsP 
dharādharāyai pādau tu viśvakāyai namaḥ śiraḥ 
namo bhavānyai kāminyai kāmadevyai jagatpriye  MatsP 
ānandāyai sunandāyai subhadrāyai namo namaḥ 
evaṃ sampūjya vidhivad dvijadāmpatyam arcayet 
bhojayitvānnapānena madhureṇa vimatsaraḥ  MatsP 
jalapūritaṃ tathā kumbhaṃ śuklāmbarayugadvayam 
dattvā suvarṇakamalaṃ gandhamālyaiḥ samarcayet  MatsP 
prīyatāmatra kumudā gṛhṇīyāllavaṇavratam 
anena vidhinā devī māsi māsi sadārcayet  MatsP 
lavaṇaṃ varjayenmāghe phālgune ca guḍaṃ punaḥ 
tailaṃ rājiṃ tathā caitre varjyaṃ ca madhu mādhave  MatsP 
pānakaṃ jyeṣṭhamāse tu āṣāḍhe cātha jīrakam 
śrāvaṇe varjayetkṣīraṃ dadhi bhādrapade tathā  MatsP 
ghṛtamāśvayuje tadvad ūrje varjyaṃ ca mākṣikam 
dhānyakaṃ mārgaśīrṣe tu pauṣe varjyā ca śarkarā  MatsP 
vratānte karakaṃ pūrṇam eteṣāṃ māsi māsi ca 
dadyāddvikālavelāyāṃ pūrṇapātreṇa saṃyutam  MatsP 
laḍḍukāñchvetavarṇāṃśca saṃyāvamatha pūrikāḥ 
ghārikān apyapūpāṃśca piṣṭāpūpāṃśca maṇḍakān  MatsP 
kṣīraṃ śākaṃ ca dadhyannam iṇḍaryo 'śokavartikāḥ 
māghādikramaśo dadyād etāni karakopari  MatsP 
kumudā mādhavī gaurī rambhā bhadrā jayā śivā 
umā ratiḥ satī tadvan maṅgalā ratilālasā  MatsP 
kramānmāghādi sarvatra prīyatāmiti kīrtayet 
sarvatra pañcagavyena prāśanaṃ samudāhṛtam 
upavāsī bhavennityam aśakte naktamiṣyate  MatsP 
punarmāghe tu samprāpte śarkarāṃ karakopari 
kṛtvā tu kāñcanīṃ gaurīṃ pañcaratnasamanvitām  MatsP 
haimīmaṅguṣṭhamātrāṃ ca sākṣasūtrakamaṇḍalum 
caturbhujāminduyutāṃ sitanetrapaṭāvṛtām  MatsP 
tadvadgomithunaṃ śuklaṃ suvarṇāsyaṃ sitāmbaram 
savastrabhājanaṃ dadyād bhavānī prīyatāmiti  MatsP 
anena vidhinā yastu rasakalyāṇinīvratam 
kuryātsa sarvapāpebhyas tatkṣaṇādeva mucyate  MatsP 
navārbudasahasraṃ tu na duḥkhī jāyate naraḥ 
suvarṇakamalaṃ gauri māsi māsi dadannaraḥ 
agniṣṭomasahasrasya yatphalaṃ tadavāpnuyāt  MatsP 
nārī vā kurute yā tu kumārī vā varānane 
vidhavā yā tathā nārī sāpi tatphalamāpnuyāt 
saubhāgyārogyasampannā gaurīloke mahīyate  MatsP 
iti paṭhati śṛṇoti śrāvayedyaḥ prasaṅgāt kalikaluṣavimuktaḥ pārvatīlokameti 
matimapi ca narāṇāṃ yo dadāti priyārthaṃ vibudhapativimāne nāyakaḥ syādamoghaḥ  MatsP

īśvara uvāca
tathaivānyāṃ pravakṣyāmi tṛtīyāṃ pāpanāśinīm 
nāmnā ca loke vikhyātām ārdrānandakarīmimām  MatsP 
yadā śuklatṛtīyāyām āṣāḍharkṣaṃ bhavetkvacit 
brahmarkṣaṃ vā mṛgarkṣaṃ vā hasto mūlamathāpi vā 
darbhagandhodakaiḥ snānaṃ tadā samyaksamācaret  MatsP 
śuklamālyāmbaradharaḥ śuklagandhānulepanaḥ 
bhavānīmarcayedbhaktyā śuklapuṣpaiḥ sugandhibhiḥ 
mahādevena sahitām upaviṣṭāṃ mahāsane  MatsP 
vāsudevyai namaḥ pādau śaṃkarāya namo haram 
jaṅghe śokavināśinyai ānandāya namaḥ prabho  MatsP 
rambhāyai pūjayedūrū śivāya ca pinākinaḥ 
adityai ca kaṭiṃ devyāḥ śūlinaḥ śūlapāṇaye  MatsP

stanāvānandakāriṇyai śaṃkarasyendudhāriṇe  MatsP 
utkaṇṭhinyai namaḥ kaṇṭhaṃ nīlakaṇṭhāya vai haram 
karāvutpaladhāriṇyai rudrāya ca jagatpate 
bāhū ca parirambhiṇyai triśūlāya harasya ca  MatsP 
devyā mukhaṃ vilāsinyai vṛṣeśāya punarvibhoḥ 
smitaṃ sasmeralīlāyai viśvavaktrāya vai vibho  MatsP 
netre madanavāsinyai viśvadhāmne triśūlinaḥ 
bhruvau nṛtyapriyāyai tu tāṇḍaveśāya śūlinaḥ  MatsP 
devyā lalāṭamindrāṇyai havyavāhāya vai vibhoḥ 
svāhāyai mukuṭaṃ devyā vibhorgaṅgādharāya vai  MatsP 
viśvakāyau viśvamukhau viśvapādakarau śivau 
prasannavadanau vande pārvatīparameśvarau  MatsP 
evaṃ sampūjya vidhivad agrataḥ śivayoḥ punaḥ 
padmotpalāni rajasā nānāvarṇena kārayet  MatsP 
śaṅkhacakre sakaṭake svastikāṅkuśacāmarān 
yāvantaḥ pāṃsavastatra rajasaḥ patitā bhuvi 
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi śivaloke mahīyate  MatsP 
catvāri ghṛtapātrāṇi sahiraṇyāni śaktitaḥ 
dattvā dvijāya karakam udakānnasamanvitam 
pratipakṣaṃ caturmāsaṃ yāvadetannivedayet  MatsP 
tatastu caturo māsān pūrvavatkarakopari 
catvāri saktupātrāṇi tilapātrāṇyataḥ param  MatsP 
gandhodakaṃ puṣpavāri candanaṃ kuṅkumodakam 
apakvaṃ dadhi dugdhaṃ ca gośṛṅgodakameva ca  MatsP 
piṣṭodakaṃ tathā vāri kuṣṭhacūrṇānvitaṃ punaḥ 
uśīrasalilaṃ tadvad yavacūrṇodakaṃ punaḥ  MatsP 
tilodakaṃ ca saṃprāśya svapenmārgaśirādiṣu 
māseṣu pakṣadvitayaṃ prāśanaṃ samudāhṛtam  MatsP 
sarvatra śuklapuṣpāṇi praśastāni sadārcane 
dānakāle ca sarvatra mantrametamudīrayet  MatsP 
gaurī me prīyatāṃ nityam aghanāśāya maṅgalā 
saubhāgyāyāstu lalitā bhavānī sarvasiddhaye  MatsP 
saṃvatsarānte lavaṇaṃ guḍakumbhaṃ ca sarjikām 
candanaṃ netrapaṭṭaṃ ca sahiraṇyāmbujena tu  MatsP 
umāmaheśvaraṃ haimaṃ tadvadikṣuphalairyutam 
satūlāvaraṇāṃ śayyāṃ saviśrāmāṃ nivedayet 
sapatnīkāya viprāya gaurī me prīyatāmiti  MatsP 
ārdrānandakarī nāmnā tṛtīyaiṣā sanātanī 
yāmupoṣya naro yāti śambhoryatparamaṃ padam  MatsP 
iha loke sadānandam āpnoti dhanasampadaḥ 
āyurārogyasampattyā na kaścicchokamāpnuyāt  MatsP 
nārī vā kurute yā tu kumārī vidhavā ca yā 
sāpi tatphalamāpnoti devyanugrahalālitā  MatsP 
pratipakṣamupoṣyaivaṃ mantrārcanavidhānavit 
rudrāṇīlokamabhyeti punarāvṛttidurlabham  MatsP 
ya idaṃ śṛṇuyānnityaṃ śrāvayedvāpi mānavaḥ 
śakraloke sa gandharvaiḥ pūjyate 'pi yugatrayam  MatsP 
ānandadāṃ sakaladuḥkhaharāṃ tṛtīyāṃ yā strī karotyavidhavā vidhavātha vāpi 
sā sve gṛhe sukhaśatānyanubhūya bhūyo gaurīpadaṃ sadayitā dayitā prayāti  MatsP

īśvara uvāca
athānyāmapi vakṣyāmi tṛtīyāṃ sarvakāmadām 
yasyāṃ dattaṃ hutaṃ japtaṃ sarvaṃ bhavati cākṣayam  MatsP 
vaiśākhaśuklapakṣe tu tṛtīyā yairupoṣitā 
akṣayaṃ phalamāpnoti sarvasya sukṛtasya ca  MatsP 
sā tathā kṛttikopetā viśeṣeṇa supūjitā 
tatra dattaṃ hutaṃ japtaṃ sarvamakṣayamucyate  MatsP 
akṣayā saṃtatistasyās tasyāṃ sukṛtamakṣayam 
akṣataiḥ pūjyate viṣṇus tena sāpyakṣayā smṛtā 
akṣataistu narāḥ snātā viṣṇordattvā tathākṣatān  MatsP 
vipreṣu dattvā tāneva tathā saktūn susaṃkṛtān 
yathānnabhuṅmahābhāgaḥ phalamakṣayyamaśnute  MatsP 
ekāmapyuktavatkṛtvā tṛtīyāṃ vidhivannaraḥ 
etāsāmapi sarvāsāṃ tṛtīyānāṃ phalaṃ bhavet  MatsP 
tṛtīyāyāṃ samabhyarcya sopavāso janārdanam 
rājasūyaphalaṃ prāpya gatimagryāṃ ca vindati  MatsP 
MatsyaPurāṇa 
manuruvāca
madhurā bhāratī kena vratena madhusūdana 
tathaiva janasaubhāgyam atividyāsu kauśalam  MatsP 
abhedaścāpi dampatyos tathā bandhujanena ca 
āyuśca vipulaṃ puṃsāṃ tanme kathaya mādhava  MatsP 
matsya uvāca
samyakpṛṣṭaṃ tvayā rājañ chṛṇu sārasvataṃ vratam 
yasya saṃkīrtanādeva tuṣyatīha sarasvatī  MatsP 
yo yadbhaktaḥ pumānkuryād etadvratamanuttamam 
tadvāsarādau sampūjya viprānetānsamācaret  MatsP 
athavādityavāreṇa grahatārābalena ca 
pāyasaṃ bhojayedviprān kṛtvā brāhmaṇavācanam  MatsP 
śuklavastrāṇi dattvā ca sahiraṇyāni śaktitaḥ 
gāyatrīṃ pūjayedbhaktyā śuklamālyānulepanaiḥ  MatsP 
yathā na devi bhagavān brahmaloke pitāmahaḥ 
tvāṃ parityajya saṃtiṣṭhet tathā bhava varapradā  MatsP 
vedāḥ śāstrāṇi sarvāṇi gītanṛtyādikaṃ ca yat 
na vihīnaṃ tvayā devi tathā me santu siddhayaḥ  MatsP 
lakṣmīrmedhā dharā puṣṭir gaurī tuṣṭiḥ prabhā matiḥ 
etābhiḥ pāhi cāṣṭābhis tanubhirmāṃ sarasvati  MatsP 
evaṃ sampūjya gāyatrīṃ vīṇākṣamaṇidhāriṇīm 
śuklapuṣpākṣatair bhaktyā sakamaṇḍalupustakām 
maunavratena bhuñjīta sāyaṃ prātastu dharmavit  MatsP 
pañcamyāṃ pratipakṣaṃ ca pūjayedbrahmavāsinīm 
tathaiva taṇḍulaprasthaṃ ghṛtapātreṇa saṃyutam 
kṣīraṃ dadyāddhiraṇyaṃ ca gāyatrī prīyatāmiti  MatsP 
saṃdhyāyāṃ ca tathā maunam etatkurvansamācaret 
nāntarā bhojanaṃ kuryād yāvanmāsāstrayodaśa  MatsP 
samāpte tu vrate kuryād bhojanaṃ śuklataṇḍulaiḥ 
pūrvaṃ savastrayugmaṃ ca dadyādviprāya bhojanam  MatsP 
devyā vitānaṃ ghaṇṭāṃ ca sitanetre payasvinīm 
candanaṃ vastrayugmaṃ ca dadyācca śikharaṃ punaḥ  MatsP 
tathopadeṣṭāramapi bhaktyā sampūjayedgurum 
vittaśāṭhyena rahito vastramālyānulepanaiḥ  MatsP 
anena vidhinā yastu kuryātsārasvataṃ vratam 
vidyāvānarthasaṃyukto raktakaṇṭhaśca jāyate  MatsP 
sarasvatyāḥ prasādena brahmaloke mahīyate 
nārī vā kurute yā tu sāpi tatphalagāminī  MatsP 
brahmaloke vased rājan yāvat kalpāyutatrayam  MatsP 
sārasvataṃ vrataṃ yastu śṛṇuyādapi yaḥ paṭhet 
vidyādharapure so 'pi vasetkalpāyutatrayam  MatsP 
MatsyaPurāṇa 
candrādityoparāge tu yatsnānamabhidhīyate 
tadahaṃ śrotumicchāmi dravyamantravidhānavit  MatsP 
matsya uvāca
yasya rāśiṃ samāsādya bhavedgrahaṇasamplavaḥ 
tasya snānaṃ pravakṣyāmi mantrauṣadhavidhānataḥ  MatsP 
candroparāgaṃ samprāpya kṛtvā brāhmaṇavācanam 
sampūjya caturo viprāñ śuklamālyānulepanaiḥ  MatsP 
pūrvamevoparāgasya samāsādyauṣadhādikam 
sthāpayec caturaḥ kumbhān avraṇānsāgarāniti  MatsP 
gajāśvarathyāvalmīkasaṃgamāddhradagokulāt 
rājadvārapradeśācca mṛdamānīya cākṣipet  MatsP 
pañcagavyaṃ ca kumbheṣu śuddhamuktāphalāni ca 
rocanāṃ padmaśaṅkhau ca pañcaratnasamanvitam  MatsP 
sphaṭikaṃ candanaṃ śvetaṃ tīrthavāri sasarṣapam 
rājadantaṃ sakumudaṃ tathaivośīraguggulam 
etatsarvaṃ vinikṣipya kumbheṣvāvāhayetsurān  MatsP 
sarve samudrāḥ saritas tīrthāni jaladā nadāḥ 
āyāntu yajamānasya duritakṣayakārakāḥ  MatsP 
yo 'sau vajradharo deva ādityānāṃ prabhurmataḥ 
sahasranayanaścendro grahapīḍāṃ vyapohatu  MatsP 
mukhaṃ yaḥ sarvadevānāṃ saptārciramitadyutiḥ 
candroparāgasambhūtām agniḥ pīḍāṃ vyapohatu  MatsP 
yaḥ karmasākṣī bhūtānāṃ dharmo mahiṣavāhanaḥ 
yamaścandroparāgotthāṃ mama pīḍāṃ vyapohatu  MatsP 
rakṣogaṇādhipaḥ sākṣāt pralayānalasaṃnibhaḥ 
khaḍgavyagro 'tibhīmaśca rakṣaḥpīḍāṃ vyapohatu  MatsP 
nāgapāśadharo devaḥ sākṣānmakaravāhanaḥ 
sa jalādhipatiś candragrahapīḍāṃ vyapohatu  MatsP 
prāṇarūpeṇa yo lokān pāti kṛṣṇamṛgapriyaḥ 
vāyuścandroparāgotthāṃ pīḍāmatra vyapohatu  MatsP 
yo 'sau nidhipatirdevaḥ khaḍgaśūlagadādharaḥ 
candroparāgakaluṣaṃ dhanado me vyapohatu  MatsP 
yo 'sāvindudharo devaḥ pinākī vṛṣavāhanaḥ 
candroparāgajāṃ pīḍāṃ vināśayatu śaṃkaraḥ  MatsP 
trailokye yāni bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca 
brahmaviṣṇvarkayuktāni tāni pāpaṃ dahantu vai  MatsP 
evamāmantrya taiḥ kumbhair abhiṣikto guṇānvitaiḥ 
ṛgyajuḥsāmamantraiśca śuklamālyānulepanaiḥ 
pūjayedvastragodānair brāhmaṇāniṣṭadevatāḥ  MatsP 
etāneva tato mantrān vilikhet karakānvitān 
vastrapaṭṭe 'thavā padme pañcaratnasamanvitān  MatsP 
yajamānasya śirasi nidadhyuste dvijottamāḥ 
tato 'tivāhayedvelām uparāgānugāminīm  MatsP 
prāṅmukhaḥ pūjayitvā tu namasyanniṣṭadevatām 
candragrahe vinirvṛtte kṛtagodānamaṅgalaḥ 
kṛtasnānāya taṃ paṭṭaṃ brāhmaṇāya nivedayet  MatsP 
anena vidhinā yastu grahasnānaṃ samācaret 
na tasya grahapīḍā syān na ca bandhujanakṣayaḥ  MatsP 
paramāṃ siddhimāpnoti punarāvṛttidurlabhām 
sūryagrahe sūryanāma sadā mantreṣu kīrtayet  MatsP 
adhikāḥ padmarāgāḥ syuḥ kapilāṃ ca suśobhanām 
prayacchecca niśāṃ patye candrasūryoparāgayoḥ  MatsP 
ya idaṃ śṛṇuyānnityaṃ śrāvayedvāpi mānavaḥ 
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ śakraloke mahīyate  MatsP 
MatsyaPurāṇa 
nārada uvāca
kimudvegādbhute kṛtyam alakṣmīḥ kena hanyate 
mṛtavatsābhiṣekādikāryeṣu ca kimiṣyate  MatsP 
śrībhagavānuvāca
purā kṛtāni pāpāni phalantyasmiṃstapodhana 
rogadaurgatyarūpeṇa tathaiveṣṭavadhena ca  MatsP 
tadvighātāya vakṣyāmi sadā kalpāṇakārakam 
saptamīsnapanaṃ nāma janapīḍāvināśanam  MatsP 
bālānāṃ maraṇaṃ yatra kṣīrapāṇāṃ pradṛśyate 
tadvadvṛddhāturāṇāṃ ca yauvane cāpi vartatām  MatsP 
śāntaye tatra vakṣyāmi mṛtavatsābhiṣecanam 
etad evādbhutodvegacittabhramavināśanam  MatsP 
bhaviṣyati ca vārāho yatra kalpastapodhana 
vaivasvataśca tatrāpi yadā tu manuruttamaḥ  MatsP 
bhaviṣyati ca tatraiva pañcaviṃśatimaṃ yadā 
kṛtaṃ nāma yugaṃ tatra haihayānvayavardhanaḥ 
bhavitā nṛpatirvīraḥ kṛtavīryaḥ pratāpavān  MatsP 
sa saptadvīpamakhilaṃ pālayiṣyati bhūtalam 
yāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi saptasaptati nārada  MatsP 
jātamātraṃ ca tasyāpi yāvatputraśataṃ tathā 
cyavanasya tu śāpena vināśamapayāsyati  MatsP 
sahasrabāhuśca yadā bhavitā tasya vai sutaḥ 
kuraṅganayanaḥ śrīmān sambhūto nṛpalakṣaṇaiḥ  MatsP 
kṛtavīryastadārādhya sahasrāṃśuṃ divākaram 
upavāsairvratairdivyair vedasūktaiśca nārada 
putrasya jīvanāyālam etatsnānamavāpsyati  MatsP 
kṛtavīryeṇa vai pṛṣṭa idaṃ vakṣyati bhāskaraḥ 
aśeṣaduṣṭaśamanaṃ sadā kalmaṣanāśanam  MatsP 
sūrya uvāca
alaṃ kleśena mahatā putrastava narādhipa 
bhaviṣyati ciraṃjīvī kiṃtu kalmaṣanāśanam  MatsP 
saptamīsnapanaṃ vakṣye sarvalokahitāya vai 
jātasya mṛtavatsāyāḥ saptame māsi nārada 
athavā śuklasaptamyām etatsarvaṃ praśasyate  MatsP 
grahatārābalaṃ labdhvā kṛtvā brāhmaṇavācanam 
bālasya janmanakṣatraṃ varjayettāṃ tithiṃ budhaḥ 
tadvadvṛddhāturāṇāṃ ca kṛtyaṃ syāditareṣu ca  MatsP 
gomayenānuliptāyāṃ bhūmāvekāgnivattadā 
taṇḍulai raktaśālīyaiś caruṃ gokṣīrasaṃyutam 
nirvapetsūryarudrābhyāṃ tanmantrābhyāṃ vidhānataḥ  MatsP 
kīrtayetsūryadevatyaṃ saptarcaṃ ca ghṛtāhutīḥ 
juhuyādrudrasūktena tadvadrudrāya nārada  MatsP 
hotavyāḥ samidhaścātra tathaivārkapalāśayoḥ 
yavakṛṣṇatilairhomaḥ kartavyo 'ṣṭaśataṃ punaḥ  MatsP 
vyāhṛtībhistathājyena tathaivāṣṭaśataṃ punaḥ 
hutvā snānaṃ ca kartavyaṃ maṅgalaṃ yena dhīmatā  MatsP 
vipreṇa vedaviduṣā vidhivaddarbhapāṇinā 
sthāpayitvā tu caturaḥ kumbhānkoṇeṣu śobhanān  MatsP 
pañcamaṃ ca punarmadhye dadhyakṣatavibhūṣitam 
sthāpayedavraṇaṃ kumbhaṃ saptarcenābhimantritam  MatsP 
saureṇa tīrthatoyena pūrṇaṃ ratnasamanvitam

pañcaratnaphalaiḥ puṣpair vāsobhiḥ pariveṣṭayet  MatsP 
gajāśvarathyāvalmīkāt saṃgamāddhradagokulāt 
saṃśuddhāṃ mṛdamānīya sarveṣveva vinikṣipet  MatsP 
caturṣvapi ca kumbheṣu ratnagarbheṣu madhyamam 
gṛhītvā brāhmaṇastatra saurānmantrānudīrayet  MatsP 
nārībhiḥ saptasaṃkhyābhir avyaṅgāṅgībhiratra ca 
pūjitābhiryathāśaktyā mālyavastravibhūṣaṇaiḥ 
saviprābhiśca kartavyaṃ mṛtavatsābhiṣecanam  MatsP 
ete 'bhiṣekamantrāḥ
dīrghāyurastu bālo 'yaṃ jīvatputrā ca bhāminī 
ādityaścandramāḥ sārdhaṃ grahanakṣatramaṇḍalaiḥ  MatsP 
saśakrā lokapālā vai brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ 
te te cānye ca devaughāḥ sadā pāntu kumārakam  MatsP 
mitraḥ śanirvā hutabhug ye ca bālagrahāḥ kvacit 
pīḍāṃ kurvantu bālasya mā māturjanakasya vai  MatsP 
tataḥ śuklāmbaradharā kumārapatisaṃyutā 
saptakaṃ pūjayedbhaktyā strīṇāmatha guruṃ punaḥ  MatsP 
kāñcanīṃ ca tataḥ kuryāt tāmrapātroparisthitām 
pratimāṃ dharmarājasya gurave vinivedayet  MatsP 
vastrakāñcanaratnaughair bhakṣyaiḥ saghṛtapāyasaiḥ 
pūjayedbrāhmaṇāṃstadvad vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ  MatsP 
bhuktvā ca guruṇā ceyam uccāryā mantrasaṃtatiḥ 
dīrghāyurastu bālo 'yaṃ yāvadvarṣaśataṃ sukhī  MatsP 
yatkiṃcidasya duritaṃ tatkṣiptaṃ vaḍavānale 
brahmā rudro vasuḥ skando viṣṇuḥ śakro hutāśanaḥ  MatsP 
rakṣantu sarve duṣṭebhyo varadāḥ santu sarvadā 
evamādīni vākyāni vadantaṃ pūjayedgurum  MatsP 
śaktitaḥ kapilāṃ dadyāt praṇamya ca visarjayet 
caruṃ ca putrasahitā praṇamya raviśaṃkarau  MatsP 
hutaśeṣaṃ tadāśnīyād ādityāya namo 'stviti 
idamevādbhutodvegaduḥsvapneṣu praśasyate  MatsP 
karturjanmadinarkṣaṃ ca tyaktvā sampūjayetsadā

sadānena vidhānena dīrghāyurabhavannaraḥ

kathayitvā dvijaśreṣṭha tatraivāntaradhīyata  MatsP

īśvara uvāca
asmādrathaṃtarātkalpāt trayoviṃśāt punaryadā 
vārāho bhavitā kalpas tasya manvantare śubhe  MatsP 
vaivasvatākhye saṃjāte saptame saptalokakṛt 
dvāparākhyaṃ yugaṃ tadvad aṣṭāviṃśatimaṃ jaguḥ  MatsP 
tasyānte sa mahādevo vāsudevo janārdanaḥ 
bhārāvataraṇārthāya tridhā viṣṇurbhaviṣyati  MatsP 
dvaipāyana ṛṣistadvad rauhiṇeyo 'tha keśavaḥ 
kaṃsādidarpamathanaḥ keśavaḥ kleśanāśanaḥ  MatsP 
purīṃ dvāravatīṃ nāma sāmprataṃ yā kuśasthalī 
divyānubhāvasaṃyuktām adhivāsāya śārṅgiṇaḥ 
tvaṣṭā mamājñayā tadvat kariṣyati jagatpateḥ  MatsP 
tasyāṃ kadācidāsīnaḥ sabhāyāmamitadyutiḥ 
bhāryābhirvṛṣṇibhiścaiva bhūbhṛdbhir bhūridakṣiṇaiḥ  MatsP 
kurubhirdevagandharvair abhitaḥ kaiṭabhārdanaḥ 
pravṛttāsu purāṇīṣu dharmasambandhinīṣu ca  MatsP 
kathānte bhīmasenena paripṛṣṭaḥ pratāpavān 
tvayā pṛṣṭasya dharmasya rahasyasyāsya bhedakṛt  MatsP 
bhavitā sa tadā brahman kartā caiva vṛkodaraḥ 
pravartako 'sya dharmasya pāṇḍuputro mahābalaḥ  MatsP 
yasya tīkṣṇo vṛko nāma jaṭhare havyavāhanaḥ 
mayā dattaḥ sa dharmātmā tena cāsau vṛkodaraḥ  MatsP 
matimānmānaśīlaśca nāgāyutabalo mahān 
bhaviṣyatyajaraḥ śrīmān kandarpa iva rūpavān  MatsP 
dhārmikasyāpyaśaktasya tīvrāgnitvādupoṣaṇe 
idaṃ vratamaśeṣāṇāṃ vratānāmadhikaṃ yataḥ  MatsP 
kathayiṣyati viśvātmā vāsudevo jagadguruḥ 
aśeṣayajñaphaladam aśeṣāghavināśanam  MatsP 
aśeṣaduṣṭaśamanam aśeṣasurapūjitam 
pavitrāṇāṃ pavitraṃ ca maṅgalānāṃ ca maṅgalam 
bhaviṣyaṃ ca bhaviṣyāṇāṃ purāṇānāṃ purātanam  MatsP 
vāsudeva uvāca
yadyaṣṭamīcaturdaśyor dvādaśīṣvatha bhārata 
anyeṣvapi dinarkṣeṣu na śaktastvam upoṣitum  MatsP 
tataḥ puṇyāṃ tithimimāṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśinīm 
upoṣya vidhinānena gaccha viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam  MatsP 
māghamāsasya daśamī yadā śuklā bhavettadā 
ghṛtenābhyañjanaṃ kṛtvā tilaiḥ snānaṃ samācaret  MatsP 
tathaiva viṣṇumabhyarcya nabho nārāyaṇeti ca 
kṛṣṇāya pādau sampūjya śiraḥ sarvātmane namaḥ  MatsP 
vaikuṇṭhāyeti vaikuṇṭham uraḥ śrīvatsadhāriṇe 
śaṅkhine cakriṇe tadvad gadine varadāya vai 
sarve nārāyaṇasyaivaṃ saṃpūjyā bāhavaḥ kramāt  MatsP 
dāmodarāyetyudaraṃ meḍhraṃ pañcaśarāya vai 
ūrū saubhāgyanāthāya jānunī bhūtadhāriṇe  MatsP 
namo nīlāya vai jaṅghe pādau viśvasṛje namaḥ 
namo devyai namaḥ śāntyai namo lakṣmyai namaḥ śriyai  MatsP 
namaḥ puṣṭyai namastuṣṭyai dhṛṣṭyai hṛṣṭyai namo namaḥ 
namo vihaṃganāthāya vāyuvegāya pakṣiṇe 
viṣapramāthine nityaṃ garuḍaṃ cābhipūjayet  MatsP 
evaṃ sampūjya govindam umāpativināyakau 
gandhairmālyaistathā dhūpair bhakṣyairnānāvidhairapi  MatsP 
gavyena payasā siddhāṃ kṛsarāmatha vāgyataḥ 
sarpiṣā saha bhuktvā ca gatvā śatapadaṃ budhaḥ  MatsP 
naiyagrodhaṃ dantakāṣṭham athavā khādiraṃ budhaḥ 
gṛhītvā dhāvayeddantān ācāntaḥ prāgudaṅmukhaḥ  MatsP 
brūyāt sāyantanīṃ kṛtvā saṃdhyāmastamite ravau 
namo nārāyaṇāyeti tvāmahaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  MatsP 
ekādaśyāṃ nirāhāraḥ samabhyarcya ca keśavam 
rātriṃ ca sakalāṃ sthitvā snānaṃ ca payasā tathā  MatsP 
sarpiṣā cāpi dahanaṃ hutvā brāhmaṇapuṃgavaiḥ 
sahaiva puṇḍarīkākṣa dvādaśyāṃ kṣīrabhojanam  MatsP 
kariṣyāmi yatātmāhaṃ nirvighnenāstu tacca me 
evamuktvā svapedbhūmāv itihāsakathāṃ punaḥ  MatsP 
śrutvā prabhāte saṃjāte nadīṃ gatvā viśāṃ pate 
snānaṃ kṛtvā mṛdā tadvat pāṣaṇḍān abhivarjayet  MatsP 
upāsya saṃdhyāṃ vidhivat kṛtvā ca pitṛtarpaṇam 
praṇamya ca hṛṣīkeśaṃ saptalokaikamīśvaram  MatsP 
gṛhasya purato bhaktyā maṇḍapaṃ kārayedbudhaḥ 
daśahastamathāṣṭau vā karānkuryādviśāṃ pate  MatsP 
caturhastāṃ śubhāṃ kuryād vedīmariniṣūdana 
caturhastapramāṇaṃ ca vinyasettatra toraṇam  MatsP 
āropya kalaśaṃ tatra dikpālānpūjayettataḥ 
chidreṇa jalasampūrṇam atha kṛṣṇājinasthitaḥ 
tasya dhārāṃ ca śirasā dhārayetsakalāṃ niśām  MatsP 
tathaiva viṣṇoḥ śirasi kṣīradhārāṃ prapātayet 
aratnimātraṃ kuṇḍaṃ ca kuryāttatra trimekhalam  MatsP 
yonivaktraṃ ca tatkṛtvā brāhmaṇaiḥ yavasarpiṣī 
tilāṃśca viṣṇudevatyair mantrairekāgnivattadā  MatsP 
hutvā ca vaiṣṇavaṃ samyak caruṃ gokṣīrasaṃyutam 
niṣpāvārdhapramāṇāṃ vai dhārāmājyasya pātayet  MatsP 
jalakumbhānmahāvīrya sthāpayitvā trayodaśa 
bhakṣyairnānāvidhairyuktān sitavastrairalaṃkṛtān  MatsP 
yuktānaudumbaraiḥ pātraiḥ pañcaratnasamanvitān 
caturbhirbahvṛcairhomas tatra kārya udaṅmukhaiḥ  MatsP 
rudrajāpaścaturbhiśca yajurvedaparāyaṇaiḥ 
vaiṣṇavāni tu sāmāni caturaḥ sāmavedinaḥ 
ariṣṭavargasahitāny abhitaḥ paripāṭhayet  MatsP 
evaṃ dvādaśa tānviprān vastramālyānulepanaiḥ 
pūjayedaṅgulīyaiśca kaṭakairhemasūtrakaiḥ  MatsP 
vāsobhiḥ śayanīyaiśca vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ 
evaṃ kṣapātivāhyā ca gītamaṅgalaniḥsvanaiḥ  MatsP 
upādhyāyasya ca punar dviguṇaṃ sarvameva tu 
tataḥ prabhāte vimale samutthāya trayodaśa  MatsP 
gā vai dadyātkuruśreṣṭha sauvarṇamukhasaṃyutāḥ 
payasvinīḥ śīlavatīḥ kāṃsyadohasamanvitāḥ  MatsP 
raupyakhurāḥ savastrāśca candanenābhiṣecitāḥ 
tāstu teṣāṃ tato bhaktyā bhakṣyabhojyānnatarpitān  MatsP 
kṛtvā vai brāhmaṇān sarvān annairnānāvidhaistathā 
bhuktvā cākṣāralavaṇam ātmanā ca visarjayet  MatsP 
anugamya padānyaṣṭau putrabhāryāsamanvitaḥ 
prīyatāmatra deveśaḥ keśavaḥ kleśanāśanaḥ  MatsP 
śivasya hṛdaye viṣṇur viṣṇośca hṛdaye śivaḥ 
yathāntaraṃ na paśyāmi tathā me svasti cāyuṣaḥ  MatsP 
evamuccārya tānkumbhān gāścaiva śayanāni ca 
vāsāṃsi caiva sarveṣāṃ gṛhāṇi prāpayedbudhaḥ  MatsP 
abhāve bahuśayyānām ekāmapi susaṃskṛtām 
śayyāṃ dadyāddvijāteśca sarvopaskarasaṃyutām  MatsP 
itihāsapurāṇāni vācayitvātivāhayet 
taddinaṃ naraśārdūla ya icchedvipulāṃ śriyam  MatsP 
tasmāttvaṃ sattvamālambya bhīmasena vimatsaraḥ 
kuru vratamidaṃ samyak snehāttava mayeritam  MatsP 
tvayā kṛtamidaṃ vīra tvannāmākhyaṃ bhaviṣyati 
sā bhīmadvādaśī hyeṣā sarvapāpaharā śubhā 
yā tu kalyāṇinī nāma purā kalpeṣu paṭhyate  MatsP 
tvamādikartā bhava saukare 'smin kalpe mahāvīravarapradhāna 
yasyāḥ smarankīrtanamapyaśeṣaṃ vinaṣṭapāpastridaśādhipaḥ syāt  MatsP 
kṛtvā ca yāmapsarasām adhīśā veśyā kṛtā hyanyabhavāntareṣu 
ābhīrakanyātikutūhalena saivorvaśī samprati nākapṛṣṭhe  MatsP 
jātāthavā vaiśyakulodbhavāpi pulomakanyā puruhūtapatnī 
tatrāpi tasyāḥ paricārikeyaṃ mama priyā samprati satyabhāmā  MatsP 
snātaḥ purā maṇḍalameṣa tadvat tejomayaṃ vedaśarīramāpa 
asyāṃ ca kalyāṇatithau vivasvān sahasradhāreṇa sahasraraśmiḥ  MatsP 
idameva kṛtaṃ mahendramukhyair vasubhirdevasurāribhistathā tu 
phalamasya na śakyate 'bhivaktuṃ yadi jihvāyutakoṭayo mukhe syuḥ  MatsP 
kalikaluṣavidāriṇīmanantām iti kathayiṣyati yādavendrasūnuḥ 
api narakagatānpitṝn aśeṣān alamuddhartumihaiva yaḥ karoti  MatsP 
ya idamaghavidāraṇaṃ śṛṇoti bhaktyā paripaṭhatīha paropakārahetoḥ 
tithimiha sakalārthabhāṅnarendras tava caturānana sāmyatāmupaiti  MatsP 
kalyāṇinī nāma purā babhūva yā dvādaśī māghadineṣu pūjyā 
sā pāṇḍuputreṇa kṛtā bhaviṣyaty anantapuṇyānagha bhīmapūrvā  MatsP

īśvara uvāca
tasminneva yuge brahman sahasrāṇi tu ṣoḍaśa 
vāsudevasya nārīṇāṃ bhaviṣyantyambujodbhava  MatsP

gacchansamīpamārgeṇa sāmbaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ

matparokṣaṃ yataḥ kāmalaulyādīdṛgvidhaṃ kṛtam  MatsP 
tataḥ prasādito deva idaṃ vakṣyati śārṅgabhṛt 
tābhiḥ śāpābhitaptābhir bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ  MatsP 
uttārabhūtaṃ dāsatvaṃ samudrādbrāhmaṇapriyaḥ 
upadekṣyatyanantātmā bhāvikalyāṇakārakam  MatsP

tataḥ kālena mahatā bhārāvataraṇe kṛte

śūnye yadukule sarvaiś caurairapi jite 'rjune

āgamiṣyati yogātmā dālbhyo nāma mahātapāḥ  MatsP 
tāstamarghyeṇa sampūjya praṇipatya punaḥ punaḥ 
lālapyamānā bahuśo bāṣpaparyākulekṣaṇāḥ  MatsP

striya ūcuḥ

dālbhya uvāca
jalakrīḍāvihāreṣu purā sarasi mānase

kathaṃ nārāyaṇo 'smākaṃ bhartā syād ityupādiśa  MatsP

śayyādvayapradānena madhumādhavamāsayoḥ  MatsP

idānīmapi yadvakṣye tacchṛṇudhvaṃ varāṅganāḥ  MatsP 
dālbhya uvāca
purā devāsure yuddhe hateṣu śataśaḥ suraiḥ 
dānavāsuradaityeṣu rākṣaseṣu tatastataḥ  MatsP

indra uvāca
veśyādharmeṇa vartadhvam adhunā nṛpamandire 
bhaktimatyo varārohās tathā devakuleṣu ca  MatsP 
rājānaḥ svāminastulyāḥ sutā vāpi ca tatsamāḥ 
bhaviṣyati ca saubhāgyaṃ sarvāsāmapi śaktitaḥ  MatsP

nidhanenopacāryo vaḥ sa tadānyatra dāmbhikāt  MatsP 
devatānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca puṇyāhe samupasthite 
gobhūhiraṇyadhānyāni pradeyāni svaśaktitaḥ 
brāhmaṇānāṃ varārohāḥ kāryāṇi vacanāni ca  MatsP 
yaccāpyanyadvrataṃ samyag upadekṣyāmyahaṃ tataḥ 
avicāreṇa sarvābhir anuṣṭheyaṃ ca tatpunaḥ  MatsP

utkaṇṭhāyeti vaikuṇṭham āsyamānandakāriṇe

mānasāyeti vai mauliṃ vilolāyeti mūrdhajam 
sarvātmane ca sarvāṅgaṃ devadevasya pūjayet  MatsP

tasmai viprāya sā dadyān mādhavaḥ prīyatāmiti  MatsP

sapatnīkamalaṃkṛtya hemasūtrāṅgulīyakaiḥ

dadyādetena mantreṇa tathaikāṃ gāṃ payasvinīm  MatsP

ka idaṃ kasmā adāditi vaidikaṃ mantramīrayet  MatsP 
tataḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya visarjya dvijapuṃgavam

tataḥ prabhṛti yo vipro ratyarthaṃ gṛhamāgataḥ

sācārānaṣṭapañcāśad yathāśaktyā samācaret  MatsP

śrībhagavānuvāca
śrāvaṇasya dvitīyāyāṃ kṛṣṇāyāṃ madhusūdanaḥ 
kṣīrārṇave sapatnīkaḥ sadā vasati keśavaḥ  MatsP

aśūnyaśayanaṃ nāma dvitīyā saṃprakīrtitā 
tasyāṃ sampūjayedviṣṇum ebhirmantrairvidhānataḥ  MatsP 
śrīvatsadhāriñchrīkānta śrīdhāmañchrīpate 'vyaya 
gārhasthyaṃ mā praṇāśaṃ me yātu dharmārthakāmadam  MatsP 
agnayo mā praṇaśyantu devatāḥ puruṣottama 
pitaro mā praṇaśyantu māstu dāmpatyabhedanam  MatsP

tathā kalatrasambandho deva mā me viyujyatām  MatsP 
lakṣmyā na śūnyo varada śayyāṃ tvaṃ śayanaṃ gataḥ 
śayyā mamāpyaśūnyāstu tathaiva madhusūdana  MatsP 
gītavāditranirghoṣaṃ devadevasya kīrtayet 
ghaṇṭā bhavedaśaktasya sarvavādyamayī yataḥ  MatsP 
evaṃ sampūjya govindam aśnīyāttailavarjitam 
naktamakṣāralavaṇaṃ yāvattatsyāccatuṣṭayam  MatsP 
tataḥ prabhāte saṃjāte lakṣmīpatisamanvitām

pādukopānahacchattracāmarāsanasaṃyutām

sopadhānakaviśrāmāṃ phalairnānāvidhairyutām 
tathābharaṇadhānyaiśca yathāśaktyā samanvitām  MatsP 
avyaṅgāṅgāya viprāya vaiṣṇavāya kuṭumbine 
dātavyā vedaviduṣe bhāvenāpatitāya ca  MatsP 
tatropaviśya dāmpatyam alaṃkṛtya vidhānataḥ 
patnyāstu bhājanaṃ dadyād bhakṣyabhojyasamanvitam  MatsP 
brāhmaṇasyāpi sauvarṇīm upaskarasamanvitām 
pratimāṃ devadevasya sodakumbhāṃ nivedayet  MatsP 
evaṃ yastu pumānkuryād aśūnyaśayanaṃ hareḥ 
vittaśāṭhyena rahito nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ  MatsP 
na tasya patnyā virahaḥ kadācidapi jāyate 
nārī vā vidhavā brahman yāvaccandrārkatārakam 
na virūpau na śokārtau dampatī bhavataḥ kvacit  MatsP 
na putrapaśuratnāni kṣayaṃ yānti pitāmaha 
sapta kalpasahasrāṇi sapta kalpaśatāni ca 
kurvannaśūnyaśayanaṃ viṣṇuloke mahīyate  MatsP

īśvara uvāca
śṛṇu cānyadbhaviṣyaṃ yad rūpasampadvidhāyakam 
bhaviṣyati yuge tasmin dvāparānte pitāmaha 
pippalādasya saṃvādo yudhiṣṭhirapuraḥsaraiḥ  MatsP 
vasantaṃ naimiṣāraṇye pippalādaṃ mahāmunim 
abhigamya tadā cainaṃ praśnamekaṃ kariṣyati 
yudhiṣṭhiro dharmaputro dharmayuktastapodhanam  MatsP 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca

avyaṅgatā śive bhaktir vaiṣṇavo vā bhavetkatham  MatsP 
īśvara uvāca
tasyottaramidaṃ brahman pippalādasya dhīmataḥ 
śṛṇuṣva yadvakṣyati vai dharmaputrāya dhārmikaḥ  MatsP 
pippalāda uvāca
sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā bhadra idānīṃ kathayāmi te 
aṅgāravratam ityetat sa vakṣyati mahīpateḥ  MatsP 
atrāpyudāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam 
virocanasya saṃvādaṃ bhārgavasya ca dhīmataḥ  MatsP 
prahlādasya sutaṃ dṛṣṭvā dviraṣṭaparivatsaram 
rūpeṇāpratimaṃ kāntyā so 'hasadbhṛgunandanaḥ  MatsP 
sādhu sādhu mahābāho virocana śivaṃ tava 
tattathā hasitaṃ tasya papraccha surasūdanaḥ  MatsP 
brahmankimarthametatte hāsyamākasmikaṃ kṛtam 
sādhusādhviti māmevam uktavāṃstvaṃ vadasva me  MatsP 
tamevaṃvādinaṃ śukra uvāca vadatāṃ varaḥ 
vismayādvratamāhātmyād dhāsyametatkṛtaṃ mayā  MatsP 
purā dakṣavināśāya kupitasya tu śūlinaḥ 
atha tadbhīmavaktrasya svedabindurlalāṭajaḥ  MatsP 
bhittvā sa sapta pātālān adahatsapta sāgarān 
anekavaktranayano jvalajjvalanabhīṣaṇaḥ  MatsP 
vīrabhadra iti khyātaḥ karapādāyutairyutaḥ 
kṛtvāsau yajñamathanaṃ punarbhūtalasambhavaḥ 
trijagannirdahanbhūyaḥ śivena vinivāritaḥ  MatsP 
kṛtaṃ tvayā vīrabhadra dakṣayajñavināśanam 
idānīmalametena lokadāhena karmaṇā  MatsP 
śāntipradātā sarveṣāṃ grahāṇāṃ prathamo bhava 
prekṣiṣyante janāḥ pūjāṃ kariṣyanti varānmama  MatsP 
aṅgāraka iti khyātiṃ gamiṣyasi dharātmaja 
devaloke 'dvitīyaṃ ca tava rūpaṃ bhaviṣyati  MatsP 
ye ca tvāṃ pūjayiṣyanti caturthyāṃ tvaddine narāḥ 
rūpamārogyamaiśvaryaṃ teṣvanantaṃ bhaviṣyati  MatsP 
evamuktastadā śāntim agamat kāmarūpadhṛk 
saṃjātastatkṣaṇādrājan grahatvam agamatpunaḥ  MatsP 
sa kadācidbhavāṃstasya pūjārghyādikamuttamam 
dṛṣṭavānkriyamāṇaṃ ca śūdreṇa ca vyavasthitaḥ  MatsP 
tena tvaṃ rūpavāñjātaḥ suraśatrukulodvaha 
vividhā ca rucirjātā yasmāttava vidūragā  MatsP 
virocana iti prāhus tasmāttvāṃ devadānavāḥ 
śūdreṇa kriyamāṇasya vratasya tava darśanāt 
īdṛśīṃ rūpasampattiṃ dṛṣṭvā vismitavānaham  MatsP 
sādhu sādhviti tenoktam aho māhātmyamuttamam 
paśyato 'pi bhavedrūpam aiśvaryaṃ kimu kurvataḥ  MatsP 
yasmācca bhaktyā dharaṇīsutasya vinindyamānena gavādidānam 
ālokitaṃ tena surārigarbhe sambhūtireṣā tava daitya jātā  MatsP 
īśvara uvāca
atha tadvacanaṃ śrutvā bhārgavasya mahātmanaḥ 
prahrādanandano vīraḥ punaḥ papraccha vismitaḥ  MatsP 
virocana uvāca
bhagavaṃstadvrataṃ samyak śrotumicchāmi tattvataḥ 
dīyamānaṃ tu yaddānaṃ mayā dṛṣṭaṃ bhavāntare  MatsP 
māhātmyaṃ ca vidhiṃ tasya yathāvadvaktumarhasi 
iti tadvacanaṃ śrutvā punaḥ provāca vistarāt  MatsP 
śukra uvāca
caturthyaṅgārakadine yadā bhavati dānava 
mṛdā snānaṃ tadā kuryāt padmarāgavibhūṣitaḥ  MatsP 
agnirmūrdhā divo mantraṃ japannāste udaṅmukhaḥ 
śūdrastūṣṇīṃ smaranbhaumam āste bhogavivarjitaḥ  MatsP 
tathāstamita āditye gomayenānulepayet 
prāṅgaṇaṃ puṣpamālābhir akṣatābhiḥ samantataḥ  MatsP 
abhyarcyābhilikhetpadmaṃ kuṅkumenāṣṭapattrakam 
kuṅkumasyāpyabhāve tu raktacandanamiṣyate  MatsP 
catvāraḥ karakāḥ kāryā bhakṣyabhojyasamanvitāḥ 
taṇḍulai raktaśālīyaiḥ padmarāgaiśca saṃyutāḥ  MatsP 
catuṣkoṇeṣu tānkṛtvā phalāni vividhāni ca 
gandhamālyādikaṃ sarvaṃ tathaiva vinivedayet  MatsP 
suvarṇaśṛṅgīṃ kapilām athārcya raupyaiḥ suraiḥ kāṃsyadohāṃ savatsām 
dhuraṃdharaṃ raktamatīva saumyaṃ dhānyāni saptāmbarasaṃyutāni  MatsP 
aṅguṣṭhamātraṃ puruṣaṃ tathaiva sauvarṇamatyāyatabāhudaṇḍam 
caturbhujaṃ hemamaye niviṣṭaṃ pātre guḍasyopari sarpiyukte  MatsP 
samastayajñāya jitendriyāya pātrāya śīlānvayasaṃyutāya 
dātavyametatsakalaṃ dvijāya kuṭumbine naiva tu dāmbhikāya 
samarpayedvipravarāya bhaktyā kṛtāñjaliḥ pūrvamudīrya mantram  MatsP 
bhūmiputra mahābhāga svedodbhava pinākinaḥ 
rūpārthī tvāṃ prapanno 'haṃ gṛhāṇārghyaṃ namo 'stu te  MatsP 
mantreṇānena dattvārghyaṃ raktacandanavāriṇā 
tato 'rcayedvipravaraṃ raktamālyāmbarādibhiḥ  MatsP 
dadyāttenaiva mantreṇa bhaumaṃ gomithunānvitam 
śayyāṃ ca śaktito dadyāt sarvopaskarasaṃyutām  MatsP 
yadyadiṣṭatamaṃ loke yaccāsya dayitaṃ gṛhe 
tattadguṇavate deyaṃ tadevākṣayyamicchatā  MatsP 
pradakṣiṇaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā visarjya dvijapuṃgavam 
naktamakṣāralavaṇam aśnīyādghṛtasaṃyutam  MatsP 
bhaktyā yastu punaḥ kuryād evamaṅgārakāṣṭakam 
caturo vātha vā tasya yatpuṇyaṃ tadvadāmi te  MatsP 
rūpasaubhāgyasampannaḥ punarjanmani janmani 
viṣṇau vātha śive bhaktaḥ saptadvīpādhipo bhavet  MatsP 
sapta kalpasahasrāṇi rudraloke mahīyate 
tasmāttvamapi daityendra vratametatsamācara  MatsP 
pippalāda uvāca
ityevamuktvā bhṛgunandano 'pi jagāma daityaśca cakāra sarvam 
tvaṃ cāpi rājankuru sarvametad yato 'kṣayaṃ vedavido vadanti  MatsP 
īśvara uvāca
tatheti sampūjya sa pippalādaṃ vākyaṃ cakārādbhutavīryakarmā 
śṛṇoti yaścainamananyacetās tasyāpi siddhiṃ bhagavānvidhatte  MatsP 
MatsyaPurāṇa 
pippalāda uvāca
athātaḥ śṛṇu bhūpāla pratiśukraṃ praśāntaye 
yātrārambhe 'vasāne ca tathā śukrodaye tviha  MatsP 
rājate vātha sauvarṇe kāṃsyapātre 'thavā punaḥ 
śuklapuṣpāmbarayute sitataṇḍulapūrite  MatsP 
vidhāya rājataṃ śukraṃ śucimuktāphalānvitam 
mantreṇānena tatsarvaṃ sāmagāya nivedayet  MatsP 
namaste sarvalokeśa namaste bhṛgunandana 
kave sarvārthasiddhyarthaṃ gṛhāṇārghyaṃ namo 'stu te  MatsP 
evamasyodaye kurvan yātrādiṣu ca bhārata 
sarvānkāmānavāpnoti viṣṇuloke mahīyate  MatsP 
yāvacchukrasya na hṛtā pūjā sā mālyakaiḥ śubhaiḥ 
vaṭakaiḥ pūrikābhiśca godhūmaiścaṇakairapi 
tāvadannaṃ na cāśnīyāt tribhiḥ kāmārthasiddhaye  MatsP 
tadvadvācaspateḥ pūjāṃ pravakṣyāmi yudhiṣṭhira 
suvarṇapātre sauvarṇam amareśapurohitam  MatsP 
pītapuṣpāmbarayutaṃ kṛtvā snātvātha sarṣapaiḥ 
palāśāśvatthayogena pañcagavyajalena ca  MatsP 
pītāṅgarāgavasano ghṛtahomaṃ tu kārayet 
praṇamya ca gavā sārdhaṃ brāhmaṇāya nivedayet  MatsP 
namaste 'ṅgirasāṃ nātha vākpate ca bṛhaspate 
krūragrahaiḥ pīḍitānām amṛtāya namo namaḥ  MatsP 
saṃkrāntāvasya kaunteya yātrāsvabhyudayeṣu ca 
kurvanbṛhaspateḥ pūjāṃ sarvānkāmānsamaśnute  MatsP

brahmovāca
bhagavan bhavasaṃsārasāgarottārakāraka 
kiṃcidvrataṃ samācakṣva svargārogyasukhapradam  MatsP 
īśvara uvāca
sauraṃ dharmaṃ pravakṣyāmi nāmnā kalyāṇasaptamīm 
viśokasaptamīṃ tadvat phalāḍhyāṃ pāpanāśinīm  MatsP 
śarkarāsaptamīṃ puṇyāṃ tathā kamalasaptamīm 
mandārasaptamīṃ tadvac chubhadāṃ śubhasaptamīm  MatsP 
sarvānantaphalāḥ proktāḥ sarvā devarṣipūjitāḥ 
vidhānamāsāṃ vakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ  MatsP 
yadā tu śuklasaptamyām ādityasya dinaṃ bhavet 
sā tu kalyāṇinī nāma vijayā ca nigadyate  MatsP 
prātargavyena payasā snānamasyāṃ samācaret 
tataḥ śuklāmbaraḥ padmam akṣatābhiḥ prakalpayet  MatsP 
prāṅmukho 'ṣṭadalaṃ madhye tadvadvṛttāṃ ca karṇikām 
puṣpākṣatābhirdeveśaṃ vinyasetsarvataḥ kramāt  MatsP 
pūrveṇa tapanāyeti mārtaṇḍāyeti cānale 
yāmye divākarāyeti vidhātra iti nairṛte  MatsP 
paścime varuṇāyeti bhāskarāyeti cānile 
saumye vikartanāyeti ravaye cāṣṭame dale  MatsP 
ādāvante ca madhye ca namo 'stu paramātmane 
mantrairebhiḥ samabhyarcya namaskārāntadīpitaiḥ  MatsP 
śuklavastraiḥ phalairbhakṣyair dhūpamālyānulepanaiḥ 
sthaṇḍile pūjayedbhaktyā guḍena lavaṇena ca  MatsP 
tato vyāhṛtimantreṇa visṛjeddvijapuṃgavān 
śaktitaḥ pūjayedbhaktyā guḍakṣīraghṛtādibhiḥ 
tilapātraṃ hiraṇyaṃ ca brāhmaṇāya nivedayet  MatsP 
evaṃ niyamakṛtsuptvā prātarutthāya mānavaḥ 
kṛtasnānajapo vipraiḥ sahaiva ghṛtapāyasam  MatsP 
bhuktvā ca vedaviduṣe biḍālavratavarjite 
ghṛtapātraṃ sakanakaṃ sodakumbhaṃ nivedayet  MatsP 
prīyatāmatra bhagavān paramātmā divākaraḥ 
anena vidhinā sarvaṃ māsi māsi vrataṃ caret  MatsP 
tatastrayodaśe māsi gā vai dadyāttrayodaśa 
vastrālaṃkārasaṃyuktāḥ suvarṇāsyāḥ payasvinīḥ  MatsP 
ekāmapi pradadyādvā vittahīno vimatsaraḥ 
na vittaśāṭhyaṃ kurvīta yato mohātpatatyadhaḥ  MatsP 
anena vidhinā yastu kuryātkalyāṇasaptamīm 
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sūryaloke mahīyate 
āyurārogyamaiśvaryam anantamiha jāyate  MatsP 
sarvapāpaharā nityaṃ sarvadaivatapūjitā 
sarvaduṣṭopaśamanī sadā kalyāṇasaptamī  MatsP 
imāmanantaphaladāṃ yastu kalyāṇasaptamīm 
śṛṇoti paṭhate ceha sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  MatsP

īśvara uvāca
viśokasaptamīṃ tadvad vakṣyāmi munipuṃgava 
yāmupoṣya naraḥ śokaṃ na kadācidihāśnute  MatsP 
māghe kṛṣṇatilaiḥ snātvā ṣaṣṭhyāṃ vai śuklapakṣataḥ 
kṛtāhāraḥ kṛsarayā dantadhāvanapūrvakam 
upavāsavrataṃ kṛtvā brahmacārī bhavenniśi  MatsP 
tataḥ prabhāta utthāya kṛtasnānajapaḥ śuciḥ 
kṛtvā tu kāñcanaṃ padmam arkāyeti ca pūjayet 
karavīreṇa raktena raktavastrayugena ca  MatsP 
yathā viśokaṃ bhuvanaṃ tvayaivāditya sarvadā 
tathā viśokatā me 'stu tvadbhaktiḥ pratijanma ca  MatsP 
evaṃ sampūjya ṣaṣṭhyāṃ tu bhaktyā sampūjayeddvijān 
suptvā saṃprāśya gomūtram utthāya kṛtanaityakaḥ  MatsP 
sampūjya viprānannena guḍapātrasamanvitam 
tadvastrayugmaṃ padmaṃ ca brāhmaṇāya nivedayet  MatsP 
atailalavaṇaṃ bhuktvā saptamyāṃ maunasaṃyutaḥ 
tataḥ purāṇaśravaṇaṃ kartavyaṃ bhūtimicchatā  MatsP 
anena vidhinā sarvam ubhayorapi pakṣayoḥ 
kṛtvā yāvatpunarmāghaśuklapakṣasya saptamī  MatsP 
vratānte kalaśaṃ dadyāt suvarṇakamalānvitam 
śayyāṃ sopaskarāṃ dadyāt kapilāṃ ca payasvinīm  MatsP 
anena vidhinā yastu vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ 
viśokasaptamīṃ kuryāt sa yāti paramāṃ gatim  MatsP 
yāvajjanmasahasrāṇāṃ sāgraṃ koṭiśataṃ bhavet 
tāvanna śokamabhyeti rogadaurgatyavarjitaḥ  MatsP 
yaṃ yaṃ prārthayate kāmaṃ taṃ tamāpnoti puṣkalam 
niṣkāmaḥ kurute yastu sa paraṃ brahma gacchati  MatsP 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi viśokākhyāṃ ca saptamīm 
so 'pīndralokamāpnoti na duḥkhī jāyate kvacit  MatsP

īśvara uvāca
anyāmapi pravakṣyāmi nāmnā tu phalasaptamīm 
yāmupoṣya naraḥ pāpād vimuktaḥ svargabhāgbhavet  MatsP 
mārgaśīrṣe śubhe māsi saptamyāṃ niyatavrataḥ 
tāmupoṣyātha kamalaṃ kārayitvā tu kāñcanam  MatsP 
śarkarāsaṃyutaṃ dadyād brāhmaṇāya kuṭumbine 
raviṃ kāñcanakaṃ kṛtvā palasyaikasya dharmavit 
dadyāddvikālavelāyāṃ bhānurme prīyatāmiti  MatsP 
bhaktyā tu viprānsampūjya cāṣṭamyāṃ kṣīrabhojanam 
dattvā kuryātphalayutaṃ yāvatsyātkṛṣṇesaptamī  MatsP 
tāmapyupoṣya vidhivad anenaiva krameṇa tu 
tadvaddhaimaphalaṃ dattvā suvarṇakamalānvitam  MatsP 
śarkarāpātrasaṃyuktaṃ vastramālyasamanvitam 
saṃvatsaraṃ ca tenaiva vidhinobhayasaptamīm  MatsP 
upoṣya dattvā kramaśaḥ sūryamantramudīrayet 
bhānurarko ravirbrahmā sūryaḥ śakro hariḥ śivaḥ 
śrīmānvibhāvasustvaṣṭā varuṇaḥ prīyatāmiti  MatsP 
pratimāsaṃ ca saptamyām ekaikaṃ nāma kīrtayet 
pratipakṣaṃ phalatyāgam etatkurvansamācaret  MatsP 
vratānte vipramithunaṃ pūjayedvastrabhūṣaṇaiḥ 
śarkarākalaśaṃ dadyād dhemapadmadalānvitam  MatsP 
yathā na viphalāḥ kāmās tvadbhaktānāṃ sadā rave 
tathānantaphalāvāptir astu me saptajanmasu  MatsP 
imāmanantaphaladāṃ yaḥ kuryātphalasaptamīm 
sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā sūryaloke mahīyate  MatsP 
surāpānādikaṃ kiṃcid yadatrāmutra vā kṛtam 
tatsarvaṃ nāśamāyāti yaḥ kuryātphalasaptamīm  MatsP 
kurvāṇaḥ saptamīṃ cemāṃ satataṃ rogavarjitaḥ 
bhūtānbhavyāṃśca puruṣāṃs tārayedekaviṃśatim 
yaḥ śṛṇoti paṭhedvāpi so 'pi kalyāṇabhāgbhavet  MatsP

īśvara uvāca
śarkarāsaptamīṃ vakṣye tadvatkalmaṣanāśinīm 
āyurārogyamaiśvaryaṃ yayānantaṃ prajāyate  MatsP 
mādhavasya site pakṣe saptamyāṃ niyatavrataḥ 
prātaḥ snātvā tilaiḥ śuklaiḥ śuklamālyānulepanaḥ  MatsP 
sthaṇḍile padmamālikhya kuṅkumena sakarṇikam 
tasminnamaḥ savitre tu gandhadhūpau nivedayet  MatsP 
sthāpayedudakumbhaṃ ca śarkarāpātrasaṃyutam 
śuklavastrairalaṃkṛtya śuklamālyānulepanaiḥ 
suvarṇena samāyuktaṃ mantreṇānena pūjayet  MatsP 
viśvavedamayo yasmād vedavādīti paṭhyase 
sarvasyāmṛtameva tvam ataḥ śāntiṃ prayaccha me  MatsP 
pañcagavyaṃ tataḥ pītvā svapettatpārśvataḥ kṣitau 
saurasūktaṃ smarannāste purāṇaśravaṇena ca  MatsP 
ahorātre gate paścād aṣṭamyāṃ kṛtanaityakaḥ 
tatsarvaṃ viduṣe tadvad brāhmaṇāya nivedayet  MatsP 
bhojayecchaktito viprāñ charkarāghṛtapāyasaiḥ 
bhuñjītātailalavaṇaṃ svayamapyatha vāgyataḥ  MatsP 
anena vidhinā sarvaṃ māsi māsi samācaret 
saṃvatsarānte śayanaṃ śarkarākalaśānvitam  MatsP 
sarvopaskarasaṃyuktaṃ tathaikāṃ gāṃ payasvinīm 
gṛhaṃ ca śaktimāndadyāt samastopaskarānvitam  MatsP 
sahasreṇātha niṣkāṇāṃ kṛtvā dadyācchatena vā 
daśabhirvātha niṣkeṇa tadardhenāpi śaktitaḥ  MatsP 
suvarṇāśvaḥ pradātavyaḥ pūrvavanmantravādanam 
na vittaśāṭhyaṃ kurvīta kurvandoṣaṃ samaśnute  MatsP 
amṛtaṃ pibato vaktrāt sūryasyāmṛtabindavaḥ 
nipeturye dharaṇyāṃ tu śālimudgekṣavaḥ smṛtāḥ  MatsP 
śarkarā tu parā tasmād ikṣusāro 'mṛtātmavān 
iṣṭā raverataḥ puṇyā śarkarā havyakavyayoḥ  MatsP 
śarkarāsaptamī ceyaṃ vājimedhaphalapradā 
sarvaduṣṭapraśamanī putrapautrapravardhinī  MatsP 
yaḥ kuryātparayā bhaktyā sa vai sadgatimāpnuyāt 
kalpamekaṃ vasetsvarge tato yāti paraṃ padam  MatsP 
idamanaghaṃ śṛṇoti yaḥ smaredvā paripaṭhatīha divākarasya loke 
matimapi ca dadāti so 'pi devair amaravadhūjanamālayābhipūjyaḥ  MatsP

īśvara uvāca
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi tadvatkamalasaptamīm 
yasyāḥ saṃkīrtanādeva tuṣyatīha divākaraḥ  MatsP 
vasantāmalasaptamyāṃ snātaḥ sangaurasarṣapaiḥ 
tilapātre ca sauvarṇe vidhāya kamalaṃ śubham  MatsP 
vastrayugmāvṛtaṃ kṛtvā gandhapuṣpaiḥ samarcayet 
namaḥ kamalahastāya namaste viśvadhāriṇe  MatsP 
divākara namastubhyaṃ prabhākara namo 'stu te 
tato dvikālavelāyām udakumbhasamanvitām  MatsP 
viprāya dadyātsampūjya vastramālyavibhūṣaṇaiḥ 
śaktyā ca kapilāṃ dadyād alaṃkṛtya vidhānataḥ  MatsP 
ahorātre gate paścād aṣṭamyāṃ bhojayeddvijān 
yathāśaktyatha bhuñjīta māṃsatailavivarjitam  MatsP 
anena vidhinā śuklasaptamyāṃ māsi māsi ca 
sarvaṃ samācaredbhaktyā vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ  MatsP 
vratānte śayanaṃ dadyāt suvarṇakamalānvitam 
gāṃ ca dadyātsvaśaktyā tu suvarṇāḍhyāṃ payasvinīm  MatsP 
bhājanāsanadīpādīn dadyād iṣṭānupaskarān 
anena vidhinā yastu kuryātkamalasaptamīm 
lakṣmīmanantāmabhyeti sūryaloke mahīyate  MatsP 
kalpe kalpe tato lokān saptagatvā pṛthakpṛthak 
apsarobhiḥ parivṛtas tato yāti parāṃ gatim  MatsP 
yaḥ paśyatīdaṃ śṛṇuyācca martyaḥ paṭhecca bhaktyātha matiṃ dadāti 
so 'pyatra lakṣmīmacalāmavāpya gandharvavidyādharalokabhāksyāt  MatsP

īśvara uvāca
athātaḥ sampravakṣyāmi sarvapāpapraṇāśinīm 
sarvakāmapradāṃ ramyāṃ nāmnā mandārasaptamīm  MatsP 
māghasyāmalapakṣe tu pañcamyāṃ laghubhuṅnaraḥ 
dantakāṣṭhaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā ṣaṣṭhīmupavasedbudhaḥ  MatsP 
viprān sampūjayitvā tu mandāraṃ prāśayenniśi 
tataḥ prabhāta utthāya kṛtvā snānaṃ punardvijān  MatsP 
bhojayecchaktitaḥ kṛtvā mandārakusumāṣṭakam 
sauvarṇaṃ puruṣaṃ tadvat padmahastaṃ suśobhanam  MatsP 
padmaṃ kṛṣṇatilaiḥ kṛtvā tāmrapātre 'ṣṭapattrakam 
haimamandārakusumair bhāskarāyeti pūrvataḥ  MatsP 
namaskāreṇa tadvacca sūryāyetyānale dale 
dakṣiṇe tadvadarkāya tathāryamṇe ca nairṛte  MatsP 
paścime vedadhāmne ca vāyavye caṇḍabhānave 
pūṣṇetyuttarataḥ pūjyam ānandāyetyataḥ param  MatsP 
karṇikāyāṃ ca puruṣaṃ sarvātmana iti nyaset 
śuklavastraiḥ samāveṣṭya bhakṣyairmālyaphalādibhiḥ  MatsP 
evamabhyarcya tatsarvaṃ dadyādvedavide punaḥ 
bhuñjītātailalavaṇaṃ vāgyataḥ prāṅmukho gṛhī  MatsP 
anena vidhinā sarvaṃ saptamyāṃ māsi māsi ca 
kuryātsaṃvatsaraṃ yāvad vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ  MatsP 
etadeva vratānte tu nidhāya kalaśopari 
gobhirvibhavataḥ sārdhaṃ dātavyaṃ bhūtimicchatā  MatsP 
namo mandāranāthāya mandārabhavanāya ca 
tvaṃ rave tārayasvāsmān saṃsārabhayasāgarāt  MatsP 
anena vidhinā yastu kuryānmandārasaptamīm 
vipāpmā sa sukhī martyaḥ kalpaṃ ca divi modate  MatsP

vācayitvā tato viprān ārabhecchubhasaptamīm  MatsP

namāmi sūryasambhūtām aśeṣabhuvanālayām 
tvāmahaṃ śubhakalyāṇaśarīrāṃ sarvasiddhaye  MatsP 
atha kṛtvā tilaprasthaṃ tāmrapātreṇa saṃyutam

dadyāddvikālavelāyām aryamā prīyatāmiti  MatsP

tataḥ prabhāte saṃjāte bhaktyā sampūjayeddvijān  MatsP 
anena vidhinā dadyān māsi māsi sadā naraḥ

sopadhānakaviśrāmaṃ bhājanāsanasaṃyutam  MatsP 
tāmrapātre tilaprasthaṃ sauvarṇaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ tathā 
dadyādvedavide sarvaṃ viśvātmā prīyatāmiti  MatsP 
anena vidhinā vidvān kuryādyaḥ śubhasaptamīm 
tasya śrīrvipulā kīrtir bhavejjanmani janmani  MatsP 
apsarogaṇagandharvaiḥ pūjyamānaḥ surālaye

kalpādāvavatīrṇastu saptadvīpādhipo bhavet  MatsP

nāśāyālamiyaṃ puṇyā paṭhyate śubhasaptamī  MatsP 
imāṃ paṭhedyaḥ śṛṇuyānmuhūrtaṃ paśyetprasaṅgādapi dīyamānam 
so 'pyatra sarvāghavimuktadehaḥ prāpnoti vidyādharanāyakatvam  MatsP

matsya uvāca
paripṛṣṭamidaṃ jagatpriyaṃ te vibudhānāmapi durlabhaṃ mahattvāt

nāsāmaśokanidhaye vāsudevāya cākṣiṇī

tatastu maṇḍalaṃ kṛtvā sthaṇḍilaṃ kārayenmudā  MatsP

sthaṇḍilasyopariṣṭācca bhittiraṣṭāṅgulā bhavet  MatsP

namo devyai namaḥ śāntyai namo lakṣmyai namaḥ śriyai

vastrairnānāvidhaistadvat suvarṇakamalena ca  MatsP

tatastu gītanṛtyādi kārayetsakalāṃ niśām  MatsP

abhigamya ca viprāṇāṃ mithunāni tadārcayet  MatsP

tatastu gītavādyena rātrau jāgaraṇe kṛte

bhojanaṃ ca yathāśaktyā vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ 
bhuktvā śrutvā purāṇāni taddinaṃ cātivāhayet  MatsP 
anena vidhinā sarvaṃ māsi māsi samācaret

sopadhānakaviśrāmaṃ sāstarāvaraṇaṃ śubham  MatsP

uttaraiḥ kurubhiryasmāt sāvitreṇa vanena ca  MatsP
