evamāmantrya tānsarvān prabhāte vimale punaḥ  MatsP 
snātvātha gurave dadyān madhyamaṃ parvatottamam 
viṣkambhaparvatāndadyād ṛtvigbhyaḥ kramaśo mune  MatsP 
gāśca dadyāccaturviṃśat yathavā daśa nārada 
nava sapta tathāṣṭau vā pañca dadyād aśaktimān  MatsP 
ekāpi gurave deyā kapilā ca payasvinī 
parvatānāmaśeṣāṇām eṣa eva vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ  MatsP 
ta eva pūjane mantrās ta evopaskarā matāḥ 
grahāṇāṃ lokapālānāṃ brahmādīnāṃ ca sarvadā  MatsP 
svamantreṇaiva sarveṣu homaḥ śaileṣu paṭhyate 
upavāsī bhavennityam aśakte naktamiṣyate  MatsP 
vidhānaṃ sarvaśailānāṃ kramaśaḥ śṛṇu nārada 
dānakāle ca ye mantrāḥ parvateṣu ca yatphalam  MatsP 
annaṃ brahma yataḥ proktam anne prāṇāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ 
annādbhavanti bhūtāni jagadannena vartate  MatsP 
annameva tato lakṣmīr annameva janārdanaḥ 
dhānyaparvatarūpeṇa pāhi tasmānnagottama  MatsP 
anena vidhinā yastu dadyāddhānyamayaṃ girim 
manvantaraśataṃ sāgraṃ devaloke mahīyate  MatsP 
apsarogaṇagandharvair ākīrṇena virājatā 
vimānena divaḥ pṛṣṭham āyāti sma niṣevita 
dharmakṣaye rājarājyam āpnotīha na saṃśayaḥ  MatsP 
MatsyaPurāṇa 
īśvara uvāca
athātaḥ sampravakṣyāmi lavaṇācalamuttamam 
yatpradānānnaro lokān āpnoti śivasaṃyutān  MatsP 
uttamaḥ ṣoḍaśadroṇaiḥ kartavyo lavaṇācalaḥ 
madhyamaḥ syāttadardhena caturbhiradhamaḥ smṛtaḥ  MatsP 
vittahīno yathāśaktyā droṇādūrdhvaṃ tu kārayet 
caturthāṃśena viṣkambhaparvatānkārayetpṛthak  MatsP 
vidhānaṃ pūrvavatkuryād brahmādīnāṃ ca sarvadā 
tadvaddhemamayānsarvāṃl lokapālānniveśayet  MatsP 
sarāṃsi kāmadevādīṃs tadvadatrāpi kārayet 
kuryājjāgaraṇaṃ cāpi dānamantrānnibodhata  MatsP 
saubhāgyasaraḥ sambhūto yato 'yaṃ lavaṇo rasaḥ 
taddānakartṛkatvena tvaṃ māṃ pāhi nagottama  MatsP 
yasmādannarasāḥ sarve notkaṭā lavaṇaṃ vinā 
priyaṃ ca śivayornityaṃ tasmācchāntiṃ prayaccha me  MatsP 
viṣṇudehasamudbhūtaṃ yasmādārogyavardhanam 
tasmātparvatarūpeṇa pāhi saṃsārasāgarāt  MatsP 
anena vidhinā yastu dadyāllavaṇaparvatam 
umāloke vasetkalpaṃ tato yāti parāṃ gatim  MatsP 
MatsyaPurāṇa 
īśvara uvāca
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi guḍaparvatamuttamam 
yatpradānānnaraḥ svargam āpnoti surapūjitam  MatsP 
uttamo daśabhirbhārair madhyamaḥ pañcabhirmataḥ 
tribhirbhāraiḥ kaniṣṭhaḥ syāt tadardhenālpavittavān  MatsP 
tadvadāmantraṇaṃ pūjāṃ hemavṛkṣasurārcanam 
viṣkambhaparvatāṃstadvat sarāṃsi vanadevatāḥ  MatsP 
homajāgaraṇaṃ tadval lokapālādhivāsanam 
dhānyaparvatavat kuryād imaṃ mantramudīrayet  MatsP 
yathā deveṣu viśvātmā pravaro 'yaṃ janārdanaḥ 
sāmavedastu vedānāṃ mahādevastu yoginām  MatsP 
praṇavaḥ sarvamantrāṇāṃ nārīṇāṃ pārvatī yathā 
tathā rasānāṃ pravaraḥ sadaivekṣuraso mataḥ  MatsP 
mama tasmātparāṃ lakṣmīṃ guḍaparvata dehi vai 
yasmātsaubhāgyadāyinyā bhrātā tvaṃ guḍaparvata 
nivāsaścāpi pārvatyās tasmācchāntiṃ prayaccha me  MatsP 
anena vidhinā yastu dadyādguḍamayaṃ girim 
pūjyamānaḥ sa gandharvair gaurīloke mahīyate  MatsP 
tataḥ kalpaśatānte tu saptadvīpādhipo bhavet 
āyurārogyasampannaḥ śatrubhiścāparājitaḥ  MatsP

īśvara uvāca
atha pāpaharaṃ vakṣye suvarṇācalamuttamam 
yasya pradānādbhavanaṃ vairiñcaṃ yāti mānavaḥ  MatsP 
uttamaḥ palasāhasro madhyamaḥ pañcabhiḥ śataiḥ 
tadardhenādhamastadvad alpavitto 'pi śaktitaḥ 
dadyādekapalādūrdhvaṃ yathāśaktyā vimatsaraḥ  MatsP 
dhānyaparvatavatsarvaṃ vidadhyānmunipuṃgava 
viṣkambhaśailāstadvacca ṛtvigbhyaḥ pratipādayet  MatsP 
namaste brahmabījāya brahmagarbhāya te namaḥ 
yasmādanantaphaladas tasmātpāhi śiloccaya  MatsP 
yasmādagnerapatyaṃ tvaṃ yasmātpuṇyaṃ jagatpate 
hemaparvatarūpeṇa tasmātpāhi nagottama  MatsP 
anena vidhinā yastu dadyātkanakaparvatam 
sa yāti paramaṃ brahmalokamānandakārakam 
tatra kalpaśataṃ tiṣṭhet tato yāti parāṃ gatim  MatsP

īśvara uvāca
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi tilaśailaṃ vidhānataḥ 
yatpradānānnaro yāti viṣṇulokaṃ sanātanam  MatsP 
uttamo daśabhir droṇair madhyamaḥ pañcabhiḥ smṛtaḥ 
tribhiḥ kaniṣṭho viprendra tilaśailaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  MatsP 
pūrvavaccāparānsarvān viṣkambhānabhito girīn 
dānamantrān pravakṣyāmi yathāvanmunipuṃgava  MatsP 
yasmānmadhuvadhe viṣṇor dehasvedasamudbhavāḥ 
tilāḥ kuśāśca māṣāśca tasmācchāntyai bhavatviha  MatsP 
havye kavye ca yasmācca tilā evābhirakṣaṇam 
bhavāduddhara śailendra tilācala namo 'stu te  MatsP 
ityāmantrya ca yo dadyāt tilācalamanuttamam 
sa vaiṣṇavaṃ padaṃ yāti punarāvṛttidurlabham  MatsP 
dīrghāyuṣyaṃ samāpnoti putrapautraiśca modate 
pitṛbhirdevagandharvaiḥ pūjyamāno divaṃ vrajet  MatsP

īśvara uvāca
athātaḥ sampravakṣyāmi kārpāsācalamuttamam 
yatpradānānnaro nityam āpnoti paramaṃ padam  MatsP 
kārpāsaparvatas tadvad viṃśadbhārair ihottamaḥ 
daśabhirmadhyamaḥ proktaḥ pañcabhistvadhamaḥ smṛtaḥ 
bhāreṇālpadhano dadyād vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ  MatsP 
dhānyaparvatavatsarvam āsādya munipuṃgava

īśvara uvāca
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi ghṛtācalamanuttamam 
tejo 'mṛtamayaṃ divyaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam  MatsP 
viṃśatyā ghṛtakumbhānām uttamaḥ syādghṛtācalaḥ 
daśabhirmadhyamaḥ proktaḥ pañcabhistvadhamaḥ smṛtaḥ  MatsP 
alpavitto 'pi yaḥ kuryād dvābhyāmiha vidhānataḥ 
viṣkambhaparvatāṃstadvac caturbhāgeṇa kalpayet  MatsP 
śālitaṇḍulapātrāṇi kumbhopari niveśayet 
kārayetsaṃhatānuccān yathāśobhaṃ vidhānataḥ  MatsP 
veṣṭayecchuklavāsobhir ikṣudaṇḍaphalādikaiḥ 
dhānyaparvatavaccheṣaṃ vidhānamiha paṭhyate  MatsP 
adhivāsanapūrvaṃ ca tadvaddhomasurārcanam 
prabhātāyāṃ tu śarvaryāṃ gurave taṃ nivedayet 
viṣkambhaparvatāṃstadvad ṛtvigbhyaḥ śāntamānasaḥ  MatsP 
saṃyogādghṛtamutpannaṃ yasmādamṛtatejasoḥ 
tasmāddhṛtārcirviśvātmā prīyatāmatra śaṃkaraḥ  MatsP 
yasmāttejomayaṃ brahma ghṛte tadviddhyavasthitam 
ghṛtaparvatarūpeṇa tasmāttvaṃ pāhi no 'niśam  MatsP

mahāpātakayukto 'pi lokamāpnoti śāṃkaram  MatsP 
haṃsasārasayuktena kiṅkiṇījālamālinā

viharetpitṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam  MatsP

īśvara uvāca
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi ratnācalamanuttamam 
muktāphalasahasreṇa parvataḥ syādanuttamaḥ  MatsP 
madhyamaḥ pañcaśatikas triśatenādhamaḥ smṛtaḥ 
caturthāṃśena viṣkambhaparvatāḥ syuḥ samantataḥ  MatsP 
pūrveṇa vajragomedair dakṣiṇenendranīlakaiḥ 
padmarāgayutaḥ kāryo vidvadbhirgandhamādanaḥ  MatsP 
vaidūryavidrumaiḥ paścāt sammiśro vimalācalaḥ 
padmarāgaiḥ sasauvarṇair uttareṇa ca vinyaset  MatsP 
dhānyaparvatavatsarvam atrāpi parikalpayet 
tadvadāvāhanaṃ kuryād vṛkṣāndevāṃśca kāñcanān  MatsP

pūrvavadguruṛtvigbhya imānmantrānudīrayet  MatsP

tvaṃ ca ratnamayo nityaṃ namaste 'stu sadācala  MatsP

anena vidhinā yastu dadyādratnamayaṃ girim

yāvatkalpaśataṃ sāgraṃ vasecceha narādhipa 
rūpārogyaguṇopetaḥ saptadvīpādhipo bhavet  MatsP 
brahmahatyādikaṃ kiṃcid yadatrāmutra vā kṛtam

īśvara uvāca
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi raupyācalamanuttamam 
yatpradānānnaro yāti somalokamanuttamam  MatsP 
daśabhiḥ palasāhasrair uttamo rajatācalaḥ 
pañcabhirmadhyamaḥ proktas tadardhenādhamaḥ smṛtaḥ  MatsP 
aśakto viṃśaterūrdhvaṃ kārayecchaktitastadā 
viṣkambhaparvatāṃstadvat turīyāṃśena kalpayet  MatsP

kaladhautamayāṃstadval lokeśānarcayedbudhaḥ  MatsP 
brahmaviṣṇvarkavānkāryo nitambo 'tra hiraṇmayaḥ 
rājataṃ syādyadanyeṣāṃ sarvaṃ tadiha kāñcanam  MatsP 
śeṣaṃ tu pūrvavatkuryād dhomajāgaraṇādikam

imaṃ mantraṃ paṭhandadyād darbhapāṇirvimatsaraḥ  MatsP

īśvara uvāca
athātaḥ sampravakṣyāmi śarkarāśailamuttamam 
yasya pradānādviṣṇvarkarudrāstuṣyanti sarvadā  MatsP 
aṣṭābhiḥ śarkarābhārair uttamaḥ syānmahācalaḥ 
caturbhirmadhyamaḥ prokto bhārābhyāmadhamaḥ smṛtaḥ  MatsP 
bhāreṇa vārdhabhāreṇa kuryādyaḥ svalpavittavān 
viṣkambhaparvatānkuryāt turīyāṃśena mānavaḥ  MatsP 
dhānyaparvatavatsarvam āsādyāmarasaṃyutam 
merorupari tadvacca sthāpyaṃ hematarutrayam  MatsP 
mandāraḥ pārijātaśca tṛtīyaḥ kalpapādapaḥ 
etadvṛkṣatrayaṃ mūrdhni sarveṣvapi niyojayet  MatsP 
haricandanasaṃtānau pūrvapaścimabhāgayoḥ 
niveśyau sarvaśaileṣu viśeṣāccharkarācale  MatsP 
mandare kāmadevastu pratyagvaktraḥ sadā bhavet 
gandhamādanaśṛṅge tu dhanadaḥ syādudaṅmukhaḥ  MatsP 
prāṅmukho vedamūrtistu haṃsaḥ syādvipulācale 
haimī supārśve surabhir dakṣiṇābhimukhī bhavet  MatsP 
dhānyaparvatavatsarvam āvāhanavidhānakam 
kṛtvā tu gurave dadyān madhyamaṃ parvatottamam 
ṛtvigbhyaś caturaḥ śailān imānmantrānudīrayan  MatsP 
saubhāgyāmṛtasāro 'yaṃ parvataḥ śarkarāyutaḥ 
tasmādānandakārī tvaṃ bhava śailendra sarvadā  MatsP 
amṛtaṃ pibatāṃ ye tu nipeturbhuvi śīkarāḥ 
devānāṃ tatsamutthastvaṃ pāhi naḥ śarkarācala  MatsP 
manobhavadhanurmadhyād udbhūtā śarkarā yataḥ 
tanmayo 'si mahāśaila pāhi saṃsārasāgarāt  MatsP 
yo dadyāccharkarāśailam anena vidhinā naraḥ 
sarvapāpair vinirmuktaḥ sa yāti paramaṃ padam  MatsP 
candratārārkasaṃkāśam adhiruhyānujīvibhiḥ 
sahaiva yānamātiṣṭhet tatra viṣṇupracoditaḥ  MatsP 
tataḥ kalpaśatānte tu saptadvīpādhipo bhavet 
āyurārogyasampanno yāvajjanmārbudatrayam  MatsP 
bhojanaṃ śaktitaḥ kuryāt sarvaśaileṣvamatsaraḥ 
sarvatrākṣāralavaṇam aśnīyāttadanujñayā 
parvatopaskarānsarvān prāpayedbrāhmaṇālayam  MatsP 
īśvara uvāca
āsītpurā bṛhatkalpe dharmamūrtirjanādhipaḥ 
suhṛcchakrasya nihatā yena daityāḥ sahasraśaḥ  MatsP 
somasūryādayo yasya tejasā vigataprabhāḥ 
bhavanti śataśo yena śatravaścāparājitāḥ 
yathecchārūpadhārī ca manuṣyo 'pyaparājitaḥ  MatsP 
tasya bhānumatī nāma bhāryā trailokyasundarī 
lakṣmīvad divyarūpeṇa nirjitāmarasundarī  MatsP 
rājñastasyāgryamahiṣī prāṇebhyo 'pi garīyasī 
daśanārīsahasrāṇāṃ madhye śrīriva rājate  MatsP 
nṛpakoṭisahasreṇa na kadācitsa mucyate 
kadācidāsthānagataḥ papraccha sa purodhasam 
vismayenāvṛto rājā vasiṣṭhamṛṣisattamam  MatsP 
rājovāca
bhagavankena dharmeṇa mama lakṣmīranuttamā 
kasmācca vipulaṃ tejo maccharīre sadottamam  MatsP 
vasiṣṭha uvāca
purā līlāvatī nāma veśyā śivaparāyaṇā 
tayā dattaścaturdaśyāṃ gurave lavaṇācalaḥ 
hemavṛkṣādibhiḥ sārdhaṃ yathāvadvidhipūrvakam  MatsP 
śūdraḥ suvarṇakāraśca nāmnā śauṇḍo 'bhavattadā 
bhṛtyo līlāvatīgehe tena hemnā vinirmitāḥ  MatsP 
taravaḥ suramukhyāśca śraddhāyuktena pārthiva 
atirūpeṇa sampannā ghaṭayitvā vinā bhṛtim 
dharmakāryamiti jñātvā na gṛhṇāti kathaṃcana  MatsP 
ujjvālitāśca tatpatnyā sauvarṇāmarapādapāḥ 
līlāvatī gireḥ pārśve paricaryāṃ ca pārthiva  MatsP 
kṛtvā tābhyām aśāṭhyena guruśuśrūṣaṇādikam 
sā ca līlāvatī veśyākālena mahatāpi ca  MatsP 
kāladharmamanuprāptā karmayogeṇa nārada 
sarvapāpavinirmuktā jagāma śivamandiram  MatsP 
yo 'sau suvarṇakārastu daridro 'pyatisattvavān 
na maulyamādādveśyātaḥ sa bhavāniha sāmpratam  MatsP 
saptadvīpapatirjātaḥ sūryāyutasamaprabhaḥ 
yayā suvarṇakārasya taravo hemanirmitāḥ 
samyagujjvālitāḥ patnyā seyaṃ bhānumatī tava  MatsP 
ujjvālanādujjvalarupamasyāḥ saṃjātamasminbhuvanādhipatyam 
yasmātkṛtaṃ tatparikarma rātrāv anuddhatābhyāṃ lavaṇācalasya  MatsP 
tasmācca lokeṣvaparājitatvam ārogyasaubhāgyayutā ca lakṣmīḥ 
tasmāttvamapyatra vidhānapūrvaṃ dhānyācalādīndaśadhā kuruṣva  MatsP 
tatheti satkṛtya sa dharmamūrtir vaco vasiṣṭhasya dadau ca sarvān 
dhānyācaladīñchataśo murārer lokaṃ jagāmāmarapūjyamānaḥ  MatsP 
paśyedapīmānadhano 'tibhaktyā spṛśenmanuṣyairapi dīyamānān 
śṛṇoti bhaktyātha matiṃ dadāti vikalmaṣaḥ so 'pi divaṃ prayāti  MatsP 
duḥsvapnaṃ praśamamupaiti paṭhyamānaiḥ śailendrairbhavabhayabhedanairmanuṣyaiḥ 
yaḥ kuryātkimu munipuṃgaveha samyak śāntātmā sakalagirīndrasampradānam  MatsP 
MatsyaPurāṇa 
sūta uvāca
vaiśampāyanam āsīnam apṛcchacchaunakaḥ purā 
sarvakāmāptaye nityaṃ kathaṃ śāntikapauṣṭikam  MatsP 
vaiśampāyana uvāca
śrīkāmaḥ śāntikāmo vā grahayajñaṃ samārabhet 
vṛddhyāyuḥ puṣṭikāmo vā tathaivābhicaranpunaḥ 
yena brahmanvidhānena tanme nigadataḥ śṛṇu  MatsP 
sarvaśāstrāṇyanukramya saṃkṣipya granthavistaram 
grahaśāntiṃ pravakṣyāmi purāṇaśruticoditām  MatsP 
puṇye 'hni viprakathite kṛtvā brāhmaṇavācanam 
grahāngrahādhidevāṃśca sthāpya homaṃ samārabhet  MatsP 
grahayajñastridhā proktaḥ purāṇaśrutikovidaiḥ 
prathamo 'yutahomaḥ syāl lakṣahomastataḥ param  MatsP 
tṛtīyaḥ koṭihomastu sarvakāmaphalapradaḥ 
ayutenāhutīnāṃ ca navagrahamakhaḥ smṛtaḥ  MatsP 
tasya tāvadvidhiṃ vakṣye purāṇaśrutibhāṣitam 
gartasyottarapūrveṇa vitastidvayavistṛtām  MatsP 
vapradvayāvṛtāṃ vediṃ vitastyucchrāyasaṃmitām 
saṃsthāpanāya devānāṃ caturasrāmudaṅmukhām  MatsP 
agnipraṇayanaṃ kṛtvā tasyāmāvāhayetsurān 
devatānāṃ tataḥ sthāpyā viṃśatirdvādaśādhikā  MatsP 
sūryaḥ somastathā bhaumo budhajīvasitārkajāḥ 
rāhuḥ keturiti proktā grahā lokahitāvahāḥ  MatsP 
madhye tu bhāskaraṃ vidyāl lohitaṃ dakṣiṇena tu 
uttareṇa guruṃ vidyād budhaṃ pūrvottareṇa tu  MatsP 
pūrveṇa bhārgavaṃ vidyāt somaṃ dakṣiṇapūrvake 
paścimena śaniṃ vidyād rāhuṃ paścimadakṣiṇe 
paścimottarataḥ ketuṃ sthāpayecchuklataṇḍulaiḥ  MatsP 
bhāskarasyeśvaraṃ vidyād umāṃ ca śaśinastathā 
skandamaṅgārakasyāpi budhasya ca tathā harim  MatsP 
brahmāṇaṃ ca gurorvidyāc chukrasyāpi śacīpatim 
śanaiścarasya tu yamaṃ rāhoḥ kālaṃ tathaiva ca  MatsP 
ketorvai citraguptaṃ ca sarveṣāmadhidevatāḥ 
agnirāpaḥ kṣitirviṣṇur indra aindrī ca devatāḥ  MatsP 
prajāpatiśca sarpāśca brahmā pratyadhidevatāḥ

āvāhayedvyāhṛtibhis tathaivāśvikumārakau  MatsP

grahavarṇāni deyāni vāsāṃsi kusumāni ca

bṛhaspate paridīyā ratheneti gurormataḥ  MatsP

indrāyendo marutvata iti śakrasya śasyate  MatsP

jātavedase sunavāma durgāmantro 'yamucyate  MatsP

āyasaṃ rāhave dadyāt ketubhyaśchāgamuttamam 
suvarṇena samā kāryā yajamānena dakṣiṇā  MatsP

anyathā phaladaṃ puṃsāṃ na kāmyaṃ jāyate kvacit

tataḥ svargātparibhraṣṭaḥ kṣīṇakarmā divaścyutaḥ 
hiraṇyaratnasampūrṇe samṛddhe jāyate kule 
tadeva smarate tīrthaṃ smaraṇāttatra gacchati  MatsP 
deśastho yadi vāraṇye videśastho 'thavā gṛhe 
prayāgaṃ smaramāṇo 'pi yastu prāṇānparityajet 
brahmalokamavāpnoti vadanti ṛṣipuṃgavāḥ  MatsP 
sarvakāmaphalā vṛkṣā mahī yatra hiraṇmayī 
ṛṣayo munayaḥ siddhās tatra loke sa gacchati  MatsP 
strīsahasrāvṛte ramye mandākinyāstaṭe śubhe 
modate ṛṣibhiḥ sārdhaṃ sukṛteneha karmaṇā  MatsP 
siddhacāraṇagandharvaiḥ pūjyate divi daivataiḥ 
tataḥ svargātparibhraṣṭo jambūdvīpapatirbhavet  MatsP 
tataḥ śubhāni karmāṇi cintayānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ 
guṇavānvittasampanno bhavatīha na saṃśayaḥ  MatsP 
karmaṇā manasā vācā dharmasatyapratiṣṭhitaḥ 
gaṅgāyamunayormadhye yastu gāṃ samprayacchati  MatsP 
suvarṇamaṇimuktāśca yadi vānyatparigraham 
svakārye pitṛkārye vā devatābhyarcane 'pi vā 
saphalaṃ tasya tattīrthaṃ yathāvatpuṇyamāpnuyāt  MatsP 
evaṃ tīrthe na gṛhṇīyāt puṇyeṣvāyataneṣu ca 
nimitteṣu ca sarveṣu hy apramatto bhaveddvijaḥ  MatsP 
kapilāṃ pāṭalāvarṇāṃ yastu dhenuṃ prayacchati 
svarṇaśṛṅgīṃ raupyakhurāṃ kāṃsyadohāṃ payasvinīm  MatsP 
prayāge śrotriyaṃ santaṃ grāhayitvā yathāvidhi 
śuklāmbaradharaṃ śāntaṃ dharmajñaṃ vedapāragam  MatsP 
sā gaustasmai pradātavyā gaṅgāyamunasaṃgame 
vāsāṃsi ca mahārhāṇi ratnāni vividhāni ca  MatsP 
yāvadromāṇi tasyā goḥ santi gātreṣu sattama 
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate  MatsP 
yatrāsau labhate janma sā gaustasyābhijāyate 
na ca paśyati taṃ ghoraṃ narakaṃ tena karmaṇā 
uttarānsa kurūnprāpya modate kālamakṣayam  MatsP 
gavāṃ śatasahasrebhyo dadyādekāṃ payasvinīm 
putrāndārāṃstathā bhṛtyān gaurekā prati tārayet  MatsP 
tasmātsarveṣu dāneṣu godānaṃ tu viśiṣyate 
durgame viṣame ghore mahāpātakasambhave 
gaureva rakṣāṃ kurute tasmāddeyā dvijottame  MatsP

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
yathā yathā prayāgasya māhātmyaṃ kathyate tvayā 
tathā tathā pramucye 'haṃ sarvapāpairna saṃśayaḥ  MatsP 
bhagavankena vidhinā gantavyaṃ dharmaniścayaiḥ 
prayāge yo vidhiḥ proktas tanme brūhi mahāmune  MatsP 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
kathayiṣyāmi te rājaṃs tīrthayātrāvidhikramam 
ārṣeṇa vidhinānena yathādṛṣṭaṃ yathāśrutam  MatsP 
prayāgatīrthayātrārthī yaḥ prayāti naraḥ kvacit 
balīvardasamārūḍhaḥ śṛṇu tasyāpi yatphalam  MatsP

salilaṃ na ca gṛhṇanti pitarastasya dehinaḥ  MatsP

yathātmanā tathā sarvaṃ dānaṃ vipreṣu dāpayet  MatsP

niṣphalaṃ tasya tatsarvaṃ tasmādyānaṃ vivarjayet  MatsP

ārṣeṇaiva vivāhena yathāvibhavasambhavam  MatsP

svarge tiṣṭhati rājendra yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam  MatsP

nirdahanti jagatsarvaṃ vaṭamūlaṃ na dahyate  MatsP

tato gaccheta rājendra prayāgaṃ saṃstuvaṃśca yat 
yatra brahmādayo devā ṛṣayaḥ siddhacāraṇāḥ  MatsP 
lokapālāśca sādhyāśca pitaro lokasaṃmatāḥ 
sanatkumārapramukhās tathaiva paramarṣayaḥ  MatsP

sāgarāḥ saritaḥ śailā nāgā vidyādharāśca ye 
hariśca bhagavanāste prajāpatipuraḥsaraḥ  MatsP

tataḥ puṇyatamaṃ nāsti triṣu lokeṣu bhārata  MatsP

tatrābhiṣekaṃ yaḥ kuryāt saṃgame śaṃsitavrataḥ 
tulyaṃ phalamavāpnoti rājasūyāśvamedhayoḥ  MatsP 
na devavacanāttāta na lokavacanāttathā

yā gatir yogayuktasya satyasthasya manīṣiṇaḥ 
sā gatistyajataḥ prāṇān gaṅgāyamunasaṃgame  MatsP 
na te jīvanti loke 'smiṃs tatra tatra yudhiṣṭhira 
ye prayāgaṃ na samprāptās triṣu lokeṣu vañcitāḥ  MatsP 
evaṃ dṛṣṭvā tu tattīrthaṃ prayāgaṃ paramaṃ padam 
mucyate sarvapāpebhyaḥ śaśāṅka iva rāhuṇā  MatsP 
kambalāśvatarau nāgau vipule yamunātaṭe 
tatra snātvā ca pītvā ca sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  MatsP 
tatra gatvā ca saṃsthānaṃ mahādevasya viśrutam 
narastārayate sarvān daśa pūrvāndaśāparān  MatsP

upavāsī śuciḥ saṃdhyāṃ brahmalokamavāpnuyāt  MatsP

caturvedeṣu yatpuṇyaṃ yatpuṇyaṃ satyavādiṣu

tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate  MatsP 
tataḥ svargātparibhraṣṭo jambūdvīpapatirbhavet

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
yamunāyāṃ tu kiṃ puṇyaṃ kiṃ phalaṃ tu mahāmune 
etanme sarvamākhyāhi yathādṛṣṭaṃ yathāśrutam  MatsP 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

uttareṇa pravakṣyāmi ādityasya mahātmanaḥ 
tīrthaṃ nirañjanaṃ nāma yatra devāḥ savāsavāḥ  MatsP 
upāsate sma saṃdhyāṃ ye trikālaṃ hi yudhiṣṭhira 
devāḥ sevanti tattīrthaṃ ye cānye vibudhā janāḥ  MatsP 
śraddadhānaparo bhūtvā kuru tīrthābhiṣecanam 
anye ca bahavastīrthāḥ sarvapāpaharāḥ smṛtāḥ 
teṣu snātvā divaṃ yānti ye mṛtāste 'punarbhavāḥ  MatsP 
gaṅgā ca yamunā caiva ubhe tulyaphale smṛte 
kevalaṃ jyeṣṭhabhāvena gaṅgā sarvatra pūjyate  MatsP 
evaṃ kuruṣva kaunteya sarvatīrthābhiṣecanam 
yāvajjīvakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇādeva naśyati  MatsP 
yastvimaṃ kalya utthāya paṭhate ca śṛṇoti ca 
mucyate sarvapāpebhyaḥ svargalokaṃ sa gacchati  MatsP

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śrutaṃ me brahmaṇā proktaṃ purāṇe brahmasambhave 
tīrthānāṃ tu sahasrāṇi śatāni niyutāni ca 
sarve puṇyāḥ pavitrāśca gatiśca paramā smṛtā  MatsP 
somatīrthaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam 
snānamātreṇa rājendra puruṣāṃstārayecchatam 
tasmātsarvaprayatnena tatra snānaṃ samācaret  MatsP 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
pṛthivyāṃ naimiṣaṃ puṇyam antarikṣe ca puṣkaram 
trayāṇāmapi lokānāṃ kurukṣetraṃ viśiṣyate  MatsP 
sarvāṇi tāni saṃtyajya kathamekaṃ praśaṃsasi 
apramāṇaṃ tu tatroktam aśraddheyamanuttamam  MatsP 
gatiṃ ca paramāṃ divyāṃ bhogāṃścaiva yathepsitān 
kimarthamalpayogena bahu dharmaṃ praśaṃsasi 
etanme saṃśayaṃ brūhi yathādṛṣṭaṃ yathāśrutam  MatsP 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
aśraddheyaṃ na vaktavyaṃ pratyakṣamapi yadbhavet 
narasyāśraddadhānasya pāpopahatacetasaḥ  MatsP 
aśraddadhāno hyaśucir durmatistyaktamaṅgalaḥ 
ete pātakinaḥ sarve tenedaṃ bhāṣitaṃ tvayā  MatsP 
śṛṇu prayāgamāhātmyaṃ yathādṛṣṭaṃ yathāśrutam 
pratyakṣaṃ ca parokṣaṃ ca yathānyastaṃ bhaviṣyati  MatsP 
yathaivānyadadṛṣṭaṃ ca yathādṛṣṭaṃ yathāśrutam 
śāstraṃ pramāṇaṃ kṛtvā ca yujyate yogamātmanaḥ  MatsP 
kliśyate cāparastatra naiva yogamavāpnuyāt 
janmāntarasahasrebhyo yogo labhyeta mānavaiḥ  MatsP 
yathā yogasahasreṇa yogo labhyeta mānavaiḥ 
yastu sarvāṇi ratnāni brāhmaṇebhyaḥ prayacchati  MatsP 
tena dānena dattena yogaṃ nābhyeti mānavaḥ 
prayāge tu mṛtasyedaṃ sarvaṃ bhavati nānyathā  MatsP 
pradhānahetuṃ vakṣyāmi śraddadhatsva ca bhārata 
yathā sarveṣu bhūteṣu brahma sarvatra dṛśyate  MatsP 
brāhmaṇe vāsti yatkiṃcid abrāhmam iti vocyate 
evaṃ sarveṣu bhūteṣu brahma sarvatra pūjyate  MatsP 
tathā sarveṣu lokeṣu prayāgaṃ pūjayedbudhaḥ 
pūjyate tīrtharājastu satyameva yudhiṣṭhira  MatsP 
brahmāpi smarate nityaṃ prayāgaṃ tīrthamuttamam 
tīrtharājam anuprāpya na cānyatkiṃcidarhati  MatsP 
ko hi devatvamāsādya manuṣyatvaṃ cikīrṣati 
anenaivopamānena tvaṃ jñāsyasi yudhiṣṭhira 
yathā puṇyatamaṃ cāsti tathaiva kathitaṃ mayā  MatsP 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
śrutaṃ cedaṃ tvayā proktaṃ vismito 'haṃ punaḥ punaḥ 
kathaṃ yogena tatprāptiḥ svargavāsastu karmaṇā  MatsP 
dātā vai labhate bhogān gāṃ ca yatkarmaṇaḥ phalam 
tāni karmāṇi pṛcchāmi punastaiḥ prāpyate mahī  MatsP 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇu rājanmahābāho yathoktakaraṇaṃ mahīm 
gāmagniṃ brāhmaṇaṃ śāstraṃ kāñcanaṃ salilaṃ striyaḥ  MatsP 
mātaraṃ pitaraṃ caiva ye nindanti narādhamāḥ 
na teṣāmūrdhvagamanam idamāha prajāpatiḥ  MatsP 
evaṃ yogasya samprāptisthānaṃ paramadurlabham 
gacchanti narakaṃ ghoraṃ ye narāḥ pāpakarmiṇaḥ  MatsP 
hastyaśvaṃ gām anaḍvāhaṃ maṇimuktādikāñcanam 
parokṣaṃ harate yastu paścāddānaṃ prayacchati  MatsP 
na te gacchanti vai svargaṃ dātāro yatra bhoginaḥ 
anenakarmaṇā yuktāḥ pacyante narake punaḥ  MatsP 
evaṃ yogaṃ ca dharmaṃ ca dātāraṃ ca yudhiṣṭhira 
yathā satyamasatyaṃ vā asti nāstīti yatphalam 
niruktaṃ tu pravakṣyāmi yathāha svayamaṃśumān  MatsP

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇu rājanprayāgasya māhātmyaṃ punareva tu 
naimiṣaṃ puṣkaraṃ caiva gotīrthaṃ sindhusāgaram  MatsP 
gayā ca caitrakaṃ caiva gaṅgāsāgarameva ca 
ete cānye ca bahavo ye ca puṇyāḥ śiloccayāḥ  MatsP 
daśa tīrthasahasrāṇi triṃśatkoṭyastathā parāḥ 
prayāge saṃsthitā nityam evamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ  MatsP 
trīṇi cāpyagnikuṇḍāni yeṣāṃ madhye tu jāhnavī 
prayāgādabhiniṣkrāntā sarvatīrthanamaskṛtā  MatsP 
tapanasya sutā devī triṣu lokeṣu viśrutā 
yamunā gaṅgayā sārdhaṃ saṃgatā lokabhāvinī  MatsP 
gaṅgāyamunayormadhye pṛthivyā jaghanaṃ smṛtam

tisraḥ koṭyo 'rdhakoṭiśca tīrthānāṃ vāyurabravīt

prayāgaṃ samadhiṣṭhānaṃ kambalāśvatarāvubhau 
bhogavatyatha yā caiṣā vedireṣā prajāpateḥ  MatsP

prajāpatim upāsante ṛṣayaśca tapodhanāḥ  MatsP

tataḥ puṇyatamaṃ nāsti triṣu lokeṣu bhārata  MatsP

yatra gaṅgā mahābhāgā sa deśastattapodhanam 
siddhakṣetraṃ ca vijñeyaṃ gaṅgātīrasamanvitam  MatsP 
idaṃ satyaṃ vijānīyāt sādhūnāmātmanaśca vai 
suhṛdaśca japetkarṇe śiṣyasyānugatasya ca  MatsP 
idaṃ dhanyamidaṃ svargyam idaṃ satyamidaṃ sukham 
idaṃ puṇyamidaṃ dharmyaṃ pāvanaṃ dharmamuttamam  MatsP 
maharṣīṇāmidaṃ guhyaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam 
adhītya ca dvijo 'pyetan nirmalaḥ svargamāpnuyāt  MatsP 
ya idaṃ śṛṇuyānnityaṃ tīrthaṃ puṇyaṃ sadā śuciḥ 
jātismaratvaṃ labhate nākapṛṣṭhe ca modate  MatsP 
prāpyante tāni tīrthāni sadbhiḥ śiṣṭānudarśibhiḥ 
snāhi tīrtheṣu kauravya na ca vakramatirbhava  MatsP 
tvayā ca samyakpṛṣṭena kathitaṃ vai mayā vibho 
pitarastāritāḥ sarve tathaiva ca pitāmahāḥ  MatsP 
vrataṃ dānaṃ tapastīrthaṃ yāgāḥ sarve sadakṣiṇāḥ 
yogāḥ sāṃkhyaṃ sadācāro ye cānye jñānahetavaḥ 
prayāgasya tu sarve te kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm  MatsP 
evaṃ jñānaṃ ca yogaśca tīrthaṃ caiva yudhiṣṭhira 
bahukleśena yujyante tena yānti parāṃ gatim 
trikālaṃ jāyate jñānaṃ svargalokaṃ gamiṣyati  MatsP

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇu rājanprayāge tu proktaṃ sarvamidaṃ jagat 
brahmā viṣṇustatheśāno devatāḥ prabhuravyayaḥ  MatsP 
brahmā sṛjati bhūtāni sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ ca yat 
tānyetāni paraṃ loke viṣṇuḥ saṃvardhate prajāḥ  MatsP

tadā prayāgatīrthaṃ ca na kadācidvinaśyati  MatsP 
īśvaraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati 
yatnenānena tiṣṭhanti te yānti paramāṃ gatim  MatsP 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
ākhyāhi me yathātathyaṃ yathaiṣā tiṣṭhati śrutiḥ 
kena vā kāraṇenaiva tiṣṭhante lokasattamāḥ  MatsP 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
prayāge nivasantyete brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ

tiṣṭhanti rakṣaṇāyātra pāpakarmanivāraṇāt  MatsP 
uttareṇa pratiṣṭhānāc chadmanā brahma tiṣṭhati 
veṇīmādhavarūpī tu bhagavāṃstatra tiṣṭhati  MatsP 
māheśvaro vaṭo bhūtvā tiṣṭhate parameśvaraḥ

rakṣanti maṇḍalaṃ nityaṃ pāpakarmanivāraṇāt  MatsP 
yasmiñjuhvansvakaṃ pāpaṃ narakaṃ ca na paśyati 
evaṃ brahmā ca viṣṇuśca prayāge sa maheśvaraḥ  MatsP 
saptadvīpāḥ samudrāśca parvatāśca mahītale 
rakṣamāṇāśca tiṣṭhanti yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam  MatsP 
ye cānye bahavaḥ sarve tiṣṭhanti ca yudhiṣṭhira 
yat pṛthivī tatsamāśritya nirmitā daivatais tribhiḥ  MatsP 
prajāpateridaṃ kṣetraṃ prayāgamiti viśrutam

vāsudeva uvāca
mama vākyaṃ ca kartavyaṃ mahārāja bravīmyaham 
nityaṃ japasva juhvasva prayāge vigatajvaraḥ  MatsP 
prayāgaṃ smara vai nityaṃ sahāsmābhiryudhiṣṭhira

pratigrahādupāvṛttaḥ saṃtuṣṭo niyataḥ śuciḥ

svastho bhava mahārāja bhuṅkṣva rājyamakaṇṭakam 
punardrakṣyasi rājendra yajamāno viśeṣataḥ  MatsP 
nandikeśvara uvāca

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ

teṣāṃ manuṣyatarkeṇa pramāṇāni pracakṣate  MatsP 
acintyāḥ khalu ye bhāvās tāṃstu tarkeṇa sādhayet

pārśvamuttaratastasya raktavarṇaṃ svabhāvataḥ

teṣāmantaraviṣkambho navasāhasramucyate  MatsP

madhye tasya mahāmerur vidhūma iva pāvakaḥ 
vedyardhaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ meror uttarārdhaṃ tathottaram  MatsP

dve dve sahasre vistīrṇā yojanairdakṣiṇottaram  MatsP

varṣāṇāṃ parvatānāṃ ca yathābhedaṃ tathottaram 
teṣāṃ madhye janapadās tāni varṣāṇi sapta vai  MatsP 
prapātaviṣamaistaistu parvatairāvṛtāni tu 
sapta tāni nadībhedair agamyāni parasparam  MatsP 
vasanti teṣu sattvāni nānājātīni sarvaśaḥ 
imaṃ haimavataṃ varṣaṃ bhārataṃ nāma viśrutam  MatsP 
hemakūṭaṃ paraṃ tasmān nāmnā kimpuruṣaṃ smṛtam 
hemakūṭācca niṣadhaṃ harivarṣaṃ taducyate  MatsP 
harivarṣātparaṃ cāpi merostu tadilāvṛtam 
ilāvṛtātparaṃ nīlaṃ ramyakaṃ nāma viśrutam  MatsP 
ramyakādaparaṃ śvetaṃ viśrutaṃ taddhiraṇyakam 
hiraṇyakātparaṃ caiva śṛṅgaśākaṃkuraṃ smṛtam  MatsP 
dhanuḥsaṃsthe tu vijñeye devarṣe dakṣiṇottare

pūrvato niṣadhasyedaṃ vedyardhaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ smṛtam 
paraṃ tvilāvṛtaṃ paścād vedyardhaṃ tu taduttaram  MatsP 
tayormadhye tu vijñeyo meruryatra tvilāvṛtam 
dakṣiṇena tu nīlasya niṣadhasyottareṇa tu  MatsP 
udagāyato mahāśailo mālyavānnāma parvataḥ 
dvātriṃśatā sahasreṇa pratīcyāṃ sāgarānugaḥ  MatsP 
mālyavānvai sahasraika ā nīlaniṣadhāyataḥ 
dvātriṃśattvevamapyuktaḥ parvato gandhamādanaḥ  MatsP 
parimaṇḍalayormadhye meruḥ kanakaparvataḥ 
cāturvarṇyasamo varṇaiś caturasraḥ samucchritaḥ  MatsP 
nānāvarṇaḥ sa pārśveṣu pūrvānte śveta ucyate 
pītaṃ tu dakṣiṇaṃ tasya bhṛṅgipattranibhaṃ param 
uttaraṃ tasya raktaṃ vai iti varṇasamanvitaḥ  MatsP 
merustu śuśubhe divyo rājavatsa tu veṣṭitaḥ 
ādityataruṇābhāso vidhūma iva pāvakaḥ  MatsP 
yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi caturāśītisūcchritaḥ

vistarāddviguṇaścāsya parīṇāhaḥ samantataḥ 
sa parvato mahādivyo divyauṣadhisamanvitaḥ  MatsP 
bhuvanairāvṛtaḥ sarvair jātarūpapariṣkṛtaiḥ 
tatra devagaṇāścaiva gandharvāsurarākṣasāḥ 
śailarāje pramodante sarvato 'psarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ  MatsP 
sa tu meruḥ parivṛto bhuvanairbhūtabhāvanaiḥ 
yasyeme caturo deśā nānāpārśveṣu saṃsthitāḥ  MatsP 
bhadrāśvaṃ bhārataṃ caiva ketumālaṃ ca paścime 
uttarāścaiva kuravaḥ kṛtapuṇyapratiśrayāḥ  MatsP 
viṣkambhaparvatāstadvan mandaro gandhamādanaḥ 
vipulaśca supārśvaśca sarvaratnavibhūṣitāḥ  MatsP 
aruṇodaṃ mānasaṃ ca sitodaṃ bhadrasaṃjñitam 
teṣāmupari catvāri sarāṃsi ca vanāni ca  MatsP 
tathā bhadrakadambastu parvate gandhamādane 
jambūvṛkṣastathāśvattho vipule 'tha vaṭaḥ param  MatsP 
gandhamādanapārśve tu paścime 'maragaṇḍikaḥ 
dvātriṃśacca sahasrāṇi yojanaiḥ sarvataḥ samaḥ  MatsP 
tatra te śubhakarmāṇaḥ ketumālāḥ pariśrutāḥ 
tatra kālānalāḥ sarve mahāsattvā mahābalāḥ  MatsP 
striyaś cotpalavarṇābhāḥ sundaryaḥ priyadarśanāḥ 
tatra divyo mahāvṛkṣaḥ panasaḥ pattrabhāsuraḥ  MatsP 
tasya pītvā phalarasaṃ saṃjīvanti samāyutam 
tasya mālyavataḥ pārśve pūrve pūrvā tu gaṇḍikā 
dvātriṃśacca sahasrāṇi tatrāpi śatamucyate  MatsP 
bhadrāśvastatra vijñeyo nityaṃ muditamānasaḥ 
bhadramālavanaṃ tatra kālāmraśca mahādrumaḥ  MatsP 
tatra te puruṣāḥ śvetā mahāsattvā mahābalāḥ 
striyaḥ kumudavarṇābhāḥ sundaryaḥ priyadarśanāḥ  MatsP 
candraprabhāś candravarṇāḥ pūrṇacandranibhānanāḥ 
candraśītalagātrāśca striyo hyutpalagandhikāḥ  MatsP 
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi āyusteṣāmanāmayam 
kālāmrasya rasaṃ pītvā te sarve sthirayauvanāḥ  MatsP

ityuktavānṛṣīnbrahmā varṣāṇi ca nisargataḥ

jātakautūhalāḥ sarve pratyūcuste mudānvitāḥ  MatsP

pūrvāparau samākhyātau yau deśau tau tvayā mune

ākhyāhi no yathātathyaṃ ye ca parvatavāsinaḥ

śṛṇudhvaṃ yāni varṣāṇi pūrvoktāni ca vai mayā 
dakṣiṇena tu nīlasya niṣadhasyottareṇa tu  MatsP 
varṣaṃ ramaṇakaṃ nāma jāyante yatra vai prajāḥ 
ratipradhānā vimalā jāyante yatra mānavāḥ 
śuklābhijanasampannāḥ sarve te priyadarśanāḥ  MatsP 
tatrāpi ca mahāvṛkṣo nyagrodho rohiṇo mahān 
tasyāpi te phalarasaṃ pibanto vartayanti hi  MatsP 
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi daśavarṣaśatāni ca 
jīvanti te mahābhāgāḥ sadā hṛṣṭā narottamāḥ  MatsP 
uttareṇa tu śvetasya pārśve śṛṅgasya dakṣiṇe 
varṣaṃ hiraṇvataṃ nāma yatra hairaṇvatī nadī  MatsP 
mahābalā mahāsattvā nityaṃ muditamānasāḥ 
śuklābhijanasampannāḥ sarve ca priyadarśanāḥ  MatsP 
ekādaśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ te narottamāḥ 
āyuṣpramāṇaṃ jīvanti śatāni daśa pañca ca  MatsP 
tasminvarṣe mahāvṛkṣo lakucaḥ pattrasaṃśrayaḥ 
tasya pītvā phalarasaṃ tatra jīvanti mānavāḥ  MatsP 
śṛṅgasāhvasya śṛṅgāṇi trīṇi tāni mahānti vai 
ekaṃ maṇiyutaṃ tatra ekaṃ tu kanakānvitam 
sarvaratnamayaṃ caikaṃ bhuvanairupaśobhitam  MatsP 
uttare cāsya śṛṅgasya samudrānte ca dakṣiṇe 
kuravastatra tadvaryaṃ puṇyaṃ siddhaniṣevitam  MatsP

vastrāṇi te prasūyante phalaiścābharaṇāni ca  MatsP 
sarvakāmapradātāraḥ kecidvṛkṣā manoramāḥ 
apare kṣīriṇo nāma vṛkṣāstatra manoramāḥ 
ye rakṣanti sadā kṣīraṃ ṣaḍrasaṃ cāmṛtopamam  MatsP 
sarvā maṇimayī bhūmiḥ sūkṣmā kāñcanavālukā 
sarvatra sukhasaṃsparśā niḥśabdāḥ pavanāḥ śubhāḥ  MatsP 
devalokacyutāstatra jāyante mānavāḥ śubhāḥ 
śuklābhijanasampannāḥ sarve te sthirayauvanāḥ  MatsP 
mithunāni prajāyante striyaścāpsarasopamāḥ 
teṣāṃ te kṣīriṇāṃ kṣīraṃ pibanti hyamṛtopamam  MatsP

yadidaṃ bhārataṃ varṣaṃ yasmin svāyambhuvādayaḥ 
caturdaśaiva manavaḥ prajāsargaṃ sasarjire  MatsP 
etad veditum icchāmaḥ sakāśāttava suvrata 
uttaraśravaṇaṃ bhūyaḥ prabrūhi vadatāṃ vara  MatsP 
etacchrutvā ṛṣīṇāṃ tu prābravīllaumaharṣaṇiḥ 
paurāṇikastadā sūta ṛṣīṇāṃ bhāvitātmanām  MatsP 
buddhyā vicārya bahudhā vimṛśya ca punaḥ punaḥ 
tebhyastu kathayāmāsa uttaraśravaṇaṃ tadā  MatsP 
sūta uvāca
athāhaṃ varṇayiṣyāmi varṣe 'sminbhārate prajāḥ 
bharaṇātprajanāccaiva manurbharata ucyate  MatsP 
niruktavacanaiścaiva varṣaṃ tadbhārataṃ smṛtam 
yataḥ svargaśca mokṣaśca madhyamaścāpi hi smṛtaḥ  MatsP 
na khalvanyatra martyānāṃ bhūmau karmavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ 
bhāratasyāsya varṣasya nava bhedānnibodhata  MatsP 
indradvīpaḥ kaśeruśca tāmraparṇo gabhastimān 
nāgadvīpastathā saumyo gandharvastvatha vāruṇaḥ  MatsP 
ayaṃ tu navamasteṣāṃ dvīpaḥ sāgarasaṃvṛtaḥ 
yojanānāṃ sahasraṃ tu dvīpo 'yaṃ dakṣiṇottaraḥ  MatsP 
āyatastu kumārīto gaṅgāyāḥ pravahāvadhiḥ 
tiryagūrdhvaṃ tu vistīrṇaḥ sahasrāṇi daśaiva tu  MatsP 
dvīpo hyupaniviṣṭo 'yaṃ mlecchairanteṣu sarvaśaḥ 
yavanāśca kirātāśca tasyānte pūrvapaścime  MatsP 
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyā madhye śūdrāśca bhāgaśaḥ 
ijyāyutavaṇijyādi vartayanto vyavasthitāḥ  MatsP 
teṣāṃ sa vyavahāro 'yaṃ vartanaṃ tu parasparam 
dharmārthakāmasaṃyukto varṇānāṃ tu svakarmasu  MatsP 
saṃkalpapañcamānāṃ tu āśramāṇāṃ yathāvidhi 
iha svargāpavargārthaṃ pravṛttiriha mānuṣe  MatsP 
yastvayaṃ mānavo dvīpas tiryagyāmaḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
ya enaṃ jayate kṛtsnaṃ sa samrāḍiti kīrtitaḥ  MatsP 
ayaṃ lokastu vai samrāḍ antarikṣajitāṃ smṛtaḥ 
svarāḍasau smṛto lokaḥ punarvakṣyāmi vistarāt  MatsP 
sapta cāsminmahāvarṣe viśrutāḥ kulaparvatāḥ 
mahendro malayaḥ sahyaḥ śuktimānṛkṣavānapi  MatsP 
vindhyaśca pāriyātraśca ityete kulaparvatāḥ 
teṣāṃ sahasraśaścānye parvatāstu samīpataḥ  MatsP 
abhijñātāstataścānye vipulāścitrasānavaḥ 
anye tebhyaḥ parijñātā hrasvā hrasvopajīvinaḥ  MatsP 
tairvimiśrā jānapadā āryā mlecchāśca sarvataḥ 
pibanti bahulā nadyo gaṅgā sindhuḥ sarasvatī  MatsP 
śatadruścandrabhāgā ca yamunā sarayūstathā 
airāvatī vitastā ca viśālā devikā kuhūḥ  MatsP 
gomatī dhautapāpā ca bāhudā ca dṛṣadvatī 
kauśikī tu tṛtīyā ca niścalā gaṇḍakī tathā  MatsP 
ikṣurlauhitam ityetā himavatpārśvaniḥsṛtāḥ 
vedasmṛtir vetravatī vṛtraghnī sindhureva ca 
parṇāśā narmadā caiva kāverī mahatī tathā  MatsP 
pārā ca dhanvatīrūpā viduṣā veṇumatyapi 
śiprā hyavantī kuntī ca pāriyātrāśritāḥ smṛtāḥ  MatsP 
śoṇo mahānadaścaiva nandanā sukṛśā kṣamā

tamasā pippalī śyenī tathā citrotpalāpi ca  MatsP 
vimalā cañcalā caiva tathā ca dhūtavāhinī

ṛṣyavantaprasūtās tā nadyo 'malajalāḥ śubhāḥ  MatsP 
tāpī payoṣṇī nirvindhyā kṣiprā ca ṛṣabhā nadī 
veṇā vaitaraṇī caiva viśvamālā kumudvatī  MatsP 
toyā caiva mahāgaurī durgamā tu śilā tathā 
vindhyapādaprasūtās tāḥ sarvāḥ śītajalāḥ śubhāḥ  MatsP 
godāvarī bhīmarathī kṛṣṇaveṇī ca vañjulā

dakṣiṇāpathanadyastāḥ sahyapādādviniḥsṛtāḥ  MatsP 
kṛtamālā tāmraparṇī puṣpajā hyutpalāvatī 
malayaprasūtā nadyas tāḥ sarvāḥ śītajalāḥ śubhāḥ  MatsP

mahendratanayāḥ sarvāḥ prakhyātāḥ śubhagāminīḥ  MatsP 
kāśikā sukumārī ca mandagā mandavāhinī

sarvāḥ puṇyajalāḥ puṇyāḥ sarvagāśca samudragāḥ

tāsāṃ nadyupanadyaśca śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ 
tāsvime kurupāñcālāḥ śālvāścaiva sajāṅgalāḥ  MatsP

matsyāḥ kirātāḥ kulyāśca kuntalāḥ kāśikośalāḥ  MatsP

madhyadeśā janapadāḥ prāyaśaḥ parikīrtitāḥ  MatsP 
sahyasyānantare caite tatra godāvarī nadī

tataḥ puṣpavaro deśas tena jajñe manoramaḥ  MatsP

puraṃdhrāścaiva śūdrāśca pallavāś cāttakhaṇḍikāḥ  MatsP 
gāndhārā yavanāścaiva sindhusauvīramadrakāḥ 
śakā druhyāḥ pulindāśca pāradāhāramūrtikāḥ  MatsP

kṣatriyopaniveśyāśca vaiśyāḥ śūdrakulāni ca  MatsP 
atrayo 'tha bharadvājāḥ prasthalāḥ sadaserakāḥ 
lampakās talagānāśca sainikāḥ saha jāṅgalaiḥ 
ete deśā udīcyāstu prācyāndeśānnibodhata  MatsP 
aṅgā vaṅgā madgurakā antargiribahirgirī 
tataḥ plavaṃgamātaṃgā yamakā mallavarṇakāḥ 
suhmottarāḥ pravijayā mārgavā geyamālavāḥ  MatsP 
prāgjyotiṣāśca puṇḍrāśca videhāstāmraliptakāḥ 
śālvamāgadhagonardāḥ prācyā janapadāḥ smṛtāḥ  MatsP 
teṣāṃ pare janapadā dakṣiṇāpathavāsinaḥ 
pāṇḍyāśca keralāścaiva colāḥ kulyāstathaiva ca  MatsP 
setukāḥ sūtikāścaiva kupathāṃ vājivāsikāḥ 
navarāṣṭrā māhiṣikāḥ kaliṅgāścaiva sarvaśaḥ  MatsP 
kārūṣāśca sahaiṣīkā āṭavyāḥ śabarāstathā 
pulindā vindhyapuṣikā vaidarbhā daṇḍakaiḥ saha  MatsP 
kulīyāśca sirālāśca rūpasās tāpasaiḥ saha 
tathā taittirikāścaiva sarve kāraskarāstathā  MatsP 
vāsikyāścaiva ye cānye ye caivāntaranarmadāḥ 
bhārukacchāḥ samāheyāḥ saha sārasvataistathā  MatsP 
kācchīkāścaiva saurāṣṭrā ānartā arbudaiḥ saha 
ityete aparāntāstu śṛṇu ye vindhyavāsinaḥ  MatsP 
mālavāśca karūṣāśca mekalāścotkalaiḥ saha 
auṇḍrā māṣā daśārṇāśca bhojāḥ kiṣkindhakaiḥ saha  MatsP 
stośalāḥ kosalāścaiva traipurā vaidiśāstathā

arūpāḥ śauṇḍikerāśca vītihotrā avantayaḥ

yacca kimpuruṣaṃ varṣaṃ harivarṣaṃ tathaiva ca

sūta uvāca
śuśrūṣavastu yadviprāḥ śuśrūṣadhvamatandritāḥ 
jambūvarṣaḥ kimpuruṣaḥ sumahānandanopamaḥ  MatsP 
daśa varṣasahasrāṇi sthitiḥ kimpuruṣe smṛtā 
jāyante mānavāstatra sutaptakanakaprabhāḥ  MatsP 
varṣe kimpuruṣe puṇye plakṣo madhuvahaḥ smṛtaḥ

tataḥ paraṃ kimpuruṣād dharivarṣaṃ pracakṣate 
mahārajatasaṃkāśā jāyante yatra mānavāḥ  MatsP 
devalokacyutāḥ sarve bahurūpāśca sarvaśaḥ 
harivarṣe narāḥ sarve pibantīkṣurasaṃ śubham  MatsP 
na jarā bādhate tatra tena jīvanti te ciram 
ekādaśa sahasrāṇi teṣāmāyuḥ prakīrtitam  MatsP 
madhyamaṃ tanmayā proktaṃ nāmnā varṣamilāvṛtam 
na tatra sūryastapati na ca jānanti mānavāḥ  MatsP 
candrasūryau sanakṣatrāv aprakāśāvilāvṛte 
padmaprabhāḥ padmavarṇāḥ padmapattranibhekṣaṇāḥ  MatsP 
padmagandhāśca jāyante tatra sarve ca mānavāḥ 
jambūphalarasāhārā aniṣpandāḥ sugandhinaḥ  MatsP 
devalokacyutāḥ sarve mahārajatavāsasaḥ 
trayodaśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ te narottamāḥ  MatsP 
āyuṣpramāṇaṃ jīvanti ye tu varṣa ilāvṛte 
merostu dakṣiṇe pārśve niṣadhasyottareṇa vā  MatsP 
sudarśano nāma mahāñ jambūvṛkṣaḥ sanātanaḥ 
nityapuṣpaphalopetaḥ siddhacāraṇasevitaḥ  MatsP 
tasya nāmnā samākhyāto jambūdvīpo vanaspateḥ 
yojanānāṃ sahasraṃ ca śatadhā ca mahānpunaḥ  MatsP 
utsedho vṛkṣarājasya divam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati 
tasya jambūphalaraso nadī bhūtvā prasarpati  MatsP 
meruṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā jambūmūlagatā punaḥ 
taṃ pibanti sadā hṛṣṭā jambūrasamilāvṛte  MatsP 
jambūphalarasaṃ pītvā na jarā bādhate 'pi tān 
na kṣudhā na klamo vāpi na duḥkhaṃ ca tathāvidham  MatsP 
tatra jāmbūnadaṃ nāma kanakaṃ devabhūṣaṇam 
indragopakasaṃkāśaṃ jāyate bhāsuraṃ ca yat  MatsP 
sarveṣāṃ varṣavṛkṣāṇāṃ śubhaḥ phalarasastu saḥ 
skannaṃ tu kāñcanaṃ śubhraṃ jāyate devabhūṣaṇam  MatsP 
teṣāṃ mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ vā dikṣvaṣṭāsu ca sarvaśaḥ 
īśvarānugrahādbhūmir mṛtāṃśca grasate tu tān  MatsP 
rakṣaḥpiśācā yakṣāśca sarve haimavatāstu te 
hemakūṭe tu vijñeyā gandharvāḥ sāpsarogaṇāḥ  MatsP 
sarve nāgā niṣevante śeṣavāsukitakṣakāḥ

nīlavaiḍūryayukte 'smin siddhā brahmarṣayo 'vasan 
daityānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca śvetaḥ parvata ucyate  MatsP 
śṛṅgavān parvataśreṣṭhaḥ pitṝṇāṃ pratisaṃcaraḥ 
ityetāni mayoktāni navavarṣāṇi bhārate  MatsP 
bhūtairapi niviṣṭāni gatimanti dhruvāṇi ca

aśakyā parisaṃkhyātuṃ śraddheyā ca bubhūṣatā  MatsP

matsya uvāca
śṛṇu karmavipākena yena rājā purūravāḥ 
avāpa tādṛśaṃ rūpaṃ saubhāgyamapi cottamam  MatsP 
atīte janmani purā yo 'yaṃ rājā purūravāḥ

cākṣuṣasyānvaye rājā cākṣuṣasyāntare manoḥ 
sa vai nṛpaguṇairyuktaḥ kevalaṃ rūpavarjitaḥ  MatsP 
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
purūravā madrapatiḥ karmaṇā kena pārthivaḥ 
babhūva karmaṇā kena rūpavāṃścaiva sūtaja  MatsP 
sūta uvāca
dvijagrāme dvijaśreṣṭho nāmnā cāsītpurūravāḥ 
nadyāḥ kūle mahārājaḥ pūrvajanmani pārthivaḥ  MatsP 
sa tu madrapatī rājā yastu nāmnā purūravāḥ 
tasmiñjanmanyasau vipro dvādaśyāṃ tu sadānagha  MatsP 
upoṣya pūjayāmāsa rājyakāmo janārdanam 
cakāra sopavāsaśca snānam abhyaṅgapūrvakam  MatsP 
upavāsaphalātprāptaṃ rājyaṃ madreṣvakaṇṭakam 
upoṣitas tathābhyaṅgād rūpahīno vyajāyata  MatsP 
upoṣitairnarais tasmāt snānam abhyaṅgapūrvakam 
varjanīyaṃ prayatnena rūpaghnaṃ tatparaṃ nṛpa  MatsP 
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ yadvṛttaṃ pūrvajanmani 
madreśvaratvacaritaṃ śṛṇu tasya mahīpateḥ  MatsP

janānurāgo naivāsīd rūpahīnasya tasya vai  MatsP

śatasaṅkhyais tāpanīyaiḥ śṛṅgairdivamivollikhan 
śṛṅgavānsumahādivyo durgaḥ śailo mahācitaḥ  MatsP 
tasmingirau nivasati giriśo dhūmralohitaḥ 
tasya pādātprabhavati śailodaṃ nāma tatsaraḥ  MatsP 
tasmātprabhavate puṇyā nadī śailodakā śubhā 
sā cakṣusī tayormadhye praviṣṭā paścimodadhim  MatsP 
astyuttareṇa kailāsāc chivaḥ sarvauṣadho giriḥ 
gauraṃ tu parvataśreṣṭhaṃ haritālamayaṃ prati  MatsP 
hiraṇyaśṛṅgaḥ sumahādivyauṣadhimayo giriḥ 
tasya pāde mahaddivyaṃ saraḥ kāñcanavālukam  MatsP 
ramyaṃ bindusaro nāma yatra rājā bhagīrathaḥ 
gaṅgārthe sa tu rājarṣir uvāsa bahulāḥ samāḥ  MatsP 
divaṃ yāsyantu me pūrve gaṅgātoyāplutāsthikāḥ 
tatra tripathagā devī prathamaṃ tu pratiṣṭhitā  MatsP 
somapādātprasūtā sā saptadhā pravibhajyate 
yūpā maṇimayāstatra vimānāśca hiraṇmayāḥ  MatsP 
tatreṣṭvā kratubhiḥ siddhaḥ śakraḥ suragaṇaiḥ saha 
divyaśchāyāpathas tatra nakṣatrāṇāṃ tu maṇḍalam  MatsP 
dṛśyate bhāsurā rātrau devī tripathagā tu sā 
antarikṣaṃ divaṃ caiva bhāvayitvā bhuvaṃ gatā  MatsP 
bhavottamāṅge patitā saṃruddhā yogamāyayā 
tasyā ye bindavaḥ kecit kruddhāyāḥ patitā bhuvi  MatsP 
kṛtaṃ tu tairbahusaras tato bindusaraḥ smṛtam 
tatastasyā niruddhāyā bhavena sahasā ruṣā  MatsP 
jñātvā tasyā hyabhiprāyaṃ krūraṃ devyāścikīrṣitam 
bhittvā viśāmi pātālaṃ srotasā gṛhya śaṃkaram  MatsP 
athāvalepaṃ taṃ jñātvā tasyāḥ kruddhastu śaṃkaraḥ 
tirobhāvayituṃ buddhir āsīdaṅgeṣu tāṃ nadīm  MatsP 
etasminneva kāle tu dṛṣṭvā rājānamagrataḥ 
dhamanīsaṃtataṃ kṣīṇaṃ kṣudhāvyākulitendriyam  MatsP 
anena toṣitaścāhaṃ nadyarthe pūrvameva tu 
buddhvā'sya varadānaṃ tu tataḥ kopaṃ nyayacchata  MatsP 
brahmaṇo vacanaṃ śrutvā yaduktaṃ dhārayannadīm 
tato visarjayāmāsa saṃruddhāṃ svena tejasā  MatsP 
nadīṃ bhagīrathasyārthe tapasogreṇa toṣitaḥ 
tato visarjayāmāsa sapta srotāṃsi gaṅgayā  MatsP 
trīṇi prācīmabhimukhaṃ pratīcīṃ trīṇyathaiva tu 
srotāṃsi tripathāyāstu pratyapadyanta saptadhā  MatsP 
nalinī hlādinī caiva pāvanī caiva prācyagā 
sītā cakṣuśca sindhuśca tisrastā vai pratīcyagāḥ  MatsP 
saptamī tvanugā tāsāṃ dakṣiṇena bhagīratham 
tasmādbhāgīrathī sā vai praviṣṭā dakṣiṇodadhim  MatsP 
sapta caitāḥ plāvayanti varṣaṃ tu himasāhvayam 
prasūtāḥ sapta nadyastu śubhā bindusarodbhavāḥ  MatsP 
tāndeśānplāvayanti sma mlecchaprāyāṃśca sarvaśaḥ 
saśailānkukurānraudhrān barbarānyavanānkhasān  MatsP 
pulikāṃśca kulatthāṃśca aṅgalokyānvarāṃśca yān 
kṛtvā dvidhā himavantaṃ praviṣṭā dakṣiṇodadhim  MatsP 
atha vīramarūṃścaiva kālikāṃścaiva śūlikān 
tukarānbarbarākārān pahlavānpāradāñchakān  MatsP 
etāñjanapadāṃścakṣuḥ plāvayitvodadhiṃ gatā 
daradorjaguḍāṃścaiva gāndhārānaurasānkuhūn  MatsP 
śivapaurānindramarūn vasatīnsamatejasam 
saindhavānurvasānbarbān kupathānbhīmaromakān  MatsP 
śunāmukhāṃścordamarūn sindhuretānniṣevate 
gandharvānkinnarānyakṣān rakṣovidyādharoragān  MatsP 
kalāpagrāmakāṃścaiva tathā kimpuruṣānnarān 
kirātāṃśca pulindāṃśca kurūnvai bhāratānapi  MatsP 
pāñcālānkauśikānmatsyān māgadhāṅgāṃstathaiva ca 
brahmottarāṃśca vaṅgāṃśca tāmraliptāṃstathaiva ca  MatsP 
etāñjanapadānāryān gaṅgā bhāvayate śubhā 
tataḥ pratihatā vindhye praviṣṭā dakṣiṇodadhim  MatsP 
tatastu hlādinī puṇyā prācīnābhimukhī yayau 
plāvayantyupakāṃścaiva niṣādānapi sarvaśaḥ  MatsP 
dhīvarānṛṣikāṃścaiva tathā nalimukhānapi 
kekarānekakarṇāṃśca kirātānapi caiva hi  MatsP 
kālañjarānvikarṇāṃśca kuśikānsvargabhaumakān 
sā maṇḍale samudrasya tīre bhūtvā tu sarvaśaḥ  MatsP 
tatastu nalinī cāpi prācīmeva diśaṃ yayau 
kupathānplāvayantī sā indradyumnasarāṃsyapi  MatsP 
tathā kharapathāndeśān vetraśaṅkupathānapi 
madhyenojjānakamarūn kuthaprāvaraṇānyayau  MatsP 
indradvīpasamīpe tu praviṣṭā lavaṇodadhim 
tatastu pāvanī prāyāt prācīmāśāṃ javena tu  MatsP 
tomarānplāvayatī ca haṃsamārgānsamūhakān 
pūrvāndeśāṃśca sevantī bhittvā sā bahudhā girim 
karṇaprāvaraṇānprāpya gatā sāśvamukhānapi  MatsP 
siktvā parvatameruṃ sā gatvā vidyādharānapi 
śaimimaṇḍalakoṣṭhaṃ tu sā praviṣṭā mahatsaraḥ  MatsP 
tāsāṃ nadyupanadyo 'nyāḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ 
upagacchanti tā nadyo yato varṣati vāsavaḥ  MatsP 
tīre vaṃśaukasārāyāḥ surabhirnāma tadvanam 
hiraṇyaśṛṅgo vasati vidvānkauberako vaśī  MatsP 
yajñādapetaḥ sumahān amitaujāḥ suvikramaḥ 
tatrāgastyaiḥ parivṛtā vidvabhirdbrahmarākṣasaiḥ  MatsP 
kuberānucarā hyete catvārastatsamāśritāḥ 
evameva tu vijñeyā siddhiḥ parvatavāsinām  MatsP 
paraspareṇa dviguṇā dharmataḥ kāmato 'rthataḥ 
hemakūṭasya pṛṣṭhe tu sarpāṇāṃ tatsaraḥ smṛtam  MatsP 
sarasvatī prabhavati tasmājjyotiṣmatī tu yā 
avagāḍhe hyubhayataḥ samudrau pūrvapaścimau  MatsP 
saro viṣṇupadaṃ nāma niṣadhe parvatottame 
yasmādagre prabhavati gandharvānukule ca te  MatsP 
meroḥ pārśvātprabhavati hradaścandraprabho mahān 
jambūścaiva nadī puṇyā yasyāṃ jāmbūnadaṃ smṛtam  MatsP 
payodastu hrado nīlaḥ sa śubhraḥ puṇḍarīkavān 
puṇḍarīkātpayodācca tasmād dve samprasūyatām  MatsP 
sarasastu sarastvetat smṛtamuttaramānasam 
mṛgyā ca mṛgakāntā ca tasmād dve samprasūyatām  MatsP 
hradāḥ kuruṣu vikhyātāḥ padmamīnakulākulāḥ 
nāmnā te vai jayā nāma dvādaśodadhisaṃnibhāḥ  MatsP 
tebhyaḥ śāntī ca madhvī ca dve nadyau samprasūyatām 
kimpuruṣādyāni yānyaṣṭau teṣu devo na varṣati  MatsP 
udbhidānyudakānyatra pravahanti saridvarāḥ 
balāhakaśca ṛṣabho cakro maināka eva ca  MatsP 
viniviṣṭāḥ pratidiśaṃ nimagnā lavaṇāmbudhim 
candrakāntastathā droṇaḥ sumahāṃśca śiloccayaḥ  MatsP 
udgāyatā udīcyāṃ tu avagāḍhā mahodadhim 
cakro badhirakaścaiva tathā nāradaparvataḥ  MatsP 
pratīcīmāyatāste vai pratiṣṭhāste mahodadhim 
jīmūto drāvaṇaścaiva mainākaścandraparvataḥ  MatsP 
āyatāste mahāśailāḥ samudraṃ dakṣiṇaṃ prati 
cakramainākayormadhye divi san dakṣiṇāpathe  MatsP 
tatra saṃvartako nāma so 'gniḥ pibati tajjalam 
agniḥ samudravāsastu aurvo 'sau vaḍavāmukhaḥ  MatsP 
ityete parvatāviṣṭāś catvāro lavaṇodadhim 
chidyamāneṣu pakṣeṣu purā indrasya vai bhayāt  MatsP 
teṣāṃ tu dṛśyate candre śukle kṛṣṇe samāplutiḥ 
te bhāratasya varṣasya bhedā yena prakīrtitāḥ  MatsP 
ihoditasya dṛśyante anye tvanyatra coditāḥ 
uttarottarameteṣāṃ varṣam udricyate guṇaiḥ  MatsP 
ārogyāyuḥpramāṇābhyāṃ dharmataḥ kāmato 'rthataḥ 
samanvitāni bhūtāni teṣu varṣeṣu bhāgaśaḥ  MatsP 
vasanti nānājātīni teṣu sarveṣu tāni vai 
ityetaddhārayadviśvaṃ pṛthvī jagadidaṃ sthitā  MatsP 
MatsyaPurāṇa 
sūta uvāca
śākadvīpasya vakṣyāmi yathāvadiha niścayam 
kathyamānaṃ nibodha tvaṃ śākaṃ dvīpaṃ dvijottamāḥ  MatsP 
jambūdvīpasya vistārād dviguṇastasya vistaraḥ 
vistārāttriguṇaścāpi pariṇāhaḥ samantataḥ  MatsP 
tenāvṛtaḥ samudro 'yaṃ dvīpena lavaṇodadhiḥ 
tatra puṇyā janapadāś cirācca mriyate janaḥ  MatsP 
kuta eva ca durbhikṣaṃ kṣamātejoyuteṣviha 
tatrāpi parvatāḥ śubhrāḥ saptaiva maṇibhūṣitāḥ  MatsP 
śākadvīpādiṣu tveṣu sapta sapta nagās triṣu 
ṛjvāyatāḥ pratidiśaṃ niviṣṭā varṣaparvatāḥ  MatsP 
ratnākarādināmānaḥ sānumanto mahācitāḥ 
samoditāḥ pratidiśaṃ dvīpavistāramānataḥ  MatsP 
ubhayatrāvagāḍhau ca lavaṇakṣīrasāgarau 
śākadvīpe tu vakṣyāmi sapta divyānmahācalān  MatsP 
devarṣigandharvayutaḥ prathamo merurucyate 
prāgāyataḥ sa sauvarṇa udayo nāma parvataḥ  MatsP 
tatra meghāstu vṛṣṭyarthaṃ prabhavantyapayānti ca 
tasyāpareṇa sumahāñ jaladhāro mahāgiriḥ  MatsP 
sa vai candraḥ samākhyātaḥ sarvauṣadhisamanvitaḥ 
tasmānnityamupādatte vāsavaḥ paramaṃ jalam  MatsP 
nārado nāma caivokto durgaśailo mahācitaḥ 
tatrācalau samutpannau pūrvaṃ nāradaparvatau  MatsP 
tasyāpareṇa sumahāñ śyāmo nāma mahāgiriḥ 
yatra śyāmatvamāpannāḥ prajāḥ pūrvamimāḥ kila  MatsP 
sa eva dundubhirnāma śyāmaparvatasaṃnibhaḥ 
śabdamṛtyuḥ purā tasmin dundubhistāḍitaḥ suraiḥ  MatsP 
ratnamālāntaramayaḥ śālmalaścāntarālakṛt 
tasyāpareṇa rajato mahānasto giriḥ smṛtaḥ  MatsP 
sa vai somaka ityukto devairyatrāmṛtaṃ purā 
saṃbhṛtaṃ ca hṛtaṃ caiva māturarthe garutmatā  MatsP 
tasyāpare cāmbikeyaḥ sumanāścaiva sa smṛtaḥ 
hiraṇyākṣo varāheṇa tasmiñchaile niṣūditaḥ  MatsP 
āmbikeyātparo ramyaḥ sarvauṣadhiniṣevitaḥ 
vibhrājastu samākhyātaḥ sphāṭikastu mahāngiriḥ  MatsP 
yasmādvibhrājate vahnir vibhrājastena sa smṛtaḥ 
saiveha keśavetyukto yato vāyuḥ pravāti ca  MatsP 
teṣāṃ varṣāṇi vakṣyāmi parvatānāṃ dvijottamāḥ 
śṛṇudhvaṃ nāmatastāni yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ  MatsP 
dvināmānyeva varṣāṇi yathaiva girayastathā 
udayasyodayaṃ varṣaṃ jaladhāreti viśrutam  MatsP 
nāmnā gatabhayaṃ nāma varṣaṃ tatprathamaṃ smṛtam 
dvitīyaṃ jaladhārasya sukumāramiti smṛtam  MatsP 
tadeva śaiśiraṃ nāma varṣaṃ tatparikīrtitam 
nāradasya ca kaumāraṃ tadeva ca sukhodayam  MatsP 
śyāmaparvatavarṣaṃ tad anīcakam iti smṛtam 
ānandakamiti proktaṃ tadeva munibhiḥ śubham  MatsP 
somakasya śubhaṃ varṣaṃ vijñeyaṃ kusumotkaram 
tadevāsitam ityuktaṃ varṣaṃ somakasaṃjñitam  MatsP 
āmbikeyasya mainākaṃ kṣemakaṃ caiva tatkṛtam 
kesaraḥ parvatasyāpi mahādrumamiti smṛtam 
tadeva dhavamityuktaṃ varṣaṃ vibhrājasaṃjñitam  MatsP 
dvīpasya pariṇāhaṃ ca hrasvadīrghatvameva ca 
jambūdvīpena saṃkhyātaṃ tasya madhye vanaspatiḥ  MatsP 
śāko nāma mahāvṛkṣaḥ prajāstasya mahānugāḥ 
eteṣu devagandharvāḥ siddhāśca saha cāraṇaiḥ  MatsP 
viharanti ramante ca dṛśyamānāśca taiḥ saha 
tatra puṇyā janapadāś cāturvarṇyasamanvitāḥ  MatsP 
teṣu nadyaśca saptaiva prativarṣaṃ samudragāḥ 
dvināmnā caiva tāḥ sarvā gaṅgāḥ saptavidhāḥ smṛtāḥ  MatsP 
prathamā sukumārīti gaṅgā śivajalā śubhā 
munitaptā ca nāmnaiṣā nadī samparikīrtitā  MatsP 
sukumārī tapaḥsiddhā dvitīyā nāmataḥ satī 
nandā ca pāvanī caiva tṛtīyā parikīrtitā  MatsP 
śibikā ca caturthī syād dvividhā ca punaḥ smṛtā 
ikṣuśca pañcamī jñeyā tathaiva ca punaḥ kuhūḥ  MatsP 
veṇukā cāmṛtā caiva ṣaṣṭhī samparikīrtitā 
sukṛtā ca gabhastī ca saptamī parikīrtitā  MatsP 
etāḥ sapta mahābhāgāḥ prativarṣaṃ śivodakāḥ 
bhāvayanti janaṃ sarvaṃ śākadvīpanivāsinam  MatsP 
abhigacchanti tāścānyā nadā nadyaḥ sarāṃsi ca 
bahūdakaparisrāvā yato varṣati vāsavaḥ  MatsP 
tāsāṃ tu nāmadheyāni parimāṇaṃ tathaiva ca 
na śakyaṃ parisaṃkhyātuṃ puṇyāstāḥ sariduttamāḥ  MatsP 
tāḥ pibanti sadā hṛṣṭā nadīrjanapadāstu te 
ete śāntabhayāḥ proktāḥ pramodā ye ca vai śivāḥ  MatsP 
ānandāśca sukhāścaiva kṣemakāśca navaiḥ saha 
varṇāśramācārayutā deśāste sapta viśrutāḥ  MatsP 
ārogyā balinaścaiva sarve maraṇavarjitāḥ 
avasarpiṇī na teṣvasti tathaivotsarpiṇī punaḥ  MatsP 
na tatrāsti yugāvasthā caturyugakṛtā kvacit 
tretāyugasamaḥ kālas tathā tatra pravartate  MatsP 
śākadvīpādiṣu jñeyaṃ pañcasveteṣu sarvaśaḥ 
deśasya tu vicāreṇa kālaḥ svābhāvikaḥ smṛtaḥ  MatsP 
na teṣu saṃkaraḥ kaścid varṇāśramakṛtaḥ kvacit 
dharmasya cāvyabhīcārād ekāntasukhinaḥ prajāḥ  MatsP 
na teṣu māyā lobho vā īrṣyāsūyā bhayaṃ kutaḥ 
viparyayo na teṣvasti tadvai svābhāvikaṃ smṛtam  MatsP 
kālo naiva ca teṣvasti na daṇḍo na ca dāṇḍikaḥ 
svadharmeṇa ca dharmajñās te rakṣanti parasparam  MatsP 
parimaṇḍalastu sumahān dvīpo vai kuśasaṃjñakaḥ 
nadījalaiḥ parivṛtaḥ parvataścābhrasaṃnibhaiḥ  MatsP 
sarvadhātuvicitraiśca maṇividrumabhūṣitaiḥ 
anyaiśca vividhākārai ramyairjanapadaistathā  MatsP 
vṛkṣaiḥ puṣpaphalopetaiḥ sarvato dhanadhānyavān 
nityaṃ puṣpaphalopetaḥ sarvaratnasamāvṛtaḥ  MatsP 
āvṛtaḥ paśubhiḥ sarvair grāmyāraṇyaiśca sarvaśaḥ 
ānupūrvyātsamāsena kuśadvīpaṃ nibodhata  MatsP 
atha tṛtīyaṃ vakṣyāmi kuśadvīpaṃ ca kṛtsnaśaḥ 
kuśadvīpena kṣīrodaḥ sarvataḥ parivāritaḥ  MatsP 
śākadvīpasya vistārād dviguṇena samanvitaḥ 
tatrāpi parvatāḥ sapta vijñeyā ratnayonayaḥ  MatsP 
ratnākarāstathā nadyas teṣāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu 
dvināmānaśca te sarve śākadvīpe yathā tathā  MatsP 
prathamaḥ sūryasaṃkāśaḥ kumudo nāma parvataḥ 
vidrumoccaya ityuktaḥ sa eva ca mahīdharaḥ  MatsP 
sarvadhātumayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ śilājālasamanvitaiḥ 
dvitīyaḥ parvatastatra unnato nāma viśrutaḥ  MatsP 
hemaparvata ityuktaḥ sa eva ca mahīdharaḥ 
haritālamayaiḥ śṛṅgair dvīpamāvṛtya sarvaśaḥ  MatsP 
balāhakastṛtīyastu jātyañjanamayo giriḥ 
dyutimānnāmataḥ proktaḥ sa eva ca mahīdharaḥ  MatsP 
caturthaḥ parvato droṇo yatrauṣadhyo mahāgirau 
viśalyakaraṇī caiva mṛtasaṃjīvanī tathā  MatsP 
puṣpavānnāma saivoktaḥ parvataḥ sumahācitaḥ 
kaṅkastu pañcamasteṣāṃ parvato nāma sāravān  MatsP 
kuśeśaya iti proktaḥ punaḥ sa pṛthivīdharaḥ 
divyapuṣpaphalopeto divyavirutsamanvitaḥ  MatsP 
ṣaṣṭhastu parvatastatra mahiṣo meghasaṃnibhaḥ 
sa eva tu punaḥ prokto harirityabhiviśrutaḥ  MatsP 
tasminso 'gnirnivasati mahiṣo nāma yo 'psujaḥ 
saptamaḥ parvatastatra kakudmānsa hi bhāṣate  MatsP 
mandaraḥ saiva vijñeyaḥ sarvadhātumayaḥ śubhaḥ 
manda ityeṣa yo dhātur apāmarthe prakāśakaḥ  MatsP 
apāṃ vidāraṇāccaiva mandaraḥ sa nigadyate 
tatra ratnānyanekāni svayaṃ rakṣati vāsavaḥ  MatsP 
prajāpatimupādāya prajābhyo vidadhatsvayam 
teṣāmantaraviṣkambho dviguṇaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ  MatsP 
ityete parvatāḥ sapta kuśadvīpe prabhāṣitāḥ 
teṣāṃ varṣāṇi vakṣyāmi saptaiva tu vibhāgaśaḥ  MatsP 
kumudasya smṛtaḥ śveta unnataśceva sa smṛtaḥ 
unnatasya tu vijñeyaṃ varṣaṃ lohitasaṃjñakam  MatsP 
veṇumaṇḍalakaṃ caiva tathaiva parikīrtitam 
balāhakasya jīmūtaḥ svairathākāramityapi  MatsP 
droṇasya harikaṃ nāma lavaṇaṃ ca punaḥ smṛtam 
kaṅkasyāpi kakun nāma dhṛtimaccaiva tatsmṛtam  MatsP 
mahiṣaṃ mahiṣasyāpi punaścāpi prabhākaram 
kakudminastu tadvarṣaṃ kapilaṃ nāma viśrutam  MatsP 
etānyapi viśiṣṭāni sapta sapta pṛthakpṛthak 
varṣāṇi parvatāścaiva nadīsteṣu nibodhata  MatsP 
tatrāpi nadyaḥ saptaiva prativarṣaṃ hi tāḥ smṛtāḥ 
dvināmavatyastāḥ sarvāḥ sarvāḥ puṇyajalāḥ smṛtāḥ  MatsP 
dhūtapāpā nadī nāma yoniścaiva punaḥ smṛtā 
sītā dvitīyā vijñeyā sā caiva hi niśā smṛtā  MatsP 
pavitrā tṛtīyā vijñeyā vitṛṣṇāpi ca yā punaḥ 
caturthī hlādinītyuktā candrabhā iti ca smṛtā  MatsP 
vidyucca pañcamī proktā śuklā caiva vibhāvyate 
puṇḍrā ṣaṣṭhī tu vijñeyā punaścaiva vibhāvarī  MatsP 
mahatī saptamī proktā punaścaiṣā dhṛtiḥ smṛtā 
anyāstābhyo 'pi saṃjātāḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ  MatsP 
abhigacchanti tā nadyo yato varṣati vāsavaḥ 
ityeṣa saṃniveśo vaḥ kuśadvīpasya varṇitaḥ  MatsP 
śākadvīpena vistāraḥ proktastasya sanātanaḥ 
kuśadvīpaḥ samudreṇa ghṛtamaṇḍodakena ca  MatsP 
sarvataḥ sumahāndvīpaś candravatpariveṣṭitaḥ 
vistārānmaṇḍalāccaiva kṣīrodāddviguṇo mataḥ  MatsP 
tataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi krauñcadvīpaṃ yathā tathā 
kuśadvīpasya vistārād dviguṇastasya vistaraḥ  MatsP 
ghṛtodakaḥ samudro vai krauñcadvīpena saṃvṛtaḥ 
cakranemipramāṇena vṛto vṛttena sarvaśaḥ  MatsP 
tasmindvīpe nagāḥ śreṣṭhā devano girirucyate 
devanātparataścāpi govindo nāma parvataḥ  MatsP 
govindātparataścāpi krauñcastu prathamo giriḥ 
krauñcātpare pāvanakaḥ pāvanādandhakārakaḥ  MatsP 
andhakārātpare cāpi devāvṛn nāma parvataḥ 
devāvṛtaḥ pareṇāpi puṇḍarīko mahāngiriḥ  MatsP 
ete ratnamayāḥ sapta krauñcadvīpasya parvatāḥ 
parasparasya dviguṇo viṣkambho varṣaparvataḥ  MatsP 
varṣāṇi tasya vakṣyāmi nāmatastu nibodhata 
krauñcasya kuśalo deśo vāmanasya manonugaḥ  MatsP 
manonugātpare coṣṇās tṛtīyo 'pi sa ucyate 
uṣṇātpare pāvanakaḥ pāvanādandhakārakaḥ  MatsP 
andhakārakadeśāttu munideśastathā paraḥ 
munideśātpare cāpi procyate dundubhisvanaḥ  MatsP 
siddhacāraṇasaṃkīrṇo gauraprāyaḥ śucirjanaḥ 
śrutāstatraiva nadyastu prativarṣaṃ gatāḥ śubhāḥ  MatsP 
gaurī kumudvatī caiva saṃdhyā rātrirmanojavā 
khyātī ca puṇḍarīkā ca gaṅgā saptavidhā smṛtā  MatsP 
tāsāṃ sahasraśaścānyā nadyaḥ pārśvasamīpagāḥ 
abhigacchanti tā nadyo bahulāśca bahūdakāḥ  MatsP 
teṣāṃ nisargo deśānām ānupūrvyeṇa sarvaśaḥ 
na śakyo vistarādvaktum api varṣaśatairapi  MatsP 
sargo yaśca prajānāṃ tu saṃhāro yaśca teṣu vai 
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi śālmalasya nibodhata  MatsP 
śālmalo dviguṇo dvīpaḥ krauñcadvīpasya vistarāt 
parivārya samudraṃ tu dadhimaṇḍodakaṃ sthitaḥ  MatsP 
tatra puṇyā janapadāś cirācca mriyate janaḥ 
kuta eva tu durbhikṣaṃ kṣamātejoyutā hi te  MatsP 
prathamaḥ sūryasaṃkāśaḥ sumanā nāma parvataḥ 
pītastu madhyamaścāsīt tataḥ kumbhamayo giriḥ  MatsP 
nāmnā sarvasukho nāma divyauṣadhisamanvitaḥ 
tṛtīyaścaiva sauvarṇo bhṛṅgapattranibho giriḥ  MatsP 
sumahānrohito nāma divyo girivaro hi saḥ 
sumanāḥ kuśalo deśaḥ sukhodarkaḥ sukhodayaḥ  MatsP 
rohito yastṛtīyastu rohiṇo nāma viśrutaḥ 
tatra ratnānyanekāni svayaṃ rakṣati vāsavaḥ  MatsP 
prajāpatimupādāya prasanno vidadhatsvayam 
na tatra meghā varṣanti śītoṣṇaṃ ca na tadvidham  MatsP 
varṇāśramāṇāṃ vārttā vā triṣu dvīpeṣu vidyate 
na graho na ca candro 'sti īrṣyāsūyā bhayaṃ tathā  MatsP 
udbhidānyudakānyatra giriprasravaṇāni ca 
bhojanaṃ ṣaḍrasaṃ tatra teṣāṃ svayamupasthitam  MatsP 
adhamottamaṃ na teṣvasti na lobho na parigrahaḥ 
ārogyabalavantaśca ekāntasukhino narāḥ  MatsP 
triṃśadvarṣasahasrāṇi mānasīṃ siddhimāsthitāḥ 
sukhamāyuśca rūpaṃ ca dharmaiśvaryaṃ tathaiva ca  MatsP 
śālmalānteṣu vijñeyaṃ dvīpeṣu triṣu sarvataḥ 
vyākhyātaḥ śālmalāntānāṃ dvīpānāṃ tu vidhiḥ śubhaḥ  MatsP 
parimaṇḍalastu dvīpasya cakravatpariveṣṭitaḥ 
surodena samudreṇa dviguṇena samanvitaḥ  MatsP

gomedakaṃ pravakṣyāmi ṣaṣṭhaṃ dvīpaṃ tapodhanāḥ 
surodakasamudrastu gomedena samāvṛtaḥ  MatsP 
śālmalasya tu vistārād dviguṇastasya vistaraḥ 
tasmindvīpe tu vijñeyau parvatau dvau samāhitau  MatsP 
prathamaḥ sumanā nāma jātyañjanamayo giriḥ 
dvitīyaḥ kumudo nāma sarvauṣadhisamanvitaḥ  MatsP 
śātakaumbhamayaḥ śrīmān vijñeyaḥ sumahācitaḥ 
samudrekṣurasodena vṛto gomedakaśca saḥ  MatsP 
ṣaṣṭhena tu samudreṇa surodāddviguṇena ca 
dhātakīkumudaścaiva havyaputrau suvistṛtau  MatsP 
saumanaṃ prathamaṃ varṣaṃ dhātakīkhaṇḍamucyate 
dhātakinaḥ smṛtaṃ tadvai prathamaṃ prathamasya tu  MatsP 
gomedaṃ yatsmṛtaṃ varṣaṃ nāmnā sarvasukhaṃ tu tat 
kumudasya dvitīyasya dvitīyaṃ kumudaṃ tataḥ  MatsP 
etau dvau parvatau vṛttau śeṣau sarvasamucchritau

dakṣiṇārdhaṃ tu dvīpasya dhātakīkhaṇḍamucyate  MatsP

etau janapadau dvau tu gomedasya tu vistṛtau  MatsP

ūrdhvaṃ sa vai caturviṃśadyojanānāṃ mahābalaḥ  MatsP

tasya putro mahāvītaḥ paścimārdhasya rakṣitā  MatsP 
pūrvārdhe parvatasyāpi dvidhā deśastu sa smṛtaḥ 
svādūdakenodadhinā puṣkaraḥ parivāritaḥ  MatsP

triṃśadvarṣasahasrāṇi teṣu jīvanti mānavāḥ  MatsP 
viparyayo na teṣvasti etatsvābhāvikaṃ smṛtam 
ārogyaṃ sukhabāhulyaṃ mānasīṃ siddhimāsthitāḥ  MatsP 
sukhamāyuśca rūpaṃ ca triṣu dvīpeṣu sarvaśaḥ 
adhamottamau na teṣvāstāṃ tulyāste vīryarūpataḥ  MatsP 
na tatra vadhyavadhakau nerṣyāsūyā bhayaṃ tathā 
na lobho na ca dambho vā na ca dveṣaḥ parigrahaḥ  MatsP 
satyānṛte na teṣvāstāṃ dharmādharmau tathaiva ca 
varṇāśramāṇāṃ vārttā ca pāśupālyaṃ vaṇikkṛṣiḥ  MatsP 
trayīvidyā daṇḍanītiḥ śuśrūṣā daṇḍa eva ca

sargastu dhātakīkhaṇḍe mahāvīte tathaiva ca  MatsP

dvīpasyānantaro yastu samudrastatsamastu vai  MatsP 
evaṃ dvīpasamudrāṇāṃ vṛddhirjñeyā parasparam 
apāṃ caiva samudrekāt samudra iti saṃjñitaḥ  MatsP 
ṛṣadvasantyo varṣeṣu prajā yatra caturvidhāḥ 
ṛṣiratyeva ramaṇe varṣantvetena teṣu vai  MatsP

udayātpayasāṃ yogāt puṣpanty āpo yathā svayam

daśottarāṇi pañcāhur aṅgulānāṃ śatāni ca  MatsP

bhojanaṃ cāprayatnena sadā svayamupasthitam  MatsP

ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi sūryacandramasorgatim 
sūryācandramasāvetau bhrājantau yāvadeva tu  MatsP 
saptadvīpasamudrāṇāṃ dvīpānāṃ bhāti vistaraḥ 
vistarārdhaṃ pṛthivyāstu bhavedanyatra bāhyataḥ  MatsP 
paryāsaparimāṇaṃ ca candrādityau prakāśataḥ 
paryāsapārimāṇyāttu budhaistulyaṃ divaḥ smṛtam  MatsP 
trīṃllokānprati sāmānyāt sūryo yātyavilambataḥ 
acirāttu prakāśena avanāttu raviḥ smṛtaḥ  MatsP 
bhūyo bhūyaḥ pravakṣyāmi pramāṇaṃ candrasūryayoḥ 
mahitatvānmahacchabdo hy asminnarthe nigadyate  MatsP 
asya bhāratavarṣasya viṣkambhāttulyavistṛtam 
maṇḍalaṃ bhāskarasyātha yojanaistannibodhata  MatsP 
navayojanasāhasro vistāro maṇḍalasya tu 
vistārāttriguṇaścāpi pariṇāho 'tra maṇḍale  MatsP

ataḥ pṛthivyā vakṣyāmi pramāṇaṃ yojanaiḥ punaḥ  MatsP 
saptadvīpasamudrāyā vistāro maṇḍalasya tu 
ityetadiha saṃkhyātaṃ purāṇe parimāṇataḥ  MatsP 
tadvakṣyāmi prasaṃkhyāya sāmprataṃ cābhimānibhiḥ 
abhimānino hyatītā ye tulyāste sāmprataistviha  MatsP 
devādevair atītāstu rūpairnāmabhireva ca 
tasmādvai sāmpratairdevair vakṣyāmi vasudhātalam  MatsP 
divyasya saṃniveśo vai sāmprataireva kṛtsnaśaḥ 
śatārdhakoṭivistārā pṛthivī kṛtsnaśaḥ smṛtā  MatsP 
tasyāścārdhapramāṇaṃ ca meroścaivottarottaram

tathā śatasahasrāṇām ekonanavatiṃ punaḥ 
pañcāśacca sahasrāṇi pṛthivyardhasya vistaraḥ  MatsP 
pṛthivyā vistaraṃ kṛtyaṃ yojanaistaṃ nibodhata 
tisraḥ koṭyastu vistārāt saṃkhyātāstu caturdiśam  MatsP 
tathā śatasahasrāṇām ekonāśītir ucyate 
saptadvīpasamudrāyāḥ pṛthivyāḥ sa tu vistaraḥ  MatsP 
vistāraṃ triguṇaṃ caiva pṛthivyantaramaṇḍalam 
gaṇitaṃ yojanānāṃ tu koṭyastvekādaśa smṛtāḥ  MatsP 
tathā śatasahasrāṇāṃ saptatriṃśādhikāstu tāḥ 
ityetadvai prasaṃkhyātaṃ pṛthivyantaramaṇḍalam  MatsP 
tārakāsaṃniveśasya divi yāvattu maṇḍalam 
paryāptasaṃniveśasya bhūmestāvattu maṇḍalam  MatsP 
paryāsaparimāṇaṃ ca bhūmestulyaṃ divaḥ smṛtam 
meroḥ prācyāṃ diśāyāṃ tu mānasottaramūrdhani  MatsP 
vastvekasārā māhendrī puṇyā hemapariṣkṛtā 
dakṣiṇena punarmeror mānasasya tu pṛṣṭhataḥ  MatsP 
vaivasvato nivasati yamaḥ saṃyamane pure 
pratīcyāṃ tu punarmeror mānasasya tu mūrdhani  MatsP 
suṣā nāma purī ramyā varuṇasyāpi dhīmataḥ 
diśyuttarasyāṃ merostu mānasasyaiva mūrdhani  MatsP 
tulyā mahendrapuryāpi somasyāpi vibhāvarī 
mānasottarapṛṣṭhe tu lokapālāścaturdiśam  MatsP 
sthitā dharmavyavasthārthaṃ lokasaṃrakṣaṇāya ca 
lokapālopariṣṭāttu sarvato dakṣiṇāyane  MatsP 
kāṣṭhāgatasya sūryasya gatistatra nibodhata 
dakṣiṇopakrame sūryaḥ kṣipteṣuriva sarpati  MatsP 
jyotiṣāṃ cakramādāya satataṃ parigacchati 
madhyagaścāmarāvatyāṃ yadā bhavati bhāskaraḥ  MatsP

suṣāyāmardharātrastu vibhāvaryāstam eti ca  MatsP 
vaivasvate saṃyamane madhyāhne tu raviryadā

vibhāvaryāmardharātraṃ māhendryāmastameva ca 
suṣāyāmatha vāruṇyāṃ madhyāhne tu raviryadā  MatsP 
vibhāvaryāṃ somapuryām uttiṣṭhati vibhāvasuḥ 
mahendrasyāmarāvatyām udgacchati divākaraḥ  MatsP 
ardharātraṃ saṃyamane vāruṇyāmastameti ca 
sa śīghrameva paryeti bhānurālātacakravat  MatsP 
bhramanvai bhramamāṇāni ṛkṣāṇi carate raviḥ 
evaṃ caturṣu pārśveṣu dakṣiṇānteṣu sarpati  MatsP 
udayāstamaye vāsāv uttiṣṭhati punaḥ punaḥ 
pūrvāhṇe cāparāhṇe ca dvau dvau devālayau tu saḥ  MatsP 
patatyekaṃ tu madhyāhne bhābhireva ca raśmibhiḥ 
udito vardhamānābhir madhyāhne tapate raviḥ  MatsP 
ataḥ paraṃ hrasantībhir gobhirastaṃ sa gacchati 
udayāstamayābhyāṃ ca smṛte pūrvāpare tu vai  MatsP 
yādṛkpurastāttapati yādṛkpṛṣṭhe tu pārśvayoḥ 
yatrodayastu dṛśyeta teṣāṃ sa udayaḥ smṛtaḥ  MatsP 
praṇāśaṃ gacchate yatra teṣāmastaḥ sa ucyate 
sarveṣāmuttare merur lokālokasya dakṣiṇe  MatsP 
vidūrabhāvādarkasya bhūmereṣā gatasya ca 
śrayante raśmayo yasmāt tena rātrau na dṛśyate  MatsP 
ūrdhvaṃ śatasahasrāṃśuḥ sthitastatra pradṛśyate 
evaṃ puṣkaramadhye tu yadā bhavati bhāskaraḥ  MatsP 
triṃśadbhāgaṃ ca medinyā muhūrtena sa gacchati 
yojanānāṃ sahasrasya imāṃ saṃkhyāṃ nibodhata  MatsP 
pūrṇaṃ śatasahasrāṇām ekatriṃśacca sā smṛtā 
pañcāśacca sahasrāṇi tathānyānyadhikāni ca  MatsP 
mauhūrtikī gatirhyeṣā sūryasya tu vidhīyate 
etena kramayogeṇa yadā kāṣṭhāṃ tu dakṣiṇām  MatsP 
parigacchati sūryo 'sau māsaṃ kāṣṭhāmudagdināt 
madhyena puṣkarasyātha bhramate dakṣiṇāyane  MatsP 
mānasottaramerostu antaraṃ triguṇaṃ smṛtam

nava koṭyaḥ prasaṃkhyātā yojanaiḥ parimaṇḍalam 
tathā śatasahasrāṇi catvāriṃśacca pañca ca  MatsP 
ahorātrātpataṃgasya gatireṣā vidhīyate

tathā śatasahasrāṇi viṃśatyekādhikāni tu  MatsP

uttarāyāḥ pramāṇaṃ tu kāṣṭhāyā maṇḍalasya tu

nāgavīthyuttarā vīthī hy ajavīthis tu dakṣiṇā 
ubhe āṣāḍhamūlaṃ tu ajavīthyādayas trayaḥ  MatsP

rohiṇyārdrā mṛgaśiro nāgavīthir iti smṛtā

tisrastu vīthayo hyetā uttaro mārga ucyate 
pūrvottarā ca phalgunyau maghā caivārṣabhī bhavet  MatsP 
pūrvottaraproṣṭhapadau govīthī revatī smṛtā 
śravaṇaṃ ca dhaniṣṭhā ca vāruṇaṃ ca jaradgavam  MatsP

hastaścitrā tathā svātī hy ajavīthiriti smṛtā  MatsP 
jyeṣṭhā viśākhā maitraṃ ca mṛgavīthī tathocyate 
mūlaṃ pūrvottarāṣāḍhe vīthī vaiśvānarī bhavet  MatsP 
smṛtāstisrastu vīthyastā mārge vai dakṣiṇe punaḥ 
kāṣṭhayorantaraṃ caitad vakṣyate yojanaiḥ punaḥ  MatsP

kāṣṭhayorlekhayoścaiva ayane dakṣiṇottare  MatsP 
te vakṣyāmi prasaṃkhyāya yojanaistu nibodhata 
ekaikamantaraṃ tadvad yuktānyetāni saptabhiḥ  MatsP

pramāṇaṃ maṇḍalasyāpi yojanānāṃ nibodhata

adhikānyaṣṭapañcāśad yojanāni tu vai punaḥ 
viṣkambho maṇḍalasyaiva tiryaksa tu vidhīyate  MatsP

sūryo dvādaśabhiḥ śīghraṃ muhūrtairdakṣiṇāyane 
trayodaśārdhamṛkṣāṇāṃ madhye carati maṇḍalam  MatsP 
muhūrtaistāni ṛkṣāṇi naktamaṣṭādaśaiścaran

udagyāne tathā sūryaḥ sarpate mandavikramaḥ 
tasmāddīrgheṇa kālena bhūmiṃ so 'lpāṃ prasarpati  MatsP 
sūryo 'ṣṭādaśabhirahno muhūrtairudagāyane 
trayodaśānāṃ madhye tu ṛkṣāṇāṃ carate raviḥ 
muhūrtaistāni ṛkṣāṇi rātrau dvādaśabhiścaran  MatsP

mṛtpiṇḍa iva madhyastho bhramate 'sau dhruvastathā  MatsP 
muhūrtaistriṃśatā tāvad ahorātraṃ bhuvo bhraman 
ubhayoḥ kāṣṭhayormadhye bhramate maṇḍalāni tu  MatsP 
uttarakramaṇe 'rkasya divā mandagatiḥ smṛtā

nakṣatracandrasūryāśca grahāstārāgaṇaiḥ saha  MatsP 
abhyantare prakāśante lokālokasya vai gireḥ 
etāvāneva lokastu nirālokastataḥ param  MatsP

sūta uvāca

tadā so 'bhyantare sūryo bhramate maṇḍalāni tu  MatsP 
aśītimaṇḍalaśataṃ kāṣṭhayorubhayoścaran 
dhruveṇa mucyamānena punā raśmiyugena ca  MatsP 
tathaiva bāhyataḥ sūryo bhramate maṇḍalāni tu 
udveṣṭayanvai vegena maṇḍalāni tu gacchati  MatsP 
MatsyaPurāṇa 
sūta uvāca
sa ratho 'dhiṣṭhito devair māsi māsi yathākramam 
tato vahatyathādityaṃ bahubhir ṛṣibhiḥ saha  MatsP 
gandharvairapsarobhiśca sarpagrāmaṇirākṣasaiḥ 
ete vasanti vai sūrye māsau dvau dvau krameṇa ca  MatsP 
dhātāryamā pulastyaśca pulahaśca prajāpatī 
uragau vāsukiścaiva saṃkīrṇaścaiva tāvubhau  MatsP 
tumburur nāradaścaiva gandharvau gāyatāṃ varau 
kṛtasthalāpsarāścaiva yā ca sā puñjikasthalā  MatsP 
grāmaṇyau rathakṛttasya rathaujāścaiva tāvubhau 
rakṣo hetiḥ prahetiśca yātudhānāvubhau ṛtau  MatsP 
madhumādhavayorhyeṣa gaṇo vasati bhāskare 
vasangrīṣme tu dvau māsau mitraśca varuṇaśca vai  MatsP 
ṛṣī atrirvasiṣṭhaśca nāgau takṣakarambhakau 
menakā sahajanyā ca hāhā hūhūśca gāyakau  MatsP 
rathaṃtaraśca grāmaṇyau rathakṛccaiva tāvubhau 
puruṣādo vadhaścaiva yātudhānau tu tau smṛtau  MatsP 
ete vasanti vai sūrye māsayoḥ śuciśukrayoḥ 
tataḥ sūrye punaścānyā nivasanti sma devatāḥ  MatsP 
indraścaiva vivasvāṃśca aṅgirā bhṛgureva ca 
elāpattrastathā sarpaḥ śaṅkhapālaśca pannagaḥ  MatsP 
viśvāvasusuṣeṇau ca prātaścaiva rathaśca hi 
pramlocetyapsarāścaiva nimrocantī ca te ubhe  MatsP 
yātudhānastathā hetir vyāghraścaiva tu tāvubhau 
nabhasyanabhasoretair vasantaśca divākare  MatsP 
māsau dvau devatāḥ sūrye vasanti ca śaradṛtau 
parjanyaścaiva pūṣā ca bharadvājaḥ sagautamaḥ  MatsP 
citrasenaśca gandharvas tathā vā suruciśca yaḥ 
viśvācī ca ghṛtācī ca ubhe te puṇyalakṣaṇe  MatsP 
nāgaścairāvataścaiva viśrutaśca dhanaṃjayaḥ 
senajicca suṣeṇaśca senānīr grāmaṇīs tathā  MatsP 
cāro vātaśca dvāvetau yātudhānāvubhau smṛtau 
vasantyete ca vai sūrye māsayośca tviṣorjayoḥ  MatsP 
haimantikau ca dvau māsau nivasanti divākare 
aṃśo bhagaśca dvāvetau kaśyapaśca kratuśca tau  MatsP 
bhujaṃgaśca mahāpadmaḥ sarpaḥ karkoṭakastathā 
citrasenaśca gandharvaḥ pūrṇāyuścaiva gāyanau  MatsP 
apsarāḥ pūrvacittiśca gandharvā hyurvaśī ca yā 
tārkṣyaścāriṣṭanemiśca senānīr grāmaṇīś ca tau  MatsP 
vidyutsūryaśca tāvugrau yātudhānau tu tau smṛtau 
sahe caiva sahasye ca vasantyete divākare  MatsP 
tatastu śiśire cāpi māsayornivasanti te 
tvaṣṭā viṣṇurjamadagnir viśvāmitrastathaiva ca  MatsP 
kādraveyau tathā nāgau kambalāśvatarāvubhau 
gandharvau dhṛtarāṣṭraśca sūryavarcāśca tāvubhau  MatsP 
tilottamāpsarāścaiva devī rambhā manoramā 
grāmaṇīr ṛtajiccaiva satyajicca mahābalaḥ  MatsP 
brahmopetaśca vai rakṣo yajñopetastathaiva ca 
ityete nivasanti sma dvau dvau māsau divākare  MatsP 
sthānābhimānino hyete gaṇā dvādaśa saptakāḥ 
sūryamāpādayantyete tejasā teja uttamam  MatsP 
grathitaistu vacobhiśca stuvanti ṛṣayo ravim 
gandharvāpsarasaścaiva gītanṛtyairupāsate  MatsP 
vidyāgrāmaṇino yakṣāḥ kurvantyābhīṣusaṃgraham 
sarpāḥ sarpanti vai sūrye yātudhānānuyānti ca  MatsP 
vālakhilyā nayantyastaṃ parivāryodayādravim 
eteṣāmeva devānāṃ yathāvīryaṃ yathātapaḥ  MatsP 
yathāyogaṃ yathādharmaṃ yathātattvaṃ yathābalam 
tathā tapatyasau sūryas teṣāmiddhastu tejasā  MatsP 
bhūtānāmaśubhaṃ sarvaṃ vyapohati svatejasā 
mānavānāṃ śubhairhyetair hriyate duritaṃ tu vai  MatsP 
duritaṃ śubhacārāṇāṃ vyapohanti kvacitkvacit 
ete sahaiva sūryeṇa bhramanti sānugā divi  MatsP 
tapantaśca japantaśca hlādayantaśca vai prajāḥ 
gopāyanti sma bhūtāni īhante hyanukampayā  MatsP 
sthānābhimānināṃ hyetat sthānaṃ manvantareṣu vai 
atītānāgatānāṃ ca vartante sāmprataṃ ca ye  MatsP 
evaṃ vasanti vai sūrye saptakāste caturdaśa 
caturdaśeṣu vartante gaṇā manvantareṣu vai  MatsP 
grīṣme hime ca varṣāsu muñcamānā yathākramam 
dharmaṃ himaṃ ca varṣaṃ ca yathākramamaharniśam  MatsP 
gacchatyasāvanudinaṃ parivṛtya raśmīn devānpitṝṃśca manujāṃśca sutarpayanvai 
śukle ca kṛṣṇe tadahaḥkrameṇa kālakṣaye caiva surāḥ pibanti  MatsP 
māsena taccāmṛtamasya mṛṣṭaṃ suvṛṣṭaye raśmiṣu rakṣitaṃ tu 
sarve 'mṛtaṃ tatpitaraḥ pibanti devāśca saumyāśca tathaiva kāvyāḥ  MatsP 
sūryeṇa gobhirhi vivardhitābhir adbhiḥ punaścaiva samucchritābhiḥ 
vṛṣṭyābhivṛṣṭābhir athauṣadhībhir martyā athānnena kṣudhaṃ jayanti  MatsP 
tṛptiśca tenārdhamāsaṃ surāṇāṃ māsaṃ sudhābhiḥ svadhayā pitṝṇām 
annena jīvantyaniśaṃ manuṣyāḥ sūryaḥ śritaṃ taddhi bibharti gobhiḥ  MatsP 
ityeṣa ekacakreṇa sūryastūrṇaṃ prasarpati 
tatra tairakramairaśvaiḥ sarpate 'sau dinakṣaye  MatsP 
harir haridbhir hriyate turaṃgamaiḥ pibatyathāpo haribhiḥ sahasradhā 
punaḥ pramuñcatyatha tāśca yo hariḥ sa muhyamāno haribhisturaṃgamaiḥ  MatsP 
ahorātraṃ rathenāsāv ekacakreṇa vai bhraman 
saptadvīpasamudrāṃśca saptabhiḥ saptabhirdrutam  MatsP 
chandorūpaiśca tairaśvair yutaścakraṃ tataḥ sthitiḥ 
kāmarūpaiḥ sakṛdyuktaiḥ kāmagaistairmanojavaiḥ  MatsP 
haritairavyathaiḥ piṅgair īśvarair brahmavādibhiḥ 
bāhyato 'nantaraṃ caiva maṇḍalaṃ divasakramāt  MatsP 
kalpādau samprayuktāśca vahantyābhūtasaṃplavam 
āvṛto vālakhilyaiśca bhramate rātryahāni tu  MatsP 
grathitaiḥ svavacobhiśca stūyamāno maharṣibhiḥ 
sevyate gītanṛtyaiśca gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ  MatsP 
pataṃgaiḥ patagairaśvair bhrāmyamāṇo divaspatiḥ 
vīthyāśrayāṇi carati nakṣatrāṇi tathā śaśī  MatsP 
hrāsavṛddhī tathaivāsya raśmayaḥ sūryavatsmṛtāḥ 
tricakrobhayato 'śvaśca vijñeyaḥ śaśino rathaḥ  MatsP 
apāṃ garbhasamutpanno rathaḥ sāśvaḥ sasārathiḥ 
sahāraistaistribhiścakrair yuktaḥ śuklairhayottamaiḥ  MatsP 
daśabhisturagairdivyair asaṅgais tanmanojavaiḥ 
sakṛdyukte rathe tasmin vahantastvāyugakṣayam  MatsP 
saṃgṛhītā rathe tasmiñ chvetaścakṣuḥśravāśca vai 
aśvāstamekavarṇāste vahante śaṅkhavarcasaḥ  MatsP 
ajaśca tripathaścaiva vṛṣo vājī naro hayaḥ 
aṃśumān saptadhātuśca haṃso vyomamṛgastathā  MatsP 
ityete nāmabhiścaiva daśa candramaso hayāḥ 
evaṃ candramasaṃ devaṃ vahanti smāyugakṣayam  MatsP 
devaiḥ parivṛtaḥ somaḥ pitṛbhiḥ saha gacchati 
somasya śuklapakṣādau bhāskare parataḥ sthite  MatsP 
āpūryate paro bhāgaḥ somasya tu ahaḥkramāt 
tataḥ pītakṣayaṃ somaṃ yupagadvyāpayan raviḥ  MatsP 
pītaṃ pañcadaśāhaṃ ca raśminaikena bhāskaraḥ 
āpūrayandadau tena bhāgaṃ bhāgamahaḥkramāt  MatsP 
suṣumnāpyayamānasya śukle vardhanti vai kalāḥ 
tasmāddhrasanti vai kṛṣṇe śukle hyāpyāyayanti ca  MatsP 
ityevaṃ sūryavīryeṇa candrasyāpyāyate tanuḥ 
paurṇamāsyāṃ pradṛśyeta śuklaḥ sampūrṇamaṇḍalaḥ  MatsP 
evamāpyāyate somaḥ śuklapakṣeṣvahaḥkramāt 
tato dvitīyāprabhṛti bahulasya caturdaśī  MatsP 
apāṃ sāramayasyendo rasamātrātmakasya ca 
pibantyambumayaṃ devā madhu saumyaṃ tathāmṛtam  MatsP 
saṃbhṛtaṃ tvardhamāsena amṛtaṃ sūryatejasā 
bhakṣārthamāgataṃ somaṃ paurṇamāsyāmupāsate  MatsP 
ekarātraṃ surāḥ sārdhaṃ pitṛbhirṛṣibhiśca vai 
somasya kṛṣṇapakṣādau bhāskarābhimukhasya vai  MatsP 
prakṣīyate pare hyātmā pīyamānakalākramāt 
trayaśca triṃśatā sārdhaṃ trayastriṃśacchatāni tu  MatsP 
trayastriṃśatsahasrāṇi devāḥ somaṃ pibanti vai 
ityevaṃ pīyamānasya kṛṣṇe vardhanti tāḥ kalāḥ  MatsP 
kṣīyante ca tāḥ śuklāḥ kṛṣṇā hyāpyāyayanti ca 
evaṃ dinakramātpīte devaiścāpi niśākare  MatsP 
pītvārdhamāsaṃ gacchanti amāvāsyāṃ surāśca te 
pitaraścopatiṣṭhanti amāvāsyāṃ niśākaram  MatsP 
tataḥ pañcadaśe bhāge kiṃciccheṣe niśākare 
tato 'parāhṇe pitaro jaghanyadivase punaḥ  MatsP 
pibanti dvikalaṃ kālaṃ śiṣṭāstāstu kalāstu yāḥ 
viniḥsṛṣṭaṃ tvamāvāsyāṃ gabhastibhyastadāmṛtam  MatsP 
ardhamāsasamāptau tu pītvā gacchanti te 'mṛtam 
saumyā barhiṣadaścaiva agniṣvāttāśca ye smṛtāḥ  MatsP 
kāvyāścaiva tu ye proktāḥ pitaraḥ sarva eva te 
saṃvatsarāśca ye kāvyāḥ pañcābdā vai dvijāḥ smṛtāḥ  MatsP 
saumyāḥ sutapaso jñeyāḥ saumyā barhiṣadastathā 
agniṣvāttās trayaścaiva pitṛsargasthitā dvijāḥ  MatsP 
pitṛbhiḥ pīyamānāyāṃ pañcadaśyāṃ tu vai kalām 
yāvacca kṣīyate tasmād bhāgaḥ pañcadaśastu saḥ  MatsP 
amāvāsyāṃ tathā tasya antarā pūryate paraḥ 
vṛddhikṣayau vai pakṣādau ṣoḍaśyāṃ śaśinaḥ mṛtau 
evaṃ sūryanimitte te kṣayavṛddhī niśākare  MatsP

sūta uvāca
tārāgrahāṇāṃ vakṣyāmi svarbhānostu rathaṃ punaḥ 
atha tejomayaḥ śubhraḥ somaputrasya vai rathaḥ  MatsP 
yukto hayaiḥ piśaṅgastu daśabhir vātaraṃhasaiḥ 
śvetaḥ piśaṅgaḥ sāraṅgo nīlaḥ śyāmo vilohitaḥ  MatsP 
śvetaśca haritaścaiva pṛṣato vṛṣṇireva ca 
daśabhistu mahābhāgair uttamairvātasambhavaiḥ  MatsP 
tato bhaumarathaścāpi aṣṭāṅgaḥ kāñcanaḥ smṛtaḥ 
aṣṭabhir lohitairaśvaiḥ sadhvajair agnisambhavaiḥ 
sarpate 'sau kumāro vai ṛjuvakrānuvakragaḥ  MatsP 
ataścāṅgiraso vidvān devācāryo bṛhaspatiḥ 
gaurāśvena tu raukmeṇa syandanena visarpati  MatsP 
yuktenāṣṭābhiraśvaiśca dhvajairagnisamudbhavaiḥ 
abdaṃ vasati yo rāśau svadiśaṃ tena gacchati  MatsP 
yuktenāṣṭābhir aśvaiśca sadhvajairagnisaṃnibhaiḥ 
rathena kṣipravegeṇa bhārgavastena gacchati  MatsP 
tataḥ śanaiścaro 'pyaśvaiḥ sabalair vātaraṃhasaiḥ 
kārṣṇāyasaṃ samāruhya syandanaṃ yātyasau śaniḥ  MatsP 
svarbhānostu yathāṣṭāśvāḥ kṛṣṇā vai vātaraṃhasaḥ 
rathaṃ tamomayaṃ tasya vahanti sma sudaṃśitāḥ  MatsP 
ādityanilayo rāhuḥ somaṃ gacchati parvasu 
ādityameti somācca tamaso 'nteṣu parvasu  MatsP 
tataḥ ketumatastvaśvā aṣṭau te vātaraṃhasaḥ 
palāladhūmavarṇābhāḥ kṣāmadehāḥ sudāruṇāḥ  MatsP 
ete vāhā grahāṇāṃ vai mayā proktā rathaiḥ saha 
sarve dhruve nibaddhāste nibaddhā vātaraśmibhiḥ  MatsP 
ete vai bhrāmyamāṇāste yathāyogaṃ vahanti vai 
vāya yābhiradṛśyābhiḥ prabaddhā vātaraśmibhiḥ  MatsP 
paribhramanti tadbaddhāś candrasūryagrahā divi 
yāvattamanuparyeti dhruvaṃ ca jyotiṣāṃ gaṇaḥ  MatsP 
yathā nadyudake nostu udakena sahohyate 
tathā devagṛhāṇi syur uhyante vātaraṃhasā 
tasmādyāni pragṛhyante vyomni devagṛhā iti  MatsP 
yāvatyaścaiva tārāḥ syus tāvanto 'sya marīcayaḥ 
sarvā dhruvanibaddhāstā bhramantyo bhrāmayanti ca  MatsP 
tailapīḍaṃ yathā cakraṃ bhramate bhrāmayanti vai 
tathā bhramanti jyotīṃṣi vātabaddhāni sarvaśaḥ  MatsP 
alātacakravadyānti vātacakreritāni tu 
yasmātpravahate tāni pravahastena sa smṛtaḥ  MatsP 
evaṃ dhruve niyukto 'sau bhramate jyotiṣāṃ gaṇaḥ 
eṣa tārāmayaḥ proktaḥ śiśumāre dhruvo divi  MatsP 
yadahnā kurute pāpaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā niśi muñcati 
śiśumāraśarīrasthā yāvatyastārakāstu tāḥ  MatsP 
varṣāṇi dṛṣṭvā jīveta tāvadevādhikāni tu 
śiśumārākṛtiṃ jñātvā pravibhāgena sarvaśaḥ  MatsP 
uttānapādastasyātha vijñeyaḥ sottaro hanuḥ 
yajño 'dharastu vijñeyo dharmo mūrdhānamāśritaḥ  MatsP 
hṛdi nārāyaṇaḥ sādhyā aśvinau pūrvapādayoḥ 
varuṇaścāryamā caiva paścime tasya sakthinī  MatsP 
śiśne saṃvatsaro jñeyo mitraścāpānamāśritaḥ 
pucche 'gniśca mahendraśca marīciḥ kaśyapo dhruvaḥ  MatsP 
eṣa tārāmayaḥ stambho nāstameti na vodayam 
nakṣatracandrasūryāśca grahāstārāgaṇaiḥ saha  MatsP 
tanmukhābhimukhāḥ sarve cakrabhūtā divi sthitāḥ 
dhruveṇādhiṣṭhitāścaiva dhruvameva pradakṣiṇam  MatsP 
pariyānti suraśreṣṭhaṃ meḍhībhūtaṃ dhruvaṃ divi 
āgnīdhrakāśyapānāṃ tu teṣāṃ sa paramo dhruvaḥ  MatsP 
eka eva bhramatyeṣa merorantaramūrdhani 
jyotiṣāṃ cakramādāya ākarṣaṃstamadhomukhaḥ 
merumālokayanneva pratiyāti pradakṣiṇam  MatsP 
MatsyaPurāṇa 
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
yadetadbhavatā proktaṃ śrutaṃ sarvamaśeṣataḥ 
kathaṃ devagṛhāṇi syuḥ punarjyotīṃṣi varṇaya  MatsP 
sūta uvāca
etatsarvaṃ pravakṣyāmi sūryācandramasorgatim 
yathā devagṛhāṇi syuḥ sūryācandramasostathā  MatsP 
agnervyuṣṭau rajanyāṃ vai brahmaṇāvyaktayoninā 
avyākṛtamidaṃ tvāsīn naiśena tamasā vṛtam  MatsP 
caturbhūtāvaśiṣṭe 'smin brahmaṇā samadhiṣṭhite 
svayambhūr bhagavāṃstatra lokatattvārthasādhakaḥ  MatsP 
khadyotarūpī vicarann āvirbhāvaṃ vyacintayat 
jñātvāgniṃ kalpakālādāv apaḥ pṛthvīṃ ca saṃśritā  MatsP 
sa saṃbhṛtya prakāśārthaṃ tridhā tulyo 'bhavatpunaḥ 
pācako yastu loke 'smin pārthivaḥ so 'gnirucyate  MatsP 
yaścāsau tapate sūrye śuciragniśca sa smṛtaḥ 
vaidyuto jāṭharaḥ saumyo vaidyutaścāpyabindhanaḥ  MatsP 
tejobhiścāpyate kaścit kaścidevāpyanindhanaḥ 
kāṣṭhendhanastu nirmathyaḥ so 'dbhiḥ śāmyati pāvakaḥ  MatsP 
arciṣmānpacano 'gnistu niṣprabhaḥ saumyalakṣaṇaḥ 
yaścāsau maṇḍale śukle nirūṣmā na prakāśate  MatsP 
prabhā saurī tu pādena astaṃ yāti divākare 
agnimāviśate rātrau tasmādagniḥ prakāśate  MatsP 
udite tu punaḥ sūrye ūṣmāgnestu samāviśat 
pādena tejasaścāgnes tasmāt saṃtapate divā  MatsP 
prākāśyaṃ ca tathauṣṇyaṃ ca sauryāgneye tu tejasī 
parasparānupraveśād āpyāyete divāniśam  MatsP 
uttare caiva bhūmyardhe tathā hyasmiṃstu dakṣiṇe 
uttiṣṭhati punaḥ sūrye rātrirāviśate hy apaḥ  MatsP 
tasmāttāmrā bhavantyāpo divārātripraveśanāt 
astaṃ gate punaḥ sūrye aharvai praviśaty apaḥ  MatsP 
tasmānnaktaṃ punaḥ śuklā hy āpo dṛśyanti bhāsurāḥ 
etena kramayogeṇa bhūmyardhe dakṣiṇottare  MatsP 
udayāstamaye hyatra ahorātraṃ viśaty apaḥ 
yaścāsau tapate sūryaḥ so 'paḥ pibati raśmibhiḥ  MatsP 
sahasrapādastveṣo 'gnī raktakumbhanibhastu saḥ 
ādatte sa tu nāḍīnāṃ sahasreṇa samantataḥ  MatsP 
apo nadīsamudrebhyo hradakūpebhya eva ca 
tasya raśmisahasreṇa śītavarṣoṣṇaniḥsravaḥ  MatsP 
tāsāṃ catuḥśataṃ nāḍyo varṣante citramūrtayaḥ 
candanāścaiva medhyāśca ketanāś cetanāstathā  MatsP 
amṛtā jīvanāḥ sarvā raśmayo vṛṣṭisarjanāḥ 
himodbhavāśca te 'nyonyaṃ raśmayastriṃśataḥ smṛtāḥ 
candratārāgrahaiḥ sarvaiḥ pītā bhānorgabhastayaḥ  MatsP 
etā madhyāstathānyāśca hlādinyo himasarjanāḥ 
śuklāśca kakubhaścaiva gāvo viśvasṛtaśca yāḥ  MatsP 
śuklāstā nāmataḥ sarvās triṃśato gharmasarjanāḥ 
saṃbibhrati hi tāḥ sarvā manuṣyāndevatāḥ pitṝn  MatsP 
manuṣyānoṣadhībhiśca svadhayā ca pitṝnapi 
amṛtena surānsarvān saṃtataṃ paritarpayan  MatsP 
vasante caiva grīṣme ca śanaiḥ saṃtapate tribhiḥ 
varṣāsu ca śaradyevaṃ caturbhiḥ saṃpravarṣati  MatsP 
hemante śiśire caiva himotsargas tribhiḥ punaḥ 
oṣadhīṣu balaṃ dhatte sudhāṃ ca svadhayā punaḥ  MatsP 
sūryo 'maratvamamṛte trayas triṣu niyacchati 
evaṃ raśmisahasraṃ tu sauraṃ lokārthasādhakam  MatsP 
bhidyate ṛtumāsādya sahasraṃ bahudhā punaḥ

sūta uvāca
śṛṇudhvaṃ tripuraṃ devo yathā dāritavān bhavaḥ 
mayo nāma mahāmāyo māyānāṃ janako 'suraḥ  MatsP

arthe dharme ca kāme ca nidadhuste matīḥ svayam  MatsP

vrajati sma sukhaṃ kālaḥ svargasthānāṃ yathā tathā  MatsP 
śuśrūṣante pitṝnputrāḥ patnyaścāpi patīṃstathā 
vimuktakalahāścāpi prītayaḥ pracurābhavan  MatsP 
nādharmastripurasthānāṃ bādhate vīryavānapi 
arcayanto diteḥ putrās tripurāyatane haram  MatsP 
puṇyāhaśabdānuccerur āśīrvādāṃśca vedagān 
svanūpuraravonmiśrān veṇuvīṇāravānapi  MatsP 
hāsaśca varanārīṇāṃ cittavyākulakārakaḥ 
tripure dānavendrāṇāṃ ramatāṃ śrūyate sadā  MatsP 
teṣāmarcayatāṃ devān brāhmaṇāṃśca namasyatām 
dharmārthakāmamantrāṇāṃ mahānkālo 'bhyavartata  MatsP 
athālakṣmīrasūyā ca tṛḍbubhukṣe tathaiva ca 
kaliśca kalahaścaiva tripuraṃ viviśuḥ saha  MatsP 
saṃdhyākālaṃ praviṣṭāste tripuraṃ ca bhayāvahāḥ 
samadhyāsuḥ samaṃ ghorāḥ śarīrāṇi yathāmayāḥ  MatsP 
sarva ete viśantastu mayena tripurāntaram 
svapne bhayāvahā dṛṣṭā āviśantastu dānavān  MatsP 
udite ca sahasrāṃśau śubhabhāsākare ravau 
mayaḥ sabhāmāviveśa bhāskarābhyāmivāmbudaḥ  MatsP 
merukūṭanibhe ramya āsane svarṇamaṇḍite 
āsīnāḥ kāñcanagireḥ śṛṅge toyamuco yathā  MatsP 
pārśvayostārakākhyaśca vidyunmālī ca dānavaḥ 
upaviṣṭau mayasyānte hastinaḥ kalabhāviva  MatsP 
tataḥ surārayaḥ sarve 'śeṣakopā raṇājire 
upaviṣṭā dṛḍhaṃ viddhā dānavā devaśatravaḥ  MatsP 
teṣvāsīneṣu sarveṣu sukhāsanagateṣu ca 
mayo māyāvijanaka ityuvāca sa dānavān  MatsP 
khecarāḥ khecarārāvā bho bho dākṣāyaṇīsutāḥ 
niśāmayadhvaṃ svapno 'yaṃ mayā dṛṣṭo bhayāvahaḥ  MatsP 
catasraḥ pramadāstatra trayo martyā bhayāvahāḥ 
kopānalādīptamukhāḥ praviṣṭās tripurārdinaḥ  MatsP 
praviśya ruṣitāste ca purāṇyatulavikramāḥ 
praviṣṭāḥ sma śarīrāṇi bhūtvā bahuśarīriṇaḥ  MatsP 
nagaraṃ tripuraṃ cedaṃ tamasā samavasthitam 
sagṛhaṃ saha yuṣmābhiḥ sāgarāmbhasi majjitam  MatsP 
ulūkaṃ rucirā nārī nagnārūḍhā kharaṃ tathā 
saha strībhirhasantī ca cumbane pramadā yathā 
puruṣaḥ sindutilakaś caturaṅghris trilocanaḥ  MatsP 
yena sā pramadā nunnā ahaṃ caiva vibodhitaḥ 
īdṛśī pramadā dṛṣṭā mayā cātibhayāvahā  MatsP 
eṣa īdṛśakaḥ svapno dṛṣṭo vai ditinandanāḥ 
dṛṣṭaḥ kathaṃ hi kaṣṭāya asurāṇāṃ bhaviṣyati  MatsP 
yadi vo 'haṃ kṣamo rājā yadidaṃ vettha ceddhitam 
nibodhadhvaṃ sumanaso na cāsūyitum arhatha  MatsP 
kāmaṃ cerṣyāṃ ca kopaṃ ca asūyāṃ saṃvihāya ca 
satye dame ca dharme ca munivāde ca tiṣṭhata  MatsP 
śāntayaśca prayujyantāṃ pūjyatāṃ ca maheśvaraḥ 
yadi nāmāsya svapnasya hy evaṃ coparamo bhavet  MatsP 
kupyate no dhruvaṃ rudro devadevastrilocanaḥ 
bhaviṣyāṇi ca dṛśyante yato nastripure 'surāḥ  MatsP 
kalahaṃ varjayantaśca arjayantas tathārjavam 
svapnodayaṃ pratīkṣadhvaṃ kālodayamathāpi ca  MatsP 
śrutvā dākṣāyaṇīputrā ityevaṃ mayabhāṣitam 
krodherṣyāvasthayā yuktā dṛśyante ca vināśagāḥ  MatsP 
vināśam upapaśyanto hy alakṣmyā vyāpitāsurāḥ 
tatraiva dṛṣṭvā te 'nyonyaṃ sakrodhāpūritekṣaṇāḥ  MatsP 
atha daivaparidhvastā dānavāstripurālayāḥ 
hitvā satyaṃ ca dharmaṃ ca akāryāṇyupacakramuḥ  MatsP 
dviṣanti brāhmaṇānpuṇyān na cārcanti hi devatāḥ 
guruṃ caiva na manyante hy anyonyaṃ cāpi cukrudhuḥ  MatsP 
kalaheṣu ca sajjante svadharmeṣu hasanti ca 
parasparaṃ ca nindanti ahamityeva vādinaḥ  MatsP 
uccairgurūnprabhāṣante nābhibhāṣanti pūjitāḥ 
akasmātsāśrunayanā jāyante ca samutsukāḥ  MatsP 
dadhisaktūnpayaścaiva kapitthāni ca rātriṣu 
bhakṣayanti ca śeranta ucchiṣṭāḥ saṃvṛtāstathā  MatsP 
mūtraṃ kṛtvopaspṛśanti cākṛtvā pādadhāvanam 
saṃviśanti ca śayyāsu śaucācāravivarjitāḥ  MatsP 
saṃkucanti bhayāccaiva mārjārāṇāṃ yathākhukaḥ 
bhāryāṃ gatvā na śudhyanti rahovṛttiṣu nistrapāḥ  MatsP 
purā suśīlā bhūtvā ca duḥśīlatvamupāgatāḥ 
devāṃstapodhanāṃścaiva bādhante tripurālayāḥ  MatsP 
mayena vāryamāṇā api te vināśamupasthitāḥ 
vipriyāṇyeva viprāṇāṃ kurvāṇāḥ kalahaiṣiṇaḥ  MatsP 
vaibhrājaṃ nandanaṃ caiva tathā caitrarathaṃ vanam 
aśokaṃ ca varāśokaṃ sarvartukamathāpi ca  MatsP 
svargaṃ ca devatāvāsaṃ pūrvadevavaśānugāḥ 
vidhvaṃsayanti saṃkruddhās tapodhanavanāni ca  MatsP 
vidhvastadevāyatanāśramaṃ ca saṃbhagnadevadvijapūjakaṃ tu 
jagadbabhūvāmararājaduṣṭair abhidrutaṃ sasyamivālivṛndaiḥ  MatsP
