svāsu dikṣu svarakṣanta tasya devabalasya te  MatsP 
sūryaḥ saptāśvayuktena rathenāmitagāminā 
śriyā jājvalyamānena dīpyamānaiśca raśmibhiḥ  MatsP 
udayāstagacakreṇa meruparvatagāminā 
tridivadvāracakreṇa tapatā lokamavyayam  MatsP 
sahasraraśmiyuktena bhrājamānena tejasā

somaḥ śvetahaye bhāti syandane śītaraśmivān 
himavattoyapūrṇābhir bhābhirāhlādayañjagat  MatsP 
tamṛkṣapūgānugataṃ śiśirāṃśuṃ dvijeśvaram 
śaśacchāyāṅkitatanuṃ naiśasya tamasaḥ kṣayam  MatsP 
jyotiṣāmīśvaraṃ vyomni rasānāṃ rasadaṃ prabhum 
oṣadhīnāṃ sahasrāṇāṃ nidhānamamṛtasya ca  MatsP 
jagataḥ prathamaṃ bhāgaṃ saumyaṃ satyamayaṃ ratham 
dadṛśurdānavāḥ somaṃ himapraharaṇaṃ sthitam  MatsP 
yaḥ prāṇaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ pañcadhā bhidyate nṛṣu 
saptadhātugato lokāṃs trīndadhāra cacāra ca  MatsP 
yamāhuragnikartāraṃ sarvaprabhavamīśvaram 
saptasvaragato yaśca nityaṃ gīrbhirudīryate  MatsP 
yaṃ vadantyuttamaṃ bhūtaṃ yaṃ vadantyaśarīriṇam 
yamāhurākāśagamaṃ śīghragaṃ śabdayoginam  MatsP 
sa vāyuḥ sarvabhūtāyur udbhūtaḥ svena tejasā 
vavau pravyathayandaityān pratilomaṃ satoyadaḥ  MatsP 
maruto divyagandharvair vidyādharagaṇaiḥ saha 
cikrīḍurasibhiḥ śubhrair nirmuktairiva pannagaiḥ  MatsP 
sṛjantaḥ sarpapatayas tīvratoyamayaṃ viṣam 
śarabhūtā divīndrāṇāṃ cerurvyāttānanā divi  MatsP 
parvataiśca śilāśṛṅgaiḥ śataśaścaiva pādapaiḥ 
upatasthuḥ suragaṇāḥ prahartuṃ dānavaṃ balam  MatsP 
yaḥ sa devo hṛṣīkeśaḥ padmanābhastrivikramaḥ 
yugāntakṛṣṇavartmābho viśvasya jagataḥ prabhuḥ  MatsP 
sarvayoniḥ sa madhuhā havyabhukkratusaṃsthitaḥ 
bhūmyāpovyomabhūtātmā śyāmaḥ śāntikaro 'rihā  MatsP 
arighnamamarādīnāṃ cakraṃ gṛhya gadādharaḥ 
arkaṃ nāgādivodyantam udyamyottamatejasā  MatsP 
savyenālambya mahatīṃ sarvāsuravināśinīm 
kareṇa kālīṃ vapuṣā śatrukālapradāṃ gadām  MatsP 
anyairbhujaiḥ pradīptāni bhujagāridhvajaḥ prabhuḥ 
dadhārāyudhajātāni śārṅgādīni mahābalaḥ  MatsP 
sa kaśyapasyātmabhuvaṃ dvijaṃ bhujagabhojanam 
pavanādhikasaṃpātaṃ gaganakṣobhaṇaṃ khagam  MatsP 
bhujagendreṇa vadane niviṣṭena virājitam 
amṛtārambhanirmuktaṃ mandarādrim ivocchritam  MatsP 
devāsuravimardeṣu bahuśo dṛṣṭavikramam 
mahendreṇāmṛtasyārthe vajreṇa kṛtalakṣaṇam  MatsP

sphītakroḍāvalambena śītāṃśusamatejasā 
bhogibhogāvasaktena maṇiratnena bhāsvatā  MatsP 
pakṣābhyāṃ cārupatrābhyām āvṛtya divi līlayā 
yugānte sendracāpābhyāṃ toyadābhyāmivāmbaram  MatsP 
nīlalohitapītābhiḥ patākābhiralaṃkṛtam 
ketuveṣapraticchannaṃ mahākāyaniketanam  MatsP 
aruṇāvarajaṃ śrīmān āruhya samare vibhuḥ 
suvarṇavarṇavapuṣā suparṇaṃ khecarottamam  MatsP 
tamanvayurdevagaṇā munayaśca samāhitāḥ 
gīrbhiḥ paramamantrābhis tuṣṭuvuśca janārdanam  MatsP 
tadvaiśravaṇasaṃśliṣṭaṃ vaivasvatapuraḥsaram 
dvijarājaparikṣiptaṃ devarājavirājitam  MatsP 
candraprabhābhirvipulaṃ yuddhāya samavartata 
pavanāviddhanirghoṣaṃ saṃpradīptahutāśanam  MatsP 
viṣṇorjiṣṇośca bhrājiṣṇos tejasā tamasāvṛtam 
balaṃ balavadudvṛttaṃ yuddhāya samavartata  MatsP 
svastyastu devebhya iti bṛhaspatirabhāṣata 
svastyastu dānavānīka uśanā vākyamādade  MatsP 
MatsyaPurāṇa 
matsya uvāca
tābhyāṃ balābhyāṃ saṃjajñe tumulo vigrahastadā 
surāṇāmasurāṇāṃ ca parasparajayaiṣiṇām  MatsP 
dānavā daivataiḥ sārdhaṃ nānāpraharaṇodyatāḥ 
samīyuryudhyamānā vai parvatā iva parvataiḥ  MatsP 
tatsurāsurasaṃyuktaṃ yuddhamatyadbhutaṃ babhau 
dharmādharmasamāyuktaṃ darpeṇa vinayena ca  MatsP 
tato rathairviprayuktair vāraṇaiśca pracoditaiḥ 
utpatadbhiśca gaganam asihastaiḥ samantataḥ  MatsP 
kṣipyamāṇaiśca musalaiḥ saṃpatadbhiśca sāyakaiḥ 
cāpairvisphāryamāṇaiśca pātyamānaiśca mudgaraiḥ  MatsP 
tadyuddhamabhavadghoraṃ devadānavasaṃkulam 
jagatastrāsajananaṃ yugasaṃvartakopamam  MatsP 
hastamuktaiśca parighair viprayuktaiśca parvataiḥ 
dānavāḥ samare jaghnur devānindrapurogamān  MatsP 
te vadhyamānā balibhir dānavairjitakāśibhiḥ 
viṣaṇṇavadanā devā jagmurārtiṃ parāṃ mṛdhe  MatsP 
te 'straśūlapramathitāḥ parighairbhinnamastakāḥ 
bhinnoraskā ditisutair vemū raktaṃ vraṇairbahu  MatsP 
veṣṭitāḥ śarajālaiśca niryatnāścāsuraiḥ kṛtāḥ 
praviṣṭā dānavīṃ māyāṃ na śekuste viceṣṭitum  MatsP 
astaṃ gatamivābhāti niṣprāṇasadṛśākṛti 
balaṃ surāṇāmasurair niṣprayatnāyudhaṃ kṛtam  MatsP 
daityacāpacyutān ghorāṃś chittvā vajreṇa tāñcharān 
śakro daityabalaṃ ghoraṃ viveśa bahulocanaḥ  MatsP 
sa daityapramukhānhatvā taddānavabalaṃ mahat 
tāmasenāstrajālena tamobhūtamathākarot  MatsP 
te 'nyonyaṃ nāvabudhyanta devānāṃ vāhanāni ca 
ghoreṇa tamasāviṣṭāḥ puruhūtasya tejasā  MatsP 
māyāpāśairvimuktāstu yatnavantaḥ surottamāḥ 
vapūṃṣi daityasiṃhānāṃ tamobhūtānyapātayan  MatsP 
apadhvastā visaṃjñāśca tamasā nīlavarcasā 
petuste dānavagaṇāś chinnapakṣā ivādrayaḥ  MatsP 
tadghanībhūtadaityendram andhakāra ivārṇave 
dānavaṃ devakadanaṃ tamobhūtamivābhavat  MatsP 
tadāsṛjanmahāmāyāṃ mayastāṃ tāmasīṃ dahan 
yugāntodyotajananīṃ sṛṣṭāmaurveṇa vahninā  MatsP 
sā dadāha tataḥ sarvān māyā mayavikalpitā 
daityāścādityavapuṣaḥ sadya uttasthurāhave  MatsP 
māyāmaurvīṃ samāsādya dahyamānā divaukasaḥ 
bhejire candraviṣayaṃ śītāṃśusalilapradam  MatsP 
te dahyamānā hyaurveṇa vahninā naṣṭacetasaḥ 
śaśaṃsurvajriṇaṃ devāḥ saṃtaptāḥ śaraṇaiṣiṇaḥ  MatsP 
saṃtate māyayā sainye hanyamāne ca dānavaiḥ 
codito devarājena varuṇo vākyamabravīt  MatsP 
purā brahmarṣijaḥ śakra tapastepe sudāruṇam 
ūrvaḥ sapūrvatejasvī sadṛśo brahmaṇo guṇaiḥ  MatsP 
taṃ tapantamivādityaṃ tapasā jagadavyayam 
upatasthurmunigaṇā divyā devarṣibhiḥ saha  MatsP 
hiraṇyakaśipuścaiva dānavo dānaveśvaraḥ 
ṛṣiṃ vijñāpayāmāsuḥ purā paramatejasam  MatsP 
ūcurbrahmarṣayastaṃ tu vacanaṃ dharmasaṃhitam 
ṛṣivaṃśeṣu bhagavaṃś chinnamūlamidaṃ padam  MatsP 
ekastvamanapatyaśca gotrajo 'nyo na vartate 
kaumāraṃ vratamāsthāya kleśamevānuvartase  MatsP 
bahūni vipra gotrāṇi munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanām 
ekadehāni tiṣṭhanti viviktāni vinā prajāḥ  MatsP 
evamucchinnamūlaiśca putrairno nāsti kāraṇam 
bhavāṃstu tapasā śreṣṭho prajāpātasamadyutiḥ  MatsP 
tatra vartasva vaṃśāya vardhayātmānam ātmanā 
tvayā dharmo 'rjitastena dvitīyāṃ kuru vai tanum  MatsP 
sa evamukto munibhir munir marmasu tāḍitaḥ 
jagarhe tānṛṣigaṇān vacanaṃ cedamabravīt  MatsP 
yathāyaṃ vihito dharo munīnāṃ śāśvataḥ purā 
ārṣaṃ vai sevataḥ karma vanyamūlaphalāśinaḥ  MatsP 
brahmayonau prasūtasya brāhmaṇasyātmadarśinaḥ 
brahmacaryaṃ sucaritaṃ brahmāṇamapi cālayet  MatsP 
janānāṃ vṛttayastisro ye gṛhāśramavāsinaḥ 
asmākaṃ tu varaṃ vṛttir vanāśramanivāsinām  MatsP 
abbhakṣā vāyubhakṣāśca dantolūkhalinastathā 
aśmakuṭṭā hyaśanakāḥ pañcātapasahāśca ye  MatsP 
ete tapasi tiṣṭhanti vratairapi suduṣkaraiḥ 
brahmacaryaṃ puraskṛtya prārthayanti parāṃ gatim  MatsP 
brahyacaryādbrāhmaṇasya brāhmaṇatvaṃ vidhīyate 
evamāhuḥ pare loke brahmacaryavido janāḥ  MatsP 
brahmacarye sthitaṃ satyaṃ brahmacarye sthitaṃ tapaḥ 
ye sthitā brahmacarye tu brāhmaṇā divi saṃsthitāḥ  MatsP 
nāsti yogaṃ vinā siddhir na vā siddhiṃ vinā yaśaḥ 
nāsti loke yaśomūlaṃ brahmacaryātparaṃ tapaḥ  MatsP 
yo nigṛhyendriyagrāmaṃ bhūtagrāmaṃ ca pañcakam 
brahmacaryaṃ samādhatte kimataḥ paramaṃ tapaḥ  MatsP 
ayoge keśadharaṇam asaṃkalpavratakriyāṃ 
abrahmacarye caryā ca trayaṃ syād dambhasaṃjñakam  MatsP 
kva dārāḥ kva ca saṃyogaḥ kva ca bhāvaviparyayaḥ 
nanviyaṃ brahmaṇā sṛṣṭā manasā mānasī prajā  MatsP 
yadyasti tapaso vīryaṃ yuṣmākaṃ viditātmanām 
sṛjadhvaṃ mānasānputrān prājāpatyena karmaṇā  MatsP 
manasā nirmitā yonir ādhātavyā tapasvibhiḥ 
na dārayogo bījaṃ vā vratamuktaṃ tapasvinām  MatsP 
yadidaṃ luptadharmārthaṃ yuṣmābhiriha nirbhayaiḥ 
vyāhṛtaṃ sadbhiratyartham asadbhiriva me matam  MatsP 
vapurdīptāntarātmānam etatkṛtvā manomayam 
dārayogaṃ vinā srakṣye putram ātmatanūruham  MatsP 
evamātmānamātmā me dvitīyaṃ janayiṣyati 
vanyenānena vidhinā didhakṣantamiva prajāḥ  MatsP 
ūrvastu tapasāviṣṭo niveśyoruṃ hutāśane 
mamanthaikena darbheṇa sutasya prabhavāraṇim  MatsP 
tasyoruṃ sahasā bhittvā jvālāmālī hyanindhanaḥ 
jagato dahanākāṅkṣī putro 'gniḥ samapadyata  MatsP 
ūrvasyoruṃ vinirbhidya aurvo nāmāntako 'nalaḥ 
didhakṣanniva lokāṃstrīñ jajñe paramakopanaḥ  MatsP 
utpannamātraścovāca pitaraṃ kṣīṇayā girā 
kṣudhā me bādhate tāta jagadbhakṣye tyajasva mām  MatsP 
tridivārohibhirjvālair jṛmbhamāṇo diśo daśa 
nirdahansarvabhūtāni vavṛdhe so 'ntako 'nalaḥ  MatsP 
etasminnantare brahmā munimūrvaṃ sabhājayan 
uvāca vāryatāṃ putro jagataśca dayāṃ kuru  MatsP 
asyāpatyasya te vipra kariṣye sthānamuttamam 
tathyametadvacaḥ putra śṛṇu tvaṃ vadatāṃ vara  MatsP 
ūrva uvāca
dhanyo 'smyanugṛhīto 'smi yanme 'dya bhagavāñchiśoḥ 
matimetāṃ dadātīha paramānugrahāya vai  MatsP 
prabhātakāle samprāpte kāṅkṣitavye samāgame 
bhagavaṃstarpitaḥ putraḥ kairhavyaiḥ prāpsyate sukham  MatsP 
kutra cāsya nivāsaḥ syād bhojanaṃ vā kimātmakam 
vidhāsyatīha bhagavān vīryatulyaṃ mahaujasaḥ  MatsP 
brahmovāca
vaḍavāmukhe 'sya vasatiḥ samudre vai bhaviṣyati 
mama yonirjalaṃ vipra tasya pītavataḥ sukham  MatsP 
yatrāhamāsa niyataṃ pibanvārimayaṃ haviḥ 
taddhavistava putrasya visṛjāmyālayaṃ ca tat  MatsP 
tato yugānte bhūtānām eṣa cāhaṃ ca putraka 
sahitau vicariṣyāvo niṣputrāṇāmṛṇāpahaḥ  MatsP 
eṣo 'gnir antakāle tu salilāśī mayā kṛtaḥ 
dahanaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ sadevāsurarakṣasām  MatsP 
evamastviti taṃ so 'gniḥ saṃvṛtajvālamaṇḍalaḥ 
praviveśārṇavamukhaṃ prakṣipya pitari prabhām  MatsP 
pratiyātastato brahmā ye ca sarve maharṣayaḥ 
aurvasyāgneḥ prabhāṃ jñātvā svāṃ svāṃ gatimupāśritāḥ  MatsP 
hiraṇyakaśipurdṛṣṭvā tadā tanmahadadbhutam 
uccaiḥ praṇatasarvāṅgo vākyametaduvāca ha  MatsP 
bhagavannadbhutamidaṃ saṃvṛttaṃ lokasākṣikam 
tapasā te muniśreṣṭha parituṣṭaḥ pitāmahaḥ  MatsP 
ahaṃ tu tava putrasya tava caiva mahāvrata 
bhṛtya ityavagantavyaḥ sādhyo yadiha karmaṇā  MatsP 
tanmāṃ paśya samāpannaṃ tavaivārādhane ratam 
yadi sīdenmuniśreṣṭha tavaiva syātparājayaḥ  MatsP 
aurva uvāca
dhanyo 'smyanugṛhīto 'smi yasya te 'haṃ guruḥ sthitaḥ 
nāsti me tapasānena bhayamadyeha suvrata  MatsP 
tāmeva māyāṃ gṛhṇīṣva mama putreṇa nirmitām 
nirindhanāmagnimayīṃ durdharṣāṃ pāvakairapi  MatsP 
eṣā te svasya vaṃśasya vaśagārivinigrahe 
saṃrakṣatyātmapakṣaṃ ca vipakṣaṃ ca pradhakṣyati  MatsP 
evamastviti tāṃ gṛhya praṇamya munipuṃgavam 
jagāma tridivaṃ hṛṣṭaḥ kṛtārtho dānaveśvaraḥ  MatsP 
eṣā durviṣahā māyā devairapi durāsadā 
aurveṇa nirmitā pūrvaṃ pāvakenorvasūnunā  MatsP 
tasmiṃstu vyutthite daitye nirvīryaiṣā na saṃśayaḥ 
śāpo hyasyāḥ purā dattaḥ sṛṣṭā yenaiva tejasā  MatsP 
yadyeṣā pratihantavyā kartavyo bhagavānsukhī 
dīyatāṃ me sakhā śakra toyayonirniśākaraḥ  MatsP 
tenāhaṃ saha saṃgamya yādobhiśca samāvṛtaḥ 
māyāmetāṃ haniṣyāmi tvatprasādānna saṃśayaḥ  MatsP 
MatsyaPurāṇa 
matsya uvāca
evamastviti saṃhṛṣṭaḥ śakrastridaśavardhanaḥ 
saṃdideśāgrataḥ somaṃ yuddhāya śiśirāyudham  MatsP 
gaccha soma sahāyatvaṃ kuru pāśadharasya vai 
asurāṇāṃ vināśāya jayārthaṃ ca divaukasām  MatsP 
tvaṃ mattaḥ prativīryaśca jyotiṣāṃ ceśvareśvaraḥ 
tvanmayaṃ sarvalokeṣu rasaṃ rasavido viduḥ  MatsP 
kṣayavṛddhī tava vyakte sāgarasyeva maṇḍale 
parivartasyahorātraṃ kālaṃ jagati yojayan  MatsP 
lokacchāyāmayaṃ lakṣma tavāṅkaḥ śaśasaṃnibhaḥ 
na viduḥ soma devāpi ye ca nakṣatrayonayaḥ  MatsP 
tvamādityapathādūrdhvaṃ jyotiṣāṃ copari sthitaḥ 
tamaḥ protsārya mahasā bhāsayasyakhilaṃ jagat  MatsP 
śvetabhānur himatanur jyotiṣām adhipaḥ śaśī 
adhikṛt kālayogātmā iṣṭo yajñaraso 'vyayaḥ  MatsP 
oṣadhīśaḥ kriyāyonir haraśekharabhāktathā 
śītāṃśuramṛtādhāraś capalaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ  MatsP 
tvaṃ kāntiḥ kāntivapuṣāṃ tvaṃ somaḥ somapāyinām 
saumyastvaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ timiraghnastvam ṛkṣarāṭ  MatsP 
tadgaccha tvaṃ mahāsena varuṇena varūthinā 
śamaya tvāsurīṃ māyāṃ yayā dahyāma saṃyuge  MatsP 
soma uvāca
yanmāṃ vadasi yuddhārthe devarāja varaprada 
eṣa varṣāmi śiśiraṃ daityamāyāpakarṣaṇam  MatsP 
etānmacchītanirdagdhān paśya tvaṃ himaveṣṭitān 
vimāyānvimadāṃścaiva daityasiṃhānmahāhave  MatsP 
ityuktvā tārakādhīśaḥ sajaleśaḥ śivodakaiḥ 
plāvayāmāsa sainyāni surāṇāṃ śāntivṛddhaye  MatsP 
teṣāṃ himakarotsṛṣṭāḥ sapāśā himavṛṣṭayaḥ 
veṣṭayanti sma tānghorān daityānmeghagaṇā iva  MatsP
